vīta-rāga-bhaya-krodhaḥ rāgaḥ ca bhayam ca krodhaḥ ca vītā vigatā yasmāt saḥ vīta-rāga-bhaya-krodhaḥ
saṃkhyāyāḥca prathamā-anta-arthe anvayena kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-antaram svīkriyate
śābdatvam jñānatva-vyāpya-dharmaḥ itiullikhanti
tri-doṣa-je tu hṛd-roge yaḥ dur-ātmā niṣevate
iti mukuṃdaḥ bādha-tapta-hṛdayaḥ san samādhānam dattavān
kāka-pakṣa-dharaḥ mahendra-karatalam avalambya kruddhaḥabhibhāṣate māmabhimanyuḥ
nidrā supta-manuṣya-vīrya-tulane saṃsarpaṇe pannagaḥ
kali-puruṣaḥ aho katham śāpa-anugraha-samarthaḥ iti uccaiḥhasati
dhīrā kanyāiyaṃ dṛṣṭa-dharma-pra-cārā-mg śaktā cāritraṃ rakṣituṃ me bhaginyāḥ
eṣaḥ bhartā asmākam hṛdaya-ānandam kurvan na-kṣata-śarīraḥ itaḥ eva āgacchati
aparā padānām pada-artheṣu vākya-artha-avagama-śakti-ādhāna-śaktiḥ kalpanīyā
prakṛti-dus-tyajā matā
dyuti-dhātuḥ lakṣaṇayā nissaraṇa-pūrvaka-dyotane vartate
māyāvitva-ādi-saṃbhavāt
anayāeva saraṇyā kīdṛśau caitra-tad-anyau iti praśne
snehanā jīvanā balyā varṇa-upacaya-vardhanāḥ
vidāhi ca viśeṣeṇa sarva-doṣa-prakopaṇam
uttarāprīti-datta-alaṅkāreṇa alaṅkṛtaḥ vrīḍitaḥ ivaasmi rājānaṃ draṣṭum
nir-sampāta-puruṣa tvāt prasuptā iva ujjayanī pratibhāti
gavi citra-pada-arthasya abhedenaanvayaḥ iti na saṃbhavati
tasyāḥ mukhe agni-dāha-janitaṃ vraṇa-cihnam āsīt
bhuja-plavena āśu gata-artha-viklavaḥ
tat vacana-sama-kālam eva sevakaḥ vṛddhāya ekam anyaṃ syūtaṃ prādāt
rāmanāthasya svare tanvākrośa jala-grahaṇa-anantaram api āsīt
alpa-jñaḥ na asti bhavān iti vadatā adhyakṣena tena pracāra-kārya-mahattvam viśadīkṛtam paśyatām jāne aham yat asmin nagare sitāra-vādane bhavān prāmukhyam bhajate
pāna-āgāra-niśānta-deśa-vivareṣu ākrāntavān asmi aham
sā hi loka-uttara-saundarya-rāśiḥ
caturthe tu anna-kāle tathāvidhānāmeva śāli-taṇḍulānām utsvinnāṃ vilepīm uṣṇaudakadvitīyām a-sneha-lavaṇām alpa-sneha-lavaṇāṃ vā bhojayet
saḥ atra āgatya kṛṣi-sambandhi-jñānaṃ
iti lajjā-autsukya-sāhasa-ādīnām antaḥ vartamānā katicit kṣaṇāni dolā-sam-ārūḍha-anta taḥ sāhasāya eva jaya-patram arpitavatī
te eva vāta-pitta-śleṣmāṇaḥ sthāna-viśeṣe prakupitāḥ vyādhi-viśeṣān abhinirvartayantiagniveśa
kiṃtu abhyāsena tu abhyāsaḥ nāma citta-bhūmau kasyāṃcit samāna-pratyaya-āvṛttiḥ cittasya
tau etau arkavāyū somaḥ ca kālasvabhāvamārgaparigṛhītāḥ kāla-ṛtu-rasa-doṣa-deha-bala-nirvṛtti-pratyayabhūtāḥ samupadiśyante
pare tu iti-ādinā lakṣaṇā-svarūpa-nirūpaṇa-upakrame śaktyāeva bodhe lakṣaṇā-vyavahāraḥ itiukteḥ
alaṅkṛtāḥ aneke rājānaḥ ca śobhā-yātrā-rūpeṇa rāmasya anu-saraṇam akurvan
rāmadayāluḥ loka-arpaṇa-mahat-utsavasya tithim tasya vyaktigata-sacivāya asūcayat
catvāraḥ rogāḥ bhavanti āgantu-vāta-pitta-śleṣma-nimittāḥ
atra vyāpāra-janya-nāśa-rūpa-phala-āśraya tvāt taṇḍulasya
yāsām śākhā-bheda-pracāra-vaśāt na-antaḥ na-pāraḥ na-uparataḥ saṃsāraḥ nitya-pratataḥ vistīrṇaḥ bhavati
aparatra ca prathama-pravāsinaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ mātṛ-sneha-lobhāt mātṛ-samāṃ tāṃ putrīyitvā nānā capalāyante
tad-ghaṭaka-pada-vṛttyā eva tad-sambhavāt
viśeṣaṇa-pada-uttara-vibhakti tvena sāmānyataḥ sādhutva-arthaka-tā-kalpanāyām māna-abhāvāt ca
tāvat tasya kukkuraḥ tad-sam-kṣam agra-pādayoḥ śiraḥ nidhāya viśrāmaṃ kurute sma
tathāhi saṃbandhaḥ nāma saṃbandhibhyām bhinnaḥ dvi-niṣṭhaḥ viśiṣṭa-buddhi-niyāmakaḥ ca bhavati
dharmaḥ prāk eva cintyaḥ saciva-mati-gatiḥ prekṣitavyā sva-buddhyā
asti apālā-sama samunnata-buddhe sa-rasa-hṛdayasya ca maṇi-kāñcana-saṃyoga sarvathā virala
sāmānya-śākānām upa-jaṃ kṛtvā jīvana-upayoga-kāryaṃ kartuṃ preraṇā dātavyā
aham ātmā guḍākā-īśa sarva-bhūta-āśaya-sthitaḥ
na ca prakāratā-nirūpitā yā viśeṣyatā-bhinna-viṣayatā tadvattvam saṃbandhatvamiti na vastu-mātre ativyāptiḥiti vācyam
atraāhuḥ eka-artha-bhāva-vādinaḥ vaiyākaraṇāḥ
trayodaśī tithiḥ uktā maha-ugrā traya-daśa-dvīpavatī mahī ca
damayantī he nala-mahat-rāja ityāhvayati
tatra daivavyapāśrayaṃ mantra-auṣadhi-maṇi-maṅgala-bali-upahāra-homa-niyama-prāyaścitta-upavāsa-svastyayana-praṇipāta-gamana-ādi
tathā ca caitra-kartṛkaḥ svāpaḥ iti dhātu-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kaḥ bodhaḥ
bhāratīya-svatantratā-ākāmyamānā sandihānā bhāratīya-vīrāṇām mukhāni bhaya-santrasta-locanaiḥ prekṣantī cakitaḥ iva āsīt
bodha-janaka-tā-avacchedaka-viṣayitāka tvasya vivakṣitatvāt
tasyāṃ puryām ayodhyāyāṃ prajā-vallabhaḥ mahāt-tejāḥ dhārmikaḥ jita-na-śeṣa-śatruḥ mitra-bandhu-sambandhibhiḥ yutaḥ maharṣi-kalpaḥ rājan-ṛrṣiḥ nṛpālaḥ daśarathaḥ vasan nayena prajāḥ apālayat
aham auṣadham sarva-prāṇibhiḥ yat adyate tat auṣadha-śabda-śabditam vrīhi-yava-ādi-sādhāraṇam
tvat-upa-ā-śrayāṇām api janānām asmat-ādīnām mana moṣaṇam eva śaraṇam
ataḥ ūrdhvaṃ śarīrasya kāryam akṣi-añjana-ādi kam
piśāca-ādi-ravaḥ
ekadā kaścit abhinavaḥ eva vidvān śāstra-arthī bhūtvā dik-vijaya-yātrāyai niḥsṛtaḥ
ekaḥ sampannaḥ janaḥ svakīya-janma-dina-utsave svakīyam ekaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ prativeśinam api bhojana-artham āhvayati sma
yuddhe kruddha-sura-ibha-danta-kuliśa-vyālīḍha-vakṣaḥsthalam
ātman-nirvāha-yogyam kiñcit sthānam vāsavetanena svāyattam kṛtvā sva-patnīm tatra netukāma punaḥ tatraiva saras-taṭe prayāta
mṛgasya nāman-arthasya karmatā-saṃbandhena dhātu-arthe darśane anvaya-asaṃbhavena viśeṣyatayā karmatva-vivakṣāyām mṛga-pada-uttaram dvitīyāyāḥ dur-vāra tvāt
saptan-aha-anantaraṃ benjhiyonasya sā patrikā vipaṇyāṃ dṛṣṭi-gocaratāṃ gatā
atha mṛga-vāyasa-mūṣikāḥ param viṣādam gacchantaḥtamanujagmuḥ
go-ādi-padāt ca go-ādi-pada-artha-smṛti-mātram eva iti svīkartumucitatvāt
iha śāstra-artha-dārḍhyāya saṃkṣepataḥ upasaṃhāram kṛtvā
puṇḍra-ādi-dhāraṇe bhartsanam
vyajanaiḥ pāṇi-saṃsparśaiḥ candana-udaka-śītalaiḥ
ulkām pragṛhya sahasā añjana-rāśi-varṇaḥ
śrīmān nārāyaṇaḥ te pradiśatu vasudhām ucchrita-eka-ātapatrām
na-pūrva-darpaṇasya śaktiḥ parimitā asti iti viṣayam jñātvā mallikā cauryam kṛtvā api ātmānam rakṣitum iṣṭavatī
na-sevake caanuraktiḥdānam sa-priya-bhāṣaṇam
kaṇḍū-koṭha-aruci-vyaṅga-śotha-pāṇḍvāmaya-jvarāḥ
deha-cakṣus-manas-buddhi-ātmānaḥ draṣṭāraḥ
taila-majja-vasā-sarpiḥ-badara-triphalā-rasaiḥ
etat vīkṣa taila-kāra-patnī stabdhā sañjātā
na-mogha-vacanaḥ hi bhavān anugṛhṇātu
sarvathā śābda-bodha-upayogi-bahu-prameya-vyutpādakaḥ prauḍhaḥ laghumañjūṣā-granthaḥ paṇḍita-rūpaiḥ āsvādanīyaḥ iti dhyeyam
tad-anantaraṃ svasya āśramaṃ prati āgatavantaṃ nārada-mahat-ṛṣiṃ saḥ vālmīkiḥ pṛṣṭavān sāmpratam asmin loke kaḥ guṇavān vīryavān ca iti
na-cintya-rūpam na asya rūpam niyatam vidyamānam api kenacit cintayitum śakyate iti na-cintya-rūpaḥ tam
vākyasya vākya-artha-pratipattau tātparyamāvaśyakam
na-gocara-śaktayaḥ
upa-jilā-adhi-īśaḥ bhavitum kalpate
prasṛtaḥ ayam mahat-rodana-dhvani
ātman-sambhāvitāḥ stabdhāḥ dhana-māna-mada-anvitāḥ
aye kadācit patra-vāhaka syāt iti nidrā-ālasa-kaṣāya-svareṇa nigadat asau gṛha-dvāram adhāvat
īhante ceṣṭante kāma-bhoga-artham kāma-bhoga-prayojanāya na dharma-artham
rātrau yadā rākṣasyaḥ sva-sva-gṛham agacchan
lakṣya-artha-smṛtaye lakṣaṇāyāḥ vṛtteḥjñānamapekṣitam
pattanam hi na-maṅgala-rahitam jātam
sup-anta-arthaḥ ca ākhyāta-śabda-ita-tiṅ-anta-artha-viśeṣaṇam
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ tadīyam maunam bhañjayitum icchan avadat aye rājan bhavān kasya saṅkalpasya nimittam evam mahāntam pariśramam kurvan asti rājānaḥ adhikāra-madena ā-vṛtāḥ santaḥ kadācit kim api nirṇayanti
na pāpa-vṛttān strī-mitra-bhṛtyān bhajeta
tataḥca gaṅgā-pade tīra-bodhaka-tva-rūpāyāḥ tīre śakteḥ klṛptatayā tatra śābda-bodha-anukūla-tīra-upasthiti-janaka-tva-kalpanam apiucitameva
paṅke-jasya dhyāna-bhaṅgaḥ abhavat śīghram eva kośāt bahiḥ nava-nūtana-mudrā-patraṃ sthālyāṃ rājate sma
parastāt eva aparām dhūmaśakaṭim āruhya sva-ipsita-sthalam prasthāsye
tathā ca nirukta-saraṇyā anvita-anvaya-pratīti-nimitta tvam uktam bhavati
sītā mahat-rājñī-padaṃ bhūṣitavatī
asmin citra-paṭe citritaṃ bhāratīyaṃ jīvanaṃ nāma bhāratīyānāṃ viḍambanā khalu sādyantam na-satyaṃ pradarśanam khalu bhāratīya-jīvana-paddhatyāḥ
dharme viśeṣatvamca vidheyatā-avacchedaka tvena vaktṛ-jñāna-viṣaya tvam
gaṇikā-janaḥ nāgarika-janaḥ ca anyonya-viśeṣa-maṇḍitau ātmānam darśayitu-kāmau teṣu teṣu prāsādeṣu sa-vibhramam saṃcarataḥ
icchā-viṣaya-bodha-viṣaya tāyāḥ ghaṭa-ādi-rūpe arthe sattveapi tasyāḥ icchā-āśraya-tā-niyāmaka-tva-abhāvāt
tatra akṣayyam ha vai cāturmāsya-yājinaḥ sukṛtam bhavati iti śrutiḥ karman-phala-viśeṣasya cāturmāsasya-phalasya akṣayyatvam brūte
evañca kim pratyaya-mātrasya anvita-abhidhāyi-tva-svīkāreṇa-ardha-jaratī-īya-nyāya-viṣayeṇa
dhātu-arthe pāke iva nāman-arthe puruṣeapi viśeṣyatā-saṃbandhena pratyakṣa-janya-upasthiti-rūpa-kāraṇa-bādhāt
yathā nagna-kṣapaṇaka-ādīnām śarīra-antarvartī deha-parimāṇaḥ jīvaḥ
na-anya-gatikaḥ bhāgyanāthaḥ tayā peṭikayā saha bhū-lokam gatavān
prakṛte kaśipu-padam hiraṇya-śabda-pūrvaka-kaśipu-pada-pratipādye lākṣaṇikam
vāta-mūtra-purīṣāṇāṃ visarge gātra-lāghave
dārśinikānām ghaṭakatva-vyāpakatva-vācakatva-ādīnām saptamī-artha-tā-varṇanam anuśāsana-anurodhi evaiti nirvahanti
śreṣṭhī viṣama-rujā-ārtaḥ san devatāṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau vinatiṃ ca cakāra
tārakā api sneha-peśala-dṛṣṭim vi-kṣepayanta samantata sa-sṛjire mohakam ekam dṛśyam
caitraḥ pacati iti vākya-ja-bodhe pāka-anukūla-kṛteḥ ākhyāta-arthasya vidhetvāt
nala-rājan-kumāraḥ yathā māṃ gāḍhaṃ gṛhītavān tattvam apaśyaḥ
marmopahāsinaḥ lubdhāḥ para-vṛddhi-dviṣaḥ śaṭhāḥ
mama śāstra-cintanam ākarṇya madīya-gambhīra-vaiduṣyeṇa paricita san vismita sañjāta tapa-vana-jana
ātman-saṃyama-yoga-agnau juhvati jñāna-dīpite
pada-niṣṭhasya bodhakatvasya śakti-rūpa-tva-saṃbhave eva
maithilāḥ phaṇadaha-vaṃśa-udbhavāḥ na-eka-grantha-nirmātāraḥ gokulanātha-upādhyāyāḥ svīya-kārikābhiḥ saṃgṛhītamartham viśadīkurvantam pada-vākya-ratna-ākara-abhidham śābda-bodha-grantham racayāmāsuḥ
atha na-prāpta-samyak-darśanāḥ janaka-ādayaḥ
su-madhura-bhāṣiṇī tasya patnī
tasmāt vivāha-sambandha-vārtāṃ vijñāya prasanna-manāḥ ramābāī tenālīrāmasya anujena saha vivāhāya samudyatā abhavat
nārāca-kunta-śara-tomara-khaḍga-kīrṇā
dvedhā api atra puruṣā vilokyante sāṃyugīnā pīta-ambara-dhāriṇaḥ ca
svatantratāyāḥ caturdaśa-abda-anantaram api grāme asmin ādhunikī pra-gati na jātā
śarīra-vāk-manobhiḥ yat karma prārabhate naraḥ
na-śāstra-vihitaṃ ghoraṃ tapyante ye tapaḥ janāḥ
cikitsāprābhṛtaḥtasmātdātā deha-sukha-āyuṣām
imām aham kāliya-dhūma-dhūmrām
ānandasya prati-phala-rūpeṇa tasmai dhanam yacchanti sma te
tatra ekasmin prānte nāthadvārā-udaya-pura-madhye parvatasya racanā atīva duṣkarā
arthe padasya sva-janya-jñāna-viṣaya-tva-prakāraka-īśvara-icchā-viṣaya tvam saṃbandhaḥ
puna saṅkṣepeṇa eva svakīya-rājyasya rīti-paramparām āvedya uktavān asmadīye rājye rājña pūjā-mālā nija-hasta-gumphita eva bhavati svarṇa-kāra svarṇasya mālikām gumphati
bhogyā vāsanā-mūrtī ramaṇī katham na-avadya-premṇā samupāsyā devī bhavati iti jñātum ayam kathā-grantha upaniṣat eva
kopi ayam vismṛta-gṛha-pathaḥ dārakaḥ asti
tat dṛṣṭvā tu tāpasī-dvayaṃ vismayāt uras-nihita-hastaṃ parasparam avalokitavat
ṛjvāyatāṃ hi mukha-toraṇa-lola-mālāṃ bhraṣṭāṃ kṣitau tvamavagacchasi mūrkha sarpam
sa-bhaya-kampam iva prābravīt sādhuḥ
caitraḥ na pacatiityatra bhavadbhiḥ pāka-anukūla-kṛti-abhāva vān ekatva-viśiṣṭaḥ caitraḥ iti-ākāraka-bodhasya svīkārāt
kadācit-śabdaḥ sarva-vikriyā-pratiṣedhaiḥ saṃbadhyate na kadācit jāyate
chāga khalu hantāram eva avalokya lāṅgūla-ādi-cālanena sva-antargatām prītim upadarśayati
vāsudevaḥ sudarśana a-pratihata-parākramaḥ bhava
tathā ati-śīta-uṣṇānāṃ spṛśyānāṃ snāna-abhyaṅga-utsādana-ādīnāṃ ca ati-upasevanam atiyogaḥ
tasyāḥ śvaḥ pra-yoga-kālaḥ iti kutaḥ
kṣetra-kṣetrajña-saṃyogāt tat viddhi bharata-ṛṣabha
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat bhoḥ rājan sukhamayam antaḥpura-vāsam parityajya kaṣṭam sahamānaḥ bhavān śmaśānam eva apekṣate
nandam jaghāna cāṇakyaḥ tīkṣṇa-dūta-prayogataḥ
gāmānayaiti prayojaka-vṛddha-vākya-śravaṇa-anantaram prayojya-vṛddhaḥ go-ānayane pravartate
udyāna-vikāsa-arthaṃ dhanaṃ haṃsasya vikrayeṇa sulabhaṃ bhaviṣyati
yathā jñeyam ghaṭa-ādi-lakṣaṇam jñānena jñātā vyāptum icchati
itthaṃ dhṛta-kṛtrima-śikhi-pakṣaḥ dhvāṃkṣaḥ darpa-ādhmātaḥ kāka-maṇḍalīm upetavān
puro-hita-varyaḥ prati-dinaṃ bhayaṃ-kare śīte sūrya-udayāt pūrvameva śītale ambuni sthitvā tapaḥ caraṇe deva-ārādhane ca vyāpṛtaḥ jāyate sma
dvitīya-tṛtīya-pakṣa-vādinām ayamāśayaḥ
ye svārthinaḥ dhaurtya-kalā-pravīṇāḥ
mahyam na-bhaya-dānaṃ dīyatām
śakti-jñānasya pṛthak kāraṇatva-na-kalpanā-ātmanka-lāghava-rūpa-vinigamaka-sadbhāvena īśvara-icchāyāḥ eva śaktitvāt
upa-kumbham ityatra navīna-mate vibhakti-saṃnihita-kumbha-padasya eva kumbha-samīpe lakṣaṇā-svīkārāt na tatra vyabhicāraḥ
tīra-ādi-saṃbandha-avagāhi-śābda-buddhau tīra-upasthiteḥ na-hetu tvāt
yajñasya nirvartanāya veda-jñāḥ suyajña-vāmadeva-kāśyapa-ādayaḥ nimantritāḥ
tad-anurodhi-mānasa-bodha-kāraṇa-tā-ānantyam na doṣaḥ phala-mukha tvātiti vācyam
sva-truṭi-kṛte ca mattaḥ kṣamām api yāciṣyate
ubhaya-karaṇaka-yāgasya api anyatara-karaṇaka-tva-na-apāyāt
tadā daśa sevakāḥ mahat-rājasya puraḥ paścāt dakṣiṇa-uttara-sd-pārśvayoḥ atiṣṭhan
na-saktiḥ na-abhiṣvaṅgaḥ putra-dāra-gṛhādiṣu
gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti-ādau gaṅgā-padena tīra-bodhāt vidyamāna-sarva-viṣayaiṇī īśvara-icchā tīreapi gaṅgā-pada-janya-bodha-viṣaya tvamavagāhate iti aṅgīkaraṇīyam
yā karman-jā siddhiḥ uktā jñāna-niṣṭhā-yogyatā-lakṣaṇā
nagarī ca dhvaja-patākā-toraṇaiḥ maṅgala-kalaśaiḥ ca bhūṣitā abhavat
kintu svalpam api asya dharmasya yoga-dharmasya anuṣṭhitam trāyate rakṣati mahataḥ bhayāt saṃsāra-bhayāt janman-maraṇa-ādi-lakṣaṇāt
na ca mṛdaḥ eva ghaṭa-ādi-ākāra-prāptim icchanti
puṣkaraḥ he nala-mahat-rāja tvāṃ pratyabhijānāmi eva
tasmāt vākya-arthe prameye śabda-rūpa-pramāṇasya saṃbandhaḥ anubhāvakatva-rūpaḥ āvaśyakaḥ eva
prakṛti-madhya-vartini akac pratyaye avyāpteḥ
atīta-śloka-arthasya eva saṃkṣepaḥ ucyate
putrau api dhārā-pravāha-rūpeṇa hībrū-bhāṣayā eva vadataḥ sma
sāma-gāna-pavitram me na utśiṣṭam adharam kuru
tataḥ samudbhūtaḥ sugandhi-dhūma-parimala modayati iva manāṃsi
tad-eka-deśe bhede prakṛti-arthasya narasya kṣatriyatva-avacchinna-anya-tva-viśiṣṭa-nara-tva-vyāpaka-adhikaraṇatā-nirūpita-ādheyatā-saṃbandhena anvayaḥ
brahma-vidyāyāṃ yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde
ata eva tu mādṛśā dur-bala-gātrā janā atra nivasanti
karman-anuṣṭhāna-karman-saṃnyāsayoḥ bhinna-puruṣa-viṣayatvāt
tat na-kṛtrima-sauhārdam āpatsuapi na muñcati
tataḥ mahī-patiḥ rātrau rāmaiyā-nāmānaṃ taṃ janam ākārya sva-samīpa-sthe kakṣe śāyitavān
saha-parivāraḥ ayam sva-mitra-pārśvam vārāṇasyām ājagāma
sva-arthinaḥ sadā sva-artha-poṣaṇam eva kurvanti
varṣā-śarat-hemanteṣu tu dakṣiṇā-abhimukhe arke kāla-mārga-megha-vāta-varṣā-abhihata-pratāpe
go-ānayana-pravṛttyā madhyama-vṛddhasya saṃsṛṣṭa-artha-jñānam anuminoti taṭa-sthaḥ
evam kṛt-anta-taddhita-anta-samāsānām pada-samudāya tvena arthavattva-abhāvāt pūrva-sūtreṇa prātipadika-saṃjñāyāḥ na-prāptau
śaktyā gaṅgā-padena smṛtaḥ pravāhaḥ sva-sambandhi-tīram smārayati
kuṭajatvak śleṣma-pitta-rakta-sāṃgrāhika-upaśoṣaṇānāṃ
divā sūrya-aṃśu-saṃtaptaṃ niśi candra-aṃśu-śītalam
te sarve eva dhātavaḥ mala-ākhyāḥ prasāda-ākhyāḥ ca rasa-malābhyāṃ puṣyantaḥ svaṃ mānam anuvartante yathā-vayaḥ-śarīram
yasmāt kṣetra-kṣetrajña-īśvara-yāthātmya-vyatirekeṇa na jñāna-gocaram anyat avaśiṣṭam asti
caitraḥ pacati iti-ādau ākhyāta-eka-vacana-ekatva-upasthitiḥ na śābda-bodhe hetuḥ māna-abhāvāt
tat-prakoṣṭha-sthitam sabhyam tam sa uccaiḥ hāsam prāvocat mahāśaya dṛśyatām adya tu nibhramam daśam a-saṃkhyākam eva prakoṣṭhakam upagataḥ asmi
evañca ayam kokilaḥ itianuvyavasāyaḥ itiasya ayam kokilaḥ iti vākya-janya-bodha-samāna-ākāraka-anuvyavasāyaḥ itiarthaḥ
katipaya-taddhita-pratyaya-arthasya ca prātipadika-arthena bheda-anvaya-bodham nirūpya
kauñjāyanaḥ evam gate kāśi-rāja-dūtaḥ pūjayitavyaḥ
sadyaḥ evaupaśāmyanti pāda-abhyaṅga-niṣevaṇāt
śvetaḥaśvaḥ dhāvatiiti vākya-artha-avagamaka-tva-darśanāt
vṛddhayā kanyā-darśana-anantaram anumati pradattā
ḍorabaṃkā prāha samprati kīdṛśaḥ abhūt utsavaḥ te procatuḥ samprati api rājan-kumārikā samāgatā kintu ca ardha-rātri-paryantaṃ tatra sthitvā sā vāyu-vegena dhāvantī tasmāt vinirgatā
tayoḥ ubhayoḥ ca karman-anuṣṭhāna-karman-saṃnyāsayoḥ sthiti-gativat paraspara-virodhāt
phala-tṛṣṇā-śūnyena kriyamāṇe karmaṇi sattva-śuddhi-jā jñāna-prāpti-lakṣaṇā siddhiḥ
bhoga-aiśvarya-gatim prati bhogaḥ ca aiśvaryam ca bhoga-aiśvarye
tataḥ tatra ghoṣa-ādhāra-tva-anvaya-na-upapatti-pratisandhānam
śakyatā-avacchedaka-āropa-viṣaya-niṣṭhaḥ śakya-sambandhaḥ lakṣaṇā
sṛṣṭa mūtra-purīṣaṃ ca sarva-doṣa-nibarhaṇam
vastutaḥtu nadī-padasya eva gabhīra-nadī-tīre lakṣaṇā
viṣṭambhayati kārañjaṃ vāta-śleṣma-a-virodhi ca
itthamca śakti-traya-kalpanayā gauravam bhavati
prāptaḥ agra-yauvana-ghana-stana-marda-kālaḥ
pāṇi-gahaṇa-kālāt pūrvam eva katham na palāyitā na-nirdiṣṭam sthānam
mahat-rājā-adhirājam
lavaṇam anna-dravya-ruci-karāṇām
khāt patat soma-vāyu-arkaiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ kāla-anuvartibhiḥ
iti sat-na-sat-vibhāge buddhi-tantre sthite
patnī sīvana-kartana-ādi karma kṛtvā gṛhasya kāryam cālayati
ahaṃ cintayāmi yat evaṃ likhatu atra śete spīḍī-benyahūda-nāmakaḥ śunakaḥ
yātaḥ kṛta-artha-gaṇanām aham adya loke
ācarāmaḥ vivāha-maṅgala-utsavam iti
tatca dhātu-artha-kṛtau anveti
idānīm iha gaṅgā-snāna-upadeśena āgatau te pitarau vinā kaṣṭam gītā-bhavanam adhivasantau api asmat-hetoḥ nityam kalahena kālam yāpayata
tadā hi dus-cintayā bhṛśam sam-tāḍita śreṣṭhikapardikāmalla prathamam sva-dharma-patnyā sākam vicārayāmāsa
kevalaṃ kāntā-kamanīya-bhāvaḥ eva āyāti sma hṛdi
unmatta-cchanna-veṣasya rathyāsu paridhāvataḥ
atha matam śrauta-karma-apekṣayā etad-vacanam
dus-kara-vidheya-jātaṃ yo līlayā vidhatte
vidyāt vāta-mada-āviṣṭaṃ rūkṣa-śyāva-aruṇa-ākṛtim
tasya nir-gamana-kāle vṛddhā svayam papraccha
tyakta-vāk-manas-kāya-ceṣṭaḥ nir-āyāsaḥ prasanna-cittaḥ ātmanaḥ anyatra nivṛtta-sarva-bāhya-prayojanaḥ iti sukham āste iti ucyate
asmākaṃ pārśve yā bahu-mūlya-ratnānāṃ peṭikā asti
śrutvā etat bhṛśa-śoka-tapta-manasaḥ rāmasya kārya-arthinā
ataḥ saḥ na-vinaya-śīlaḥ asti
daṇḍinam paśya ityatra daṇḍasyaeva dvitīyā-artha-karmatve viśeṣaṇatayā anvayaḥ āpādanīyaḥ
tindukam anna-dravya-ruci-karāṇām
na ca taṇḍulasya karmatā-saṃbandhena dhātu-artha-pāke anvaya-tātparyeṇa
nanu sarvāḥ buddhayaḥ asti-nāsti-buddhi-anugatāḥ eva
tasyā premamayī gāthā ā-bāla-vṛddham janān rasa-bhara-nirbharān akārṣīt
saḥ bhaginyāḥ patyuḥ viṣaye cintayati sma yat saḥ mahān janaḥ asti yat saḥ taṃ yantra-kalā-abhijñāya preritaḥ akarot
atra śūrāḥ maheṣvāsāḥ bhīma-arjuna-samāḥ yudhi
jñāna-niṣṭhā tu karman-niṣṭhā-upāya-labdha-ātmikā satī svātantryeṇa puruṣārtha-hetuḥ anya-na-apekṣā
pada-vikṣepa-śabda-anumitasya na-jñāta-kartṛ-viśeṣasya dhāvanasya caarthasya
go-padasya svarūpa-sambandhena pratyaya-vidhāna-avadhi-rūpa-prakṛti-tva-āśraya tvāt tad-arthena citra-go-svāminā dvitīyā-artha-karmatva-anvayaḥ saṃbhavati
evaṃ sāmūhika-rūpeṇa tāni nirmāya sva-sva-bhāgaṃ gṛhṇanti
bahu-dināni vyatīnāni sva-deśa-parityāgena
jagadīśa-bhaṭṭācāryaḥ tu mocana-anukūla-vyāpāraḥ duheḥarthaḥ
tapta-kārta-svara iva tapaḥ anala-taptam mānava-hṛdayam nir-malyam upaiti
carmakāra-vasatau samutpannaḥ api tat-putraḥ adhunā mahat-jana-ucitam jīvanam jīvati dhavala-dhavalāni vastrāṇi paridhatte
māyā varṇa-śarīra-bheda-karaṇe vāk deśa-bhāṣā-antare
tasya caāśrayatayā prathamā-anta-arthe anvayāt pāka-anukūla-vartamāna-kṛti-abhāva vān caitraḥ iti bodhaḥ
katham vikārān ca guṇān ca eva vakṣyamāṇān vikārān buddhi-ādi-deha-indriya-antān guṇān ca sukha-duḥkha-moha-pratyaya-ākāra-pariṇatān viddhi jānīhi prakṛti-saṃbhavān
na hi vayam kārya-anvita-śakti-vādinaḥ
mārga-āyāsa-parihārāya tām kathām śraddhayā śṛṇotu tāvat iti
kadācit benyahūdaḥ taṃ niveditavān yat jerūsaleṃ-nagara-nivāsinaḥ uddiśya bhavatā udbodhanaṃ karaṇīyam iti
yaḥ śāstra-vidhim śāstram vedaḥ tasya vidhim kartavya-akartavya-jñāna-kāraṇam vidhi-pratiṣedha-ākhyam utsṛjya tyaktvā vartate kāmakārataḥ kāma-prayuktaḥ san
dāmodaraḥ adyaprabhṛti go-brāhmaṇa-puro-gāsu sarva-prajāsu na-pramādaḥ kartavyaḥ
dvitīyaḥ dainyaṃ yāti yudhiṣṭhiraḥatra viduraḥ bāṣpa-ākula-akṣaḥ sthitaḥ
damanakaḥ brūte yatasau sa-darpaḥ śṛṅga-agra-praharaṇa-abhimukhaḥ cakitamivaāgacchati tadā jñāsyati svāmī
gaṅgātvena tīra-śābda-bodhe satieva tīre gaṅgā-vṛtti-dharma-viśeṣa-pratipattiḥ jāyate
na pada-samudāya-ātmanka-samāsa-ādi-vṛttiḥ api
yudhi hatvā kumāreṇa gṛhīte yuṣmad-priya-arthinā
parvate tatra na dhūma-vaiśiṣṭya-jñānam guru-mate
maṇi-viracita-mauliḥ cāru-tāmra-āyata-akṣī
tathāhi arjunena rājya-guru-putra-mitra-suhṛt-svajana-saṃbandhin-bāndhaveṣu aham eṣām mama ete iti evam bhrānti-pratyaya-nimitta-sneha-viccheda-ādi-nimittau ātmanaḥ śoka-mohau pradarśitau katham bhīṣmam aham saṃkhye gītā
atyantam prajñāvantaḥ sanmārgiṇaḥ mānavāḥ api kadācit sva-artha-preritāḥ santaḥ kṛtam vāk-dānam svayam vismaranti
sahasā mama dṛṣṭiḥ bhitteḥ koṇe nihite ekasmin rakta-varṇa-puṭake apatat
rūpam mahat atipramāṇam te tava bahu-vaktra-netram bahūni vaktrāṇi mukhāni netrāṇi cakṣūṃṣi ca yasmin tat rūpam bahu-vaktra-netram
mayi arpita-manaḥ-buddhiḥ mām eva iṣyasi na-saṃśayaḥ
viṣṇuḥ kali-yuga-devatā tvena
kāryatā-smāraka-liṅ-ādi-vākyāt eva kārya-anvita-viṣayakaḥ śābda-bodhaḥ jāyate
haṃsāḥ svapanti maṇi-ratna-śilā-taleṣu
ekavāraṃ śikṣakaḥ kakṣāṃ praviśya eva yadā itastataḥ bhakṣita-mudga-phalīnām āvaraṇāni vikīrṇāni apaśyat
krodha-andha kṛṣakaḥ api laguḍam ādāya tam anu-pra-dhāvan tasya upari prahāram akarot yena ardha-mṛtam iva prasarpan yathā-kathañcit tatra prāpa
surā sa-maṇḍā rūkṣaūṣṇā yavānāṃ vāta-pitta-lā
mayā gamanam na kartavyam priyā-maraṇa-hetu tvātiti
kamalāni kamalāni ityatra lākṣaṇika-kamala-padāt saurabha-viśiṣṭa-kamala tvena bodhaḥ
aham sva-icchā-vihaṃgamaḥ
samagre tasmin nagara-koṇa-kṣetre vasantaḥ janā kārya-vaśāt tām eva ākārayāmāsu
idānīm khalu asmad-kara-sparśanāt saumya-bhāvam upagatāni gṛhyantām
saḥ mahat-mahimā-anvitaḥ
tataḥ asau smayamānaḥ ādiśat yat etasmai anyā api ekā svarṇa-mudrā-pra-pūrṇā pārītrā dīyatām
iti śrutiḥ karman-phala-sāmānyasya naśvaratvam bodhayati
gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ ityatra śakyatā-avacchedaka-gaṅgātvena tīra-bodhaḥ
sa-hṛdaya-su-mūrdhanyā śrīśilābhaṭṭārikā kaumāra-ham varam caitrakṣapā
mahendram dṛṣṭvā ghṛṇā-krodha-tiras-kāra-ādi-bhāva-śabalām sabhrūkuṃcanām phūtkṛtim iva visṛjya ayam mukham parāvartitavān
na kadācid api saḥ evam sva-kartavyam kauśikī-nadyāḥ-tīre karma-karavat pariśramam kuryāt
ḍhuṇḍhim gautama-jaiminīya-vacana-vyākhyātṛbhiḥ dūṣitān
etādṛśa-ghaṭanā-anantaram himakaraḥ jñātavān yat kācit na-dṛṣṭa-śaktiḥ mama sāhāyyam karoti
antatogatvā keśinī sva-vivāha-artham varam ekam anveṣayāmāsa
na hi asya yogasya samyak-darśana-niṣṭhā-lakṣaṇasya mokṣa-ākhyam phalam vyeti
tadā caitra-ādi-jñāne tadīya-pācakatva-ādi-dharma-viśeṣāḥ api bhāsante iti svīkaraṇīyam bhavet
taila-akta-gātrasya narasya kuṣṭhāniudvartayet aśvahana-chadaiḥ ca
calana-ātmakasya karmaṇaḥ na-ātma-kartṛkasya aham karomi iti pravṛtti-darśanāt
manaḥ-śarīra-agni-bala-pradānām a-svapna-śoka-a-ruci-nāśanānām
tad-anantaraṃ kṛṣṇadevarāyeṇa nagara-śulka-ālayasya bhraṣṭa-ācaraṇaḥ adhikārī sevā-vṛtteḥ niṣkāsitaḥ mantrī ca nirbhartsitaḥ
saṃskṛta-chātra-sulabhā yad bhāvi tad bhavatu iti bhāvanā vā āsīt
vi-kṛta-vapuṣaḥ api ugra-ācārāḥ ghṛṇā na tu varjitā
para-avara-parīkṣā-arthaṃ tatra śāstra-vidāṃ balam
prabhu-śakti-prakaṭīkaraṇam īśitavyān prati
laghu-laghu-sthāneṣu bileṣu vā drutaṃ nilīyante sma
tathāvidhāḥ hi kevale śarīra-jñāne śarīra-abhinirvṛtti-jñāne prakṛti-vikāra-jñāne ca niḥsaṃśayāḥ
atra ucyate ātman-vidaḥ nivṛtta-mithyā-jñāna tvāt
bhaṭāḥ dāsyaḥ ca ekaikaśaḥ na-pūrva-darpaṇasya agra-bhāga taḥ apara-pārśvam gatavantaḥ
teṣām na-sabhya-ceṣṭayā kupitaḥ viśvāmitraḥ śāpam dattavān re mūrkhāḥ duṣṭa-yādavāḥ etasya garbhataḥ musalaḥ utpatsyate
sā bahu-pra-yatnam akarot kintu śyāṃgaḥ kimapi kāryam na kṛtavān
pañca kāsāḥiti vāta-pitta-kapha-kṣata-kṣaya-jāḥ
pavitraṃ vṛṣyamāyuṣyaṃ śrama-sveda-mala-apaham
itastataḥ viyati pra-sarpan dhūmaḥ hasta-yugma-pramāṇaṃ pramāya saṃcitya ca kathaṃ rājñe samarpyeta iti āsīt teṣāṃ cintā-viṣayaḥ
tvamapi mahat-rāja-vacanena ārya-purohitaṃ yathāupacāreṇa tvaraya
tatra saṃbhavat-sakala-ākṣepa-parihāra-varṇana-pūrvakam
bhāvanātvamiti nirukta-kāryatā-avacchedaka-koṭi-praviṣṭam suptvam prātipadikatvam ca naanugatamiti kva anugata-kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvasya avakāśaḥ
nanu śabda-vyāpāra-janya-śābda-bodha-na-antaram vyaṅgyatva-abhimata-tad-tad-artha-viṣayaka-mānasa-pratyaya jāyate
nir-māna-mohāḥ jita-saṅga-doṣāḥ
āpīḍa-dāma-śikhi-barha-vicitra-veṣaḥ
evam-rītyā vākya-eka-vākya-tāyāḥ upapādaneapi bhāṣya-siddhāyāḥ pada-eka-vākya-tāyāḥ asaṃbhavāt
na an-āvṛta-mukhaḥ jṛmbhāṃ kṣavathuṃ hāsyaṃ vā pravartayet
iti matvā tasya nāsikā-cheda-artham utkocāya suvarṇa-khaṇḍam vastra-añcale baddhavām ca ānītavān ataḥ nyāyaḥ tasya pakṣe mayā karaṇīyaḥ
sudevaḥ he mahā-rāja ṛṣi-prasāda-sañjātāyāḥ damayantyāḥ kalpanāiyam
iti padyam priya-gamana-na-kartavya-tva-tātparyakam
joṣam sthitasya pitāmahasya anumatiḥ labdhā mayā iti ca sīvana-karma-mañjūṣām ādāya nirjagāma mandirāt
sandeśa-vāhakāt ca avāgacchat yat rātrau rājan-puro-hitaḥ rājñaḥ gupta-kakṣe gataḥ āsīt
asmābhiḥtu tad-bodha-aupayika-ākāṃkṣā-ghaṭaka tvāttatiti kaḥ viśeṣaḥ
tatra putrīṃ sukhinīṃ samavalokya saḥ muditaḥ abhavat kṛṣiphala-ādi-viṣaye apṛcchat ca
utpāda-vyaya-darśanāt nyā
ekadā kecit puṣpa-sāra-vikretāraḥ kṛṣṇadevarāyasya rājan-sabhāyām samāyayuḥ
yadi ca kṛñ-dhātu-samāna-arthaka tvāt yateḥ
kim prekṣase mama mukham cira-kāla-dṛṣṭaḥ
karma-vāk-manaḥ-śarīra-pravṛttiḥ
brahman-śabda-vācyatvāt sa-vikalpakam brahma
tathā ca arthasya hiraṇya-pūrva-kaśipu-śabdasya ca sāmānādhikaraṇyena prayogaḥ tayoḥtādātmyam draḍhayati
pratyak-ātma-avikriya-svarūpa-niṣṭhatvāt ca mokṣasya
bhavantaḥ catvāraḥ setu-pṛṣṭha-sthāḥ tat-upari nipatantu
na-kāla-sainyayuktaḥ tu hanyate kāla-yodhinā
vidarbha-rāja-udyānam pūrṇimā-samayaḥ ceṭyau praviśataḥ
iti evam manvānasya arjunasya karman-anuṣṭhāna-karman-saṃnyāsayoḥ na-vidvat-puruṣa-kartṛkatvam api asti iti
matiḥ ca mūḍhāḥ su-cira-abhilāṣāt
ahaṃ svayaṃ roga-nirmuktaḥ san tāṃ vismaya-vi-mugdhāṃ kartum icchāmi
durbhikṣavyasanaupetaḥ bala-vyasana-saṃkulaḥ
yatcaapi deśa-kāla-agni-mātrā-sātmya-anila-ādibhiḥ
yasya kṛte abhiṣeka-maṇḍapaṃ kṛtam āsīt tasya eva kṛte daṇḍaka-araṇya-gamanaṃ prastutam
īśvara-vyatirekeṇa vā saṃsāriṇaḥ anyasya abhāvāt saṃsāra-abhāva-prasaṅgaḥ
paritaḥ bhūta-preta-ādayaḥ aṭṭahāsam kurvantaḥ santi
viduṣaḥ karman-na-saṃbhava vacanāt yāni karmāṇi śāstreṇa vidhīyante tāni na viduṣaḥ vihitāni iti bhagavataḥ niścayaḥ avagamyate
sarva-mate api avaśyam jñeyaḥ saṃketaḥ eva samaya-apara-paryāyaḥ śaktiḥ
navya-vaiyākaraṇāḥ tu samayasya saṃbandhatvam nirākurvāṇāḥ vācya-vācaka-bhāva-ākhya-atirikta-saṃbandham svīkurvantaḥ svayam saṃketa-padena saṃketitasya śabda-artha-tādātmyasya tad-grāhaka tām pratipādayanti
pañca-indriya-adhiṣṭhānāni
yuktaḥ harṣa-ādi-viṣayaḥ bhagavān
yat daṃṣṭrā-nakha-lāṅgula-praharaṇaḥ siṃhaḥ vanam gāhate
bārhadratha-apahṛta-viṣaya-kīrti-bhogaḥ tava puruṣa-uttamaḥ
kathaṃ kalpanā-loka-vicaraṇaṃ kuryāt taṃ phalavantam
samyak-darśanena apāsta-mithyā-jñānasya niṣkriya-ātman-svarūpa-avasthāna-lakṣaṇam sarva-karman-saṃnyāsam uktvā
viśiṣṭa-buddhau viśeṣaṇa-jñānasya eva janakatvāt saṃsarga-jñānasya na-hetu tvāt vākya-artha-bodha-anvaya-upasthitiḥ na apekṣitā
sarva-guṇa-sampannā ca
eṣaḥ kramaḥ na-viveka-yutaḥ na vā kīdṛśam vairāgyam tasya kim saḥ mūrkhaḥ na mama eteṣām sandehānām uttaram jānan api bhavān yadi na vadet tarhi bhavataḥ śiraḥ sahasradhā bhagnam bhavet iti
adhi-vāsa-gaṃdha
varṇa-āśrama-vyavasthā api
tarūṭa-bisa-śālūka-krauñcādana-kaśerukam
viśvavidyālayaḥ api samprati ātaṅka upadruta vighnitā adhyayana-adhyāpana-kramaḥ na-udghāṭita eva
yadā vyāsaḥ vivāha-yogyaṃ kālaṃ prāptavān tadā tasya vivāhaḥ jābāli-mahat-ṛṣeḥ putrikayā vaṭikā-nāma ikayā abhavat iti kathā śrūyate
dvā-daśa-māsāḥ eva akṣāḥ
nirūpitatva-saṃbandhena taṇḍula-anvitam tat āśrayatā-saṃbandhena dhātu-artha-phale anveti
saḥ tasyām eva rātrau sa-upakaraṇa-sambhāraḥ vijayanagarāt palāyanaṃ cakāra
evam yajeta svarga-kāmaḥ iti-ādau yāge pratīyamānasya svarga-sādhana tvasya mānasa-bodha-viṣaya tvam svīkṛtya
tasya sarva-anubhava-siddha tvena tad-abhāvasya āpādayitum na-śakya tvāt
prāk-abhāvasya eva dvi-aṇuka-ādi-dravya-ākhyasya utpatti-ādi-vyavahāra-arhatvam
anubhavasya vyākhyāna-na-apekṣa tvātca itiucyate
śakaṭī-vega-ārambha-āghāta-prabhāvāt
chanda-baddha-stutyā ca taṃ tuṣṭāva
jala-da-samaya-toya-dāḥ iva amī
itiihauktāni mūtrāṇi yathā-sāmarthya-yogataḥ
tiṅ-arthasya kārakasya dhātu-arthe viśeṣaṇatvamiti pakṣe sādhakatayā apārthaka-nigraha-sthāna-lakṣaṇa-sūtra-bhāṣye sthitam kriyā-kāla-yoga-abhidhāyi ākhyātam dhātu-artha-mātram ca kāla-abhidhāna-viśiṣṭam
yadi tasmai daśa-svarṇa-mudrā dadyāṃ
patanti pitaro hi eṣām lupta-piṇḍa-udaka-kriyāḥ
anena khalu sahasā na-sāmayika-upajāta-viplava-viśeṣeṇa sampūrṇaḥ api pāñcāla-prānta nitāntam utpīḍita dukha-atiśaya-gabhīra-garte nipatita na manāk api śāntim ākalayati
viduṣaḥ punaḥ na-vikriya-ātma-darśinaḥ phala-arthitva-abhāvāt pravṛtti-na-upapattau kārya-karaṇa-saṃghāta-vyāpāra-uparame nivṛttiḥ upacaryate
aho āścaryam daśa-nimeṣa-abhyantare ākāśaḥ kṛṣṇa-meghaiḥ ācchannaḥ na-kālikī iva tasya varṣasya prathamā vṛṣṭiḥ ārabdhā eva
ākhyāta-upasthāpite pratiyogitve bhāvanāyām vartamānaḥ kālaḥ sva-vṛtti-utpattika-nāśa-nirūpita-tva-saṃbandhena anveti
na-āhūta eva yuva-rāja mantraṇā-āgāram praviṣṭaḥ hūṇa-ākramaṇa-viṣaye jāyamānām mantraṇām aśṛṇot yat asmin yuddhe ke ke gamiṣyanti kasya netṛtvam syāt katham ca yuddha-sañcālanam vidheyam ityādi
rākṣasa-mahat-rājena hiraṇyakaśipunā ghorā tapaścaryā ācaritā
saḥ sva-samudra-yātrāyāḥ prāk sva-na-upasthitau gṛha-vyayāya nācammāyai āvaśyakam arthaṃ dattvā gacchati
na-vibhaktaṃ-vibhakteṣu tat jñānam viddhi sāttvikam
dāha-jvara-apahaṃ sparśāt pānāt vāta-kapha-apaham
vṛddha-brāhmaṇa-rūpa-dhāriṇā anantena sva-guhām prati nīta
atha ekasmin dine vāsantī nitya-krama-anusāram mādhavanātham upacarantī gṛha-karmaṇi saṃlagnā āsīt
sā kadāpi na-satya-bhāṣaṇaṃ na karoti sm
kāraṇam guṇa-saṅgaḥ asya sat-asad-yoni-janmasu
āhvāna-āmantraṇa-nimantraṇam na-svīkurvantī
smṛta-śakya-artha-pravāhasya ghoṣa-pada-artha-anvaya-anupapatti-pratisandhāne sati
bhāva-viśeṣyaka-bodhaḥ abhimataḥ
dharma-artha-kāmān puruṣaḥ sukhī bhuṅkte cinoti ca
tasya hi gahana-anu-ikṣikīratā sūkṣma-īkṣiṇī dṛṣṭiḥ manye śaṅkamānā bhavet yat mā bhūt etayo sakhyam pra-gāḍham yena parastāt samasyāḥ udbhaveyuḥ iti
sveda-avagāhana-abhyaṅgān sarpiṣaḥcaavapīḍakam
benyahūdasya amerikā-gamana-vārtā tatratyānāṃ yahūdyānāṃ madhye prasṛtā
punaśca kara-tala-dhvani satatam vardhamānā āsīt
rocanaṃ dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ balyaṃ pitta-a-virodhi ca
gabhīrāyām nadīiti bhāgasya gabhīra-nadī-tīra-lakṣaka tve gabhīrām nadīm vrajet
ataḥ yat prakṛti-puruṣayoḥ kārya-karaṇa-kartṛtvena sukha-duḥkha-bhoktṛtvena ca saṃsāra-kāraṇatvam uktam
tad-anantaram kim abhūt iti kārya-antara-vyāpṛtaiḥ asmābhiḥ api na jijñāsitam
dhūli-dhūsaritasya tasya prakoṣṭhasya ekasmin koṇe svīyaṃ rāṅkavam āstaraṇa-rūpeṇa prasārya tad-upari dvi-māsa-deśīyāṃ putrīṃ yemimāṃ śāyayitvā ḍeborā putrau avadat vatsau jāgarūkatayā rakṣaṇīyā eṣā
na tu sat-buddhi-viṣayaḥ
iti sahacaraṇa-sūtra-vyākhyāna-avasare nirūpayan
yuga-pariṇāma-samudyataḥ yathā arkaḥ
jāyante a-mārga-vihite teṣāṃ siddhiṣu sādhanam
viṣṇu-bhakti-mahimā
vāsudevaḥ bhoḥ suyodhana deśa-kāla-avasthā-apekṣi khalu śauryam naya-anugāminām
mahat-bhūta-viśākhaḥ ca viṣayaiḥ patravān tathā
tādṛśa-tīra-smṛti-janaka tvamca klṛptasya śakya-saṃbandhasya eva kalpayitumucitam
na-phala-prepsunā phalam prepsati iti phala-prepsuḥ phala-tṛṣṇaḥ tad-viparītena na-phala-prepsunā kartrā kṛtam karma yat
tatviśuddhaṃ hi rudhiraṃ bala-varṇa-sukha-āyuṣā
na-ukta-klība-vacanam dhanyam kasyaapi jīvanam
advaita-tatva-vicāre api patañjali-bahumānāt śeṣa-kṛta-paramārthasārāt uddhṛtāḥ kārikāḥ vyācakṣate
kravyāt-māṃsarasa-abhyāsaḥ grahaṇīdoṣa-śoṣa-arśaḥ-ghnānāṃ
giri-taṭa-kaṭhina-aṃsau eva bāhū mama etau
rāghavaṃ sarva-dharma-jñaṃ tathā māṃ pātu pāvakaḥ
tathā ca abhyāsa-atiśaya-prayukta-saṃskāra-atiśaya-rūpa-kāraṇa-vaśāt sva-artha-svarūpa-mātra-smaraṇam upapadyate
uccaiḥ-bhāṣya-ati-bhāṣyābhyāṃ tīkṣṇa-pānāt prajāgarāt
taila-kāra-patnī rājñī-pārśvam āgatya ca ābhāra-pradarśanam kṛtavatī
sa-patnī-sneham
utpatti-rūpa-phala-āśraya tvātodanasya ca karmatā
gadādhara-bhaṭṭācārya-racitam tad-vyākhyānam tu na mudrāpitam
prakṛte ca na-jñāta-vācakaḥ artha-darśī puruṣaḥ
drākṣā-kharjūra-priyāla-badara-dāḍima-phalgu-paruṣaka-ikṣu-yava-ṣaṣṭikāḥ iti daśaimāni śramaharāṇi bhavanti
madīya-dravya-yācana-lāghavasya asya upari vismaya-ākulā mat-patnī lalitā
jayasena janma-nakṣatra-kriyā-vyāpṛtasya mahat-rājasya tāvat akāla-nivedanaṃ
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat bhoḥ rājan bhavān na-mānuṣīm na-gocarīm kāñcit śaktim sampādayitum yatamānaḥ syāt
karmatva-ādi-śaktiḥ ca dvitīyā-dyotyā prakṛti-artha-viśeṣaṇam eva
evañcaatra vivakṣita-artha-bodhaḥ saṃpannaḥ bhavati vibhakti-arthaḥ api laghuḥiti bodhyam
ataḥ ahaṃ prārthaye yat asmāsu na-viśvāsam akurvatā bhavatā etad-patra-prāpti-samanantaram eva śata nepoliyan mitaṃ dhanaṃ preṣaṇīyam iti
kuṣṭha-hṛllāsa-vīsarpāḥ chardi-nigraha jāḥ gadāḥ
antya-varṇasya vācakatvam pūrva-pūrva-varṇānām tātparya-grāhaka tvamiti kaḥarthaḥ
tenālīrāmaḥ avadat bhavatā eva kathitam āsīt yat śukasya mṛtyu-samācāra-sūcakaḥ prāṇa-daṇḍaṃ lapsyate
deśa-kāla-anusāram sva-kartavya-pālanam eva yuktaḥ dharmaḥ
bhavān tu svapna-prabhāvena svargasya api sva-manas-anukūlaṃ dohanaṃ karoti
ekā padānām sva-artha-smāraka-śaktiḥ
ataḥ vārdhakya-kāle tasya manasi evaṃ vicāraḥ āgataḥ ahaṃ sad-guṇa-sampannaḥ eva
sāmpram tu na-sūrya-paśyā rājan-dārā api vivṛta-vadanā ā-hiṇḍante pattaneṣu
ime vīra-rāja-putrā premāṇam yuddha-kauśalam ca sarvasvam amanyanta
śīta-vāta-ātapa-kleśān sahante yān para-āśritāḥ
nūnam yudhiṣṭhira-parājaya-kopita-ātmā
nūnam eva sam-ucita-sthānam tu asmākam kṛte haste mata-adhikāra-prāpaṇena eva upalabdham
śābdayāmi iti na-bādhita-anuvyavasāya-balāt anvaya-anubhavaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ eva śābda-bodha ātmankaḥ
utpannaḥ ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti pratīteḥ niṣpadyamānam prākasat iti tad-sūtra-arthaḥ
tenālīrāmasya prahasanāni jana-manas-raṃjane prabhāvīṇi āsan
āṭa-upasajjāḥ paṭaha-rūpa-veṣāḥ vyāhartum gacchāmaḥ
vayasā vṛddhaḥ aham yadākadācid api iha-loka-yātrām samāpayeyam
kadācit te pra-ucca-svareṇa cītkāram akurvan kintu himānīm vihāya na kimapi dṛk-gocaram abhūt teṣām
pra-adhyāpakānām nilayeṣu gamana-āgamana-vyājena bahiḥ eva avrajat
taiḥ pakṣa-antara-abhiprāyeṇa pravṛttam niruktam pratyaya-artha-apekṣayā dhātu-arthasya prādhānye pramāṇatayāudbhāvayitum na śakyeta
guru-jana-vandana-miśra-śubhra-vaktraḥ
rājñāṃ veṣṭana-paṭṭa-ghṛṣṭa-caraṇāḥ ślāghya-prabhūta-śravāḥ
itaḥ param eka-varṣaṃ yāvat na-jñāta-vāsaṃ kartuṃ veṣaṃ parivartya virāṭ-rājasya āśrayaṃ svīkṛtavantaḥ
iti śrīmat-bhagavat-gītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde mokṣa-yogaḥ nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ
deveśa-nirviśeṣam śerasiṃham tadīyau pitarau sa-sneha-bahumānam āmanyete
rājā rāja-guṇa-upetaḥ bhūmim ekaḥ praśāstu naḥ
tatra saḥ citra-paṭa-viṣayakāni bahūni pustakāni paṭhitavān iti saḥ svayameva likhitavān
sarve api śiṣyā mahat-ṛṣi-vacanam śrutvā jhaṭiti teṣām ātithyāya sannaddhā babhūvu
roṣā-aruṇa-nayanaḥ śreṣṭhī avadat bho kim idaṃ jalpasi tvaṃ māṃ cauryasya āropeṇa kalaṅkayasi tvadīyaḥ syūtaḥ mayā yathāvat samarpitaḥ
kiñca pratyakṣa-ādi-māna-antara-upasthitasya śābda-bodhe bhāna-abhāvena tad-viṣayaka-śābda-bodhe pada-janya-tad-upasthiteḥ hetutāyāḥ vācyatvāt
śanaiḥ vihāya kāścana pragalbhā dhṛṣṭā indra-jāla-nipuṇā patintudā anyā ramaṇya sva-gṛham gatā
apāsya nārāyaṇa-cakra-jaṃ bhayaṃ cira-pra-naṣṭān paribhūya pāṇḍavān
saḥ vi-kāryatā-grastaḥ āsīt
diṣṭyā prakṛti-stha-śarīraḥ ārya-putraḥ
ekadā kasyacit vidyārthina patram adhyakṣasya savidhe samāgacchat aham adhyāpaka-capaṇḍuka-mahodayasya sevāyām pustakam idam upahartum icchāmi iti
aham tvā tvām evam niścita-buddhim sarva-pāpebhyaḥ sarva-dharma-adharma-bandhana-rūpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi sva-ātma-bhāva-prakāśīkaraṇena
vācya-vācaka-bhāva-vyavahāra-niyāmakaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pada-artha-antaram iti vyavasthāpayanti
ulūka-svara-śravaṇa-bhītayā kāntayā pariṣvaktaḥ khalu ayam tapasvī
rājā anurūpametat bhavatyāabhihitaṃ vāsavadattā-sva-janaḥ sva-janaḥ iti
yadṛcchā-lābha-santuṣṭaḥ dvandva-atītaḥ vi-matsaraḥ
anyonya-abhāva-bodhaka tāyāḥ
tathā api te hi kāpilāḥ guṇa-gauṇa-vyāpāra-nirūpaṇe abhiyuktāḥ iti tad-śāstram api vakṣyamāṇa-artha-stuti-arthatvena upādīyate iti na virodhaḥ
saṃkṣipta-yukti-anvita-tarkabhāṣā viracyate tasya kṛte mayāeṣā
na hi icchā-dveṣa-doṣa-vaśīkṛta-cittasya yathā-bhūta-artha-viṣaya-jñānam utpadyate bahiḥ api
evam anuśāsana-udāharaṇa-prasaṅge pramādaḥapi dṛśyate bhaṭṭācāryāṇām
jala-ādi-upacāreṇa jātaḥ cetanaḥ haradeva saṃmukhe mohanam avalokya anena eva duṣṭena mama śirasi pātitaḥ daṇḍa
iti na-upapanna-artham kalpitam syāt
deva-pitṛ-manuṣya-paśu-mṛga-ādi-sarva-yoniṣu aunteya
katham saṃnyāsa-karman-yogau niḥśreyasakarau
jala-niṣkāsana-vyavasthāyāḥ abhāvaḥ
yadi grāma-pakṣa-pātam avalambya bhavantaḥ pūrva-uktam kuryuḥ tadā kim āścaryam
bhoḥ bhoḥ vṛṣṇi-yodhāḥ anāvṛṣṭi-śibaka-hṛdika-pṛthuka-somadatta-akrūra-pramukhāḥ
apabhraṃśe nirukta-śakti-jñānasya bhramatvamupapādanīyam
śābdika-maryādayā bahūnām vākyānām pramāṇika-tad-tad-grantha-anurodhena navya-naiyāyika-saraṇyā śābda-bodha-varṇana-garbhitaḥ svatantraḥ vistṛtaḥ vicāraḥ
sā iyam jñāna-niṣṭhā ārta-ādi-bhakti-traya-apekṣayā parā caturthī bhaktiḥ iti uktā
harṣa-śoka-anvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
tathā lāvaka-piñjala-śaśa-hariṇa-eṇa-kālapucchaka-mṛgamātṛka-urabhrān
ṛdhyati rāṣṭraṃ jana-śakti-yutam
yācakebhyaḥ prabhūtatayā dhana-dhānya-ādīnām dānam karotu iti
avidyā-adhyāropitatvāt ātmani kriyā-kāraka-phalānām
teṣu dineṣu vijayanagaraṃ candana-sāgauna-kāṣṭha-vikraya-arthaṃ prakhyātaṃ kendram āsīt
urvara-bhūmi-dharāḥ api bubhukṣitā sañjātā
tannāma asmākaṃ sainya-nirmāṇa-yojanā māsa-trayaṃ yāvat vyākṣiptā bhavati
vayam api khalu raudrāḥ rākṣasa-ugra-svabhāvāḥ
tvacyaḥ keśyaḥca balyaḥca vāta-ghnaḥ kapha-pitta-kṛt
pravartaka-jñāna-viṣayasya
bhiṣakbubhūṣuḥmatimānataḥ sva-guṇa-sampadi
ākhyāta-artha-kṛteḥ prathamā-anta-arthe
yadyapi śāsana-abhāva-vādaḥ samāje yaśasvī abhavat tathāpi tasya manasi ayaṃ vicāraḥ āsīt yāvat sampūrṇā prajā sat-ācāra iṇī asti vivekinī asti pāpa-bhīruḥ ca asti tāvat eva iyaṃ śāsana-rītiḥ upayuktā
vyatirikta-ātma-darśana-pratipatteḥ prāk eva phala-hetvoḥ ātman-abhimānasya siddhatvāt
rājā ghoṣaṇām kāritavān yat paraśva somavāsare lakṣa-pati-śreṣṭha inaḥ divya-parīkṣā bhaviṣyati
odana-pada-uttara-dvitīyāyāḥ dhātu-artha-anvayi-utpādakatva-arthaka tāmca vyutpādayanti bhaṭṭācāryāḥ vyutpatti-vāde
prāyaḥ prathamā-anta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣyakaḥ bodhaḥ
tādṛśa-bodha-na-sambhavāt prāthamya-viśiṣṭa-bhakṣa-vidhānam uktam saṃgacchate
na ca etat tvayā mantavyam karma nāma deha-ādi-ceṣṭāḥ loka-prasiddham
śabdasya bodha-kāraṇa tvam na-upapannam iti jñānam śabde bodha-kāraṇa-tva-prakārakam eva jñānam pratibadhnāti
cakraḥ asmi kṛṣṇasya kara-agra-śobhī
nirmāṇa-śālā-adhyakṣaḥ yuvakaṃ kim avocat
vijñapteḥ anusāreṇa ekaḥ vi-kāryatā-grastaḥ yuvakaḥ sākṣātkāra-artham upasthitaḥ
rāma-śabda-arthaḥ yathā pinākinaḥ māna-bhaṅga-prayojakaḥ tathā rāma-nāma api sva-vācya-artha-dvārā māna-bhaṅga-prayojakam itiāśayena śabdasya māna-bhañjaka tvamabhihitamiti na tādātmya-ādhyāsaḥ
vikasita-śata-patra-dāma kalpā
koṭara-antara-deha-sthāḥ khagāḥ prāṇāḥ ivaudgatāḥ
akṣṇoḥ agre vividhān vicitrān ca mahat-nagarīya-padārthān apaśyan te
gātram sandhiṣu dīrghatām upagatam śayyā-pramāṇa-adhikam
citrakamūlaṃ dīpanīya-pācanīya-guda-śotha-arśaḥ-śūla-harāṇāṃ
asmāt prasaṅgāt anantaraṃ ratnākaraḥ rāma-nāma-japarūpasya tapasaḥ prārambhaṃ kṛtavān
nāma-samudāya-ātmanka-samāsasya eka-artha-bhāvam ca nirṇīya
tad-tad-vibhakti-artha-prakāraka-śābda-bodham prati tad-tad-kriyā-pada-janya-upasthitiḥ kāraṇamiti viśiṣyaeva kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvaḥ vācyaḥ
kiṃ madīye rājye etāvantaḥ janāḥ śani-pra-kopeṇa pīḍitāḥ santi tatra sthitaḥ nara-īśaḥ janānāṃ mukhāt aśṛṇot yat asya rājyasya śāsana-vyavasthā doṣa-pūrṇā asti
caitra-ādi-pada-uttara-prathamā ca na viśeṣyatayā prātipādika-artha-anvaya-yogyam arthamabhidhate
anyā api ekā vārtā prāptā yat mahārāṣṭra-janaiḥ ajamera-mālava-prāntayoḥ svāmitvaṃ prāptam
avidyā ca saha kāryeṇa hātavyā iti śruti-smṛti-nyāyebhyaḥ avagamyate
kula-kṣaya-kṛtaṃ doṣaṃ prapaśyadbhiḥ janārdana
guṇa-pravṛddhāḥ guṇaiḥ sattva-rajas-tamobhiḥ pravṛddhāḥ sthūlīkṛtāḥ upādāna-bhūtaiḥ
śvaśrū-māna-mardanam dampatyoḥ madhye ca vāk-yuddha-ādi kam sarvam su-vicāritam caritram prasārya narakāyitam gṛham akarot
āvām asyāṃ vaṭa-vṛkṣa-cchāyāyāṃ viśramāvaḥ
yaḥ ayam laukikaḥ vaidikaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ saḥ utpanna-viveka-jñānasya sthita-prajñasya avidyā-kāryatvāt avidyā-nivṛttau nivartate
mayi arpita-manaḥ-buddhiḥ yaḥ asmat-bhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ
haste ca bābū-mahāśayasya cākacakyaśālī paṭa-sampuṭakaḥ dvitīye ca veśa-gaurava-bhayāt iva kampamānā subhagā yaṣṭiḥ āsīt
ajā-bandhana-rajjum haste dhṛtvā praśāntena cetasā nirgacchat āsīt bālakaḥ
yato hi para-dṛṣṭi-sparśanena ucchiṣṭam iva jāyate sarvam eva bhojyam
na-avaratam antaḥ vahi praviśatā nirgacchatā ca jana-sammardena samākulam āsīt dīnānātha-gṛha-dvāram
saḥ hi gagana-vihārī kalmaṣa-dhvaṃsa-kārī
auṣadhaṃ hi an-abhijñātaṃ nāma-rūpa-guṇaiḥ tribhiḥ
tataḥ saḥ rāmam uddiśya avadat bhrātaḥ strī-vacana-vaśīkṛtaḥ rājā yukta-na-yukta-vivecana-rahitaḥ jātaḥ asti iti prajāḥ jānīyuḥ
te puṇyam āsādya sura-indra-lokam aśnanti divyān divi deva-bhogān
samāna-śīla-vyasaneṣu sakhyaṃ bhavati eva
yajeta svarga-kāmaḥ iti śruti-pramāṇa-avagata-yāga-niṣṭha-svarga-sādhana-tā-nirvāhāya apūrva-kāraṇatāyāḥ kalpanātiti vācyam
yā samāna-guṇa-abhyāsa-viruddha-anna-oṣadha-kriyā
tatca nīla-tādātmya vān ghaṭaḥ iti-ākāraka-abheda-prakāraka-śābda-bodhe bādha-jñāna-vidhayā pratibandhakam
caitra-na-bhinna-āśrayakaḥ vartamāna-svāpaḥ iti anvaya-bodhaḥ
etat-sthala-anurodhena vyutpatti-antara-kalpanam tu sarva-abhimatam eva
tāḥ tārakāḥ sva-jīvana-rahasyaṃ kathayanti iti bhāsate
sva-karma-labdhena vittena sarve sukhena jīvanti
advaita-siddha-na-khaṇḍa-artha-vāde
vāta-pitta-praśamanī bṛṃhaṇī bala-vardhanī
payas-himaṃ mūlyaṃ na miliṣyati cet saḥ payas-himaṃ-udyogī tena saha kathaṃ vyavahariṣyati iti viṣaye cintayan saḥ jaḍavat bhūmau aluṭhat
nigṛhītāni sarvaśaḥ sarva-prakāraiḥ mānasa-ādi-bhedaiḥ indriyāṇi indriya-arthebhyaḥ śabda-ādibhyaḥ tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā
vi-gata-bhayāḥ hi vayam vinaṣṭa-śokāḥ
tathā gavi ayam go-śabdaḥ iti pratīteḥabhāvāt go-śabdaḥ vācyatva-upalakṣaka tayā idam-pada-artha-upādhiḥ
rājan-mārga-saṅkīrṇena śīta-sukumāreṇa vātena pade pade vikṣobhyamāṇa-janita-taraṅga-taila-pūrṇa-bhājanam dīpam katham api rakṣitvā gṛhītvā āgataḥ asmi
saḥ dakṣiṇā-abhi-mukhaṃ parivartya bhartāraṃ samara-vyāyāma-saṃ-kṣobhitān nir-upacāraṃ saṃ-kṣipya keśān pīḍayitvā kareṇa karavāle pra-hāra-vegam utpādayitu-kāmaḥ ādhāvat
medhyaṃ pavitramāyuṣyam a-lakṣmī-kali-nāśanam
go-ādi-padāt vyakteḥbodhaḥ āvaśyakaḥ
sāttvikasya api karmaṇaḥ na-ātman-vit sa-ahaṃkāraḥ kartā
yadā kṣudhāyāṃ tasya karṇau nadituṃ prārabhatāṃ tadā agre calitum na-kṣamaḥ saḥ ekatra mārga-stha-nalāt jalaṃ pītvā samīpa-sthasya vṛkṣasya adhaḥ viśrāma-artham upaviṣṭavān
sarve bhojanena sākaṃ jalam api pibanti kintu puro-hitasya kośaḥ nirantaraṃ haimī-bhakṣaṇa-paraḥ asti
ittham na-artha-śatam na-āśaṅkya kṛta-sāhasām mām mā prati ākhyāhi
ye ca yavanā bhāratavarṣīyāṇām na-upamayā anukampayā asmat-deśa-nivāsa-ādiṣu saulabhyam alabhanta
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat aye rājan bhavān kasyacit māntrikasya apa-mānam kṛtavān syāt
khura-agra-pātaiḥ likhita-ardha-candrā
tasya svāgataṃ karomi yataḥ mṛtyoḥ anantaram ahaṃ punaḥ navaṃ janma svīkṛtya sva-rājya-prāpti-arthaṃ prayatituṃ śaknomi
saṃskṛta-bhāṣāyāḥ samparke āgantukaḥ kiṃ na saṃskṛtaḥ arthāt saṃskāra-sampannaḥ bhavet saḥ akathayat aham api adhunā sva-putram āṅgla-vidyā-ālayataḥ apasārya saṃskṛta-vidyā-ālaye eva praveśayiṣyāmi iti
etau api sa-āśiṣ-vādam kim kim mahat-rāja viśvāmitra api mahat-rāja viśvāmitrasya etat sarvam sainya-ādi kam vartate
kathaṃ na ime ātmīyān putra-pautra-ādīn parama-īśvarāya balidāna-arthaṃ mārayanti kiṃ parama-īśvaraḥ asmākaṃ santānānāṃ baliṃ gṛhītvā prasannaḥ bhavati
mama pravāsa-duḥkha-ārtā mātā kuśalinī nanu
prathamā-anta-arthasya saṃkhyā-viśeṣya tvātca
deva-jāti-prasūtau api tiryaktvam asmākaṃ-ajñānaṃ-hetuḥ
śreṣṭhinaḥ mūrkhatā-pūrṇa-kriyayā dhannā nitarām ut-vignaḥ jāta
yaugandharāyaṇaḥ bhavatu bhavatu tulya-pari-śramau bhavantau āstāṃ bhavān bhavānapiāstām
iti ākhyāta-vāda-dīdhitau vākāraḥ samuccaya-arthaḥ
eṣaḥ dhūrtaḥ kapaṭī māyā-cāraḥ ca asmat dale praveśaṃ na arhati iti udīrya saḥ tābhyāṃ paśu-pakṣi-dalābhyāṃ niṣkāsitaḥ abhavat
tathā ca prātipādika-artha-prakāraka iti kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvasya nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ ityatra vyabhicārāt kāryatā-avacchedaka-koṭau bheda-saṃbandha-avacchinna-prakaratā niveśanīyā
evañca gaṅgā-pada-janya-bodha-viṣaya tāttve na
gṛhṇāti haṃsyāḥ pakṣa-āghātaḥ-dhvaniḥ
kṣut-vega-nigrahāt tatra snigdha-uṣṇaṃ laghu bhojanam
yathā hari-ādi-padasya
na-ātmanaḥ tu na-jita-ātmanaḥ tu śatrutve śatru-bhāve varteta ātmā eva śatruvat
ṛtusena kandarpa iva ramyā-ākṛti svīya-prabhāva-anubhāva-ādibhiḥ atitarām ākarṣaka kāminī-jana-mana-moha kaḥ ca avartata
atha anyedyuḥ bhaṭṭasomadevaḥ pātheya-srastara-ādi-granthim nibadhya grāma-adhipatim vīrasiṃham āpṛcchya ca piśāca-uddharaṇāya pratasthe
etasyāḥ buddheḥ janmanaḥ prāk ātmanaḥ deha-ādi-vyatiriktatva-kartṛtva-bhoktṛtva-ādi-apekṣaḥ dharma-na-dharma-viveka-pūrvakaḥ mokṣa-sādhana-anuṣṭhāna-lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ
abhihita-anvaya-mate api akṣa-śabdasya triṣu artheṣu śakti-trayam trayāṇām pada-arthānām vākya-artha-budghi-śakti-trayam iti śakti-ṣaṭkam iti śakti-kalpana-tulyam eva tathāpi yatra nānā-śabdānām ekaḥarthaḥ
etaiḥ guṇaiḥ prabhāvitaḥ bhūtvā eva vālmīki-mahat-ṛṣiḥ rāmāyaṇa-nāma kaṃ mahat-kāvyaṃ viracitavān
bhavatyā sāmanta-vaibhava śālini prāṅgaṇe eva dhānya-puñja-upari unmattam krīḍatām asmākam manasi yādṛśam sauhārdam āsīt
bhū-tala-vṛtti-abhāva-pratiyogī ghaṭaḥ iti bodhaḥ jāyate
bhojana-virāma-samaye benjhiyonaḥ punarapi ḍeviḍam apṛcchat mitra kṛpayā vadatu
yadi nahi tarhi tad-icchā-viruddhaṃ sainikānāṃ yuddha-agnau nipātanaṃ
yātrā-pathe sarve jala-pātrasya su-rakṣā-viṣaye cintā-āturāḥ āsan viśeṣataḥ kṛṣṇadevaḥ
pitrā tu uktam hanta striyaḥ api kiyatya na-dūra-darśanā bhavanti
mahīm eka-ātapatra-aṅkām
na-iṣṭa-kartuḥ svabhāvaḥ
sthūlaḥ api hetuḥ kara-tāla-nādaḥ
atha prasthāna-samaya āpṛcchamānasya tathā ca abhinandana-grantham punaḥ yācamānasya rāmadayālo karayo kauśeya-vastra-nibaddhām abhinandana-granthasya pratim samarpayan āha samaya na asti
ṛṇa-śodhana-arthaṃ tasmin patre nirdiṣṭam āsīt
pādaḥ pāyāt upa-indrasya sarva-loka-utsavaḥ saḥ vaḥ
tena śrutam mātā pitaram kathayati sma śrṛṇotu vadhūḥ sva-pitṛ-gṛhe vartate
sarva-antaḥkaraṇa-dharma-upalakṣaṇa-artham icchā-ādi-grahaṇam
samāsa-ghaṭaka-citra-rājan-ādi-padānām tu sva-sva-arthe saṃketitānām vācakatvena klṛptānām lakṣaṇā-kalpanam
sama-māṃsa-pramāṇaḥ tu sama-saṃhananaḥ naraḥ
nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ ityatra prathamā-anta-arthasya nīlasya
nisargataḥ rajo-guṇa-sampannasya viśvāmitrasya mahatā pariśrameṇa tapaścaritvā sattva-guṇa-ādhikyena brahman-ṛṣi-tva-prāptiḥ api purāṇeṣu varṇitā vidyate
tad-pūrva-dine mātaram apṛcchat benjhiyonaḥ gamanaṃ nirṇītam eva
na ca etad-pakṣe sarveṣām śabdānām sarva-artha-vācaka tvam naastiiti śaṅkanīyam
praśna-patra-nirdeśa-anusāram uttara-pustikāyāṃ mitrāya patraṃ lekhanīyam āsīt
tasmai dharma-vṛdhdi-arthaṃ svakīyam na-mogham āśīrvādam api dattavān iti
api tu viruddha-vibhakti-rāhityam eva
tad-vacasā preritaḥ bhū-paḥ puro-hitam ākārya tatsarvam akathayat graha-śānti-upāyaṃ ca apṛcchat
tatratyai paṇḍita-prakāṇḍaiḥ api uktam kṣayāhe bhūri-bhojanād eva pitṛ-pitāmaha-ādīnām ṛṇaiḥ mucyase
yuktam bhoḥ nara-pati-dharmam āsthitena
nalaḥ latā-gṛha-antaritaḥ bhūtvā ātma-dhṛta-vastraṃ śarīrātavasṛjya pakṣiṣu prakṣipati
snāna-pāna-avagāheṣu śasyate tadyathā amṛtam
hārīta-roma-harṣaṇa-ādayaḥ ṛṣayaḥ sa-patnīkāḥ tatra vasanti sma
mālā-kāra-patnī prāha anna-dātaḥ eṣā ajā nirīhā nāsti
yadi sva-cakra-uddhata-reṇu-durdinaṃ rathaṃ samāsthāya gatā bṛhannalā
trividhāḥ puruṣā rājan uttama-adhama-madhyamāḥ
sa prastara-prahāreṇa tālakam udghāṭitavān kakṣam vilokya āścarya-cakita sañjāta yat tatra anekā kāṣṭha-mañjūṣā su-sam-sthāpitā santi
dhīrā api sthira-mati sneha-nirjhara-samplutā damayantī iva para-damana-śīlā kṣamā-tala-āgatā sura-sundarī iva kamanīyā kṛṣī-valasya kṣetra-ādi-kāryeṣu mudā prayasyantī sukham āsta
prayāti saukhyam para-kānta-saṅgāt
īśvara-sthāna-āpanna-ghaṭa-pada-suhṛtvam nīla-padasya abhedena tad-artha-anvayi tvam
śrīmān saṃyuga-candanena rudhireṇa ārdrā-anulipta-cchaviḥ
a-rūkṣāḥ rasāḥ pravardhante amla-lavaṇa-madhurāḥ yathā-kramaṃ tatra balam upacīyate nṛṇām iti
sa ca na-ādiḥ vṛddha-vyavahāra-apara-paryāya-asmad-ādi-samayāt niścīyate
pakva-vaṭikām ca tābhyām jala-pāna-artham adadām
ayam tu ātmā na-indriya-gocaratvāt na-cintyaḥ
avidyā-adhyāropita-sarva-padārtha-ākāraiḥ eva viśiṣṭatayā dṛśyamānatvāt iti
e e rāma adya me muṣṭi-piṣṭa-gātra-galita-rudhira-paṭala-majjaḥ jīvitam ujjhasi
saṃyukta-viśeṣyaka-jñāna-prakāra-bhūtam dhūmatvam cakṣuṣ-indriya-vyavahita-dhūmayoḥ sambandhaḥ
madhye-mārgam na kevalam bhāratīya-yuva-rājasya
śreṣṭhī nijagāda sapta-aha-dvaye tu prabhūtam vyavasāyam kartum śakyate mayā
api tu caṇḍikā-rūpa-dharaḥ eva kaścana dhūrtaḥ iti niścitya tāṃ balāt nigṛhya tasyāḥ dur-gatiṃ kartuṃ pravṛttaḥ
kāla-krameṇa tava aśva-hṛdaya-vidyāṃ tasmai datvā
śrutaṃ mayā dṛḍham a-kalya-śarīraḥ mahat-rājaḥ iti
sā niśā avidyā-rūpatvāt parama-artha-tattvam paśyataḥ muneḥ
mārge tasya taila-kāra-gṛham api āgata
yasya samājasya sevāyām tayā samagram eva jīvanam nir-lobha-vṛtti-pūrvakam vyatītam
yasya evam tattva-vidaḥ sarva-kārya-karaṇa-ceṣṭāsu karmasu akarma eva
na-anta-vijayaṃ rājā kunti-putra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
klṛpta-sambandha-bhāvasya mukhya-artha-sambandhasya lakṣya-upasthiti-prayojaka tayā
bhāvanā-viśeṣya-virahāt na-anvitā eva saṃkhyā
kokila-rūpa-arthasya pika-pade eva śaktim jānataḥ kokila-pade tām na-jānataḥ puṃsaḥ kokila-darśane sati ayam kokilaḥ iti anuvyavasāya-āpattiḥ
tīkṣṇaūṣṇakaṭurūkṣāṇi kapha-vāta-harāṇi ca
tātparya-jñāna-kārya-tā-avacchedake bādha-jñāna-pratibadhya-tā-avacchedake ca vyañjanā-vṛtti-na-janya-tva-niveśa-gauravam tu phala-mukha tvāt na doṣaḥ
viṭ-pitta-kapha-vātānām āgatānāṃ yathā-kramam
kim karma kim ca akarma iti kavayaḥ medhāvinaḥ api atra asmin karman-ādi-viṣaye mohitāḥ moham gatāḥ
te puṇyam āsādya sura-indra-lokam
na ca vācya-vācaka-bhāva-ākhyasya pada-arthā ntarasya śaktitvam svīkurvatām mate tathā saṃbhaveapi
yadā asau sthavirā nija-gṛha-abhyantaram ālokata
jaṅghā-ūru-sadanaṃ tandrā staimityaṃ pīnasa-āgamaḥ
na hi sarvatra lakṣaṇā-sthale vācya-artha-anvaya-na-upapattiḥ asti
prāṇa-rakṣā-artham āpatti-kāle yat kiñcit kriyate saḥ eva dharmaḥ tadā
saṃśuṣka-retaḥ-rudhirāḥ niṣpīta-kapha-medasaḥ
kathañcit gardabha-avatīrṇaḥ saḥ pānthaḥ bhūmau āstaraṇam āstīrya gardabham avasthāpya tad-deha-cchāyāyām aśeta
hari-kara-dhṛta-madhyam śatru-saṅgha-eka-kālaḥ
saḥ sva-jyeṣṭha-bhrātrā saha nivasati
gramāḥ kaverajā-tīre paṇḍita-grāma-maṇḍitaḥ
tasmāt tātparya-jñānāt pūrvam pada-artha-upasthitiḥ apekṣitā
pratyākhyāne ca dāne ca sukha-duḥkhe priya-na-priye
su-saṃvṛta-aṅgaḥ su-abhyaktaḥ snehaiḥ anila-nāśanaiḥ
na madya-dyūta-veśyā-prasaṅga-ruciḥ syāt
cikitsakān kathayāmi auṣadham tu bhakṣayitum śaknomi parama etat vāṣpan-kriyā-kalāpam tu karttum na śaknomi
vidyate hi diṣṭyā paryāptam dhanam etayo savidhe asmat-poṣaṇa-artham iti sa-niścayam procyāgre ca sapadi saṃplutya uccai sthavira-kṛṣī-valasya aṅke sukham upāviśat
tatrāpi ayaṃ dvādaśa-varṣa-deśīyaḥ bālakaḥ
yonasaḥ pāda-cāreṇa vāyu-vihāra-arthaṃ gamana-samaye madhye madhye elisaram api nayati sma
loke na-ātman-vit api śrotriyaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ ucyate nirahaṃkāraḥ ayam brāhmaṇaḥ iti
arjunasya bala-vīrya-jñāḥ bahavaḥ santi
sarvatra sarva-deha-avayavatvena gamyamānāḥ pāṇi-pāda-ādayaḥ jñeya-śakti-sadbhāva-nimitta-svakāryāḥ iti jñeya-sadbhāve liṅgāni jñeyasya iti upacārataḥ ucyante
cintā-apa-gamena laghūkṛtacittaḥ cūḍāmaṇimiśra sasmitam avocat bhavatu evam api
dadhīci-mahat-ṛrṣiḥ sa-ādaram anamat
jana-sauvidhya-artham apasāritavān
sādṛśya-viśiṣṭa-anuyogikaḥ śakya-sambandhaḥ gauṇī vṛttiḥ
pitta-śleṣma-karaṃ bhavyaṃ grāhi vaktra-viśodhanam
divaḥ cyutām sura-sundarī-sahodarīm iva vā kāñcana kṛśa-udarīm kiśorīm mukha-mālinyena manasaḥ viṣamām daśām prakaṭayantīm vilokya citrita-cetā na kimapi niścetum apārayam
kim te na viduḥ mama prabhavam prabhāvam prabhu-śakti-atiśayam
malina-jala-pānena kim ete rugṇāḥ na bhaviṣyanti
dharma-sneha-antare nyastā buddhiḥ dolāyate mama
rājñaḥ anumatyā tasya bhū-khaṇḍasya mārjana-śodhana-ādi-kāryaṃ prārabdham abhūt
anyaḥ avadat astu sādhu-mahāśaya-sam-akṣam pradattam śulka-patram tu tvam na-dharmād gopayasi
mahat-udayaḥ tasya skandhe nija-hastaṃ sthāpayitvā avadan mohana mama kevalaṃ āśā na asti api tu viśvāsaḥ api asti yat tvam atra api tathā eva parapiśrameṇa kāryam kariṣyasi yathā eva tvam nija-adhyayana-kāle akaroḥ
prātipadika-artha-viśeṣyatayā karmatva-ādau vivakṣitaḥ eva dvitīya-ādīnām anuśāsana-sidva tvāt
śrīḥ yasya abhi-ratā niyoga-sumukhī śrī-vakṣa-śayyā-gṛhe
kaviḥ tu rahasyam pari-rakṣan iva tatkāla-sphurita-matiḥ pratyāha ām śrūyatām śrīman
api tu tat-sadṛśābhyām anyābhyām api dvābhyāṃ vidvadbhyāṃ tāvatā śabda-koṣa-viṣaye abhimataṃ likhitam āsīt
śrotra-rasāyanaiḥ mama hṛdaya-ātura-auṣadhaiḥ teṣāṃ nāmadheyaiḥeva śrāvaya
kasya deśa-kāla-ādi-apekṣayā dṛṣṭa-adṛṣṭa-arthānām karmaṇām
na-vivekinām hi ajñāna-kāle bālānām dṛśyate dīrghaḥ aham gauraḥ aham iti deha-ādi-saṃghāte aham-pratyayaḥ
atha na-vilambena rājan-kumārī-samīpaṃ gacchāmi
iha hi pradarśite punaḥ śāstra-viṣaya-vibhāge upariṣṭāt jñāna-yogena sāṃkhyānām karman-yogena yoginām iti niṣṭhā-dvaya-viṣayam śāstram sukham pravartiṣyate
itaḥ mahat-ātmā śreṣṭhinaḥ putrāṇāṃ saṃkhyāṃ dhana-rāśi-saṃkhyāṃ ca mukhya-lipikāt jñātavān
garbhiṇī-vṛddha-bālānāṃ naati upadrava-pīḍitam
bhūmau nipatya vadana-udara-darśanam ca
te nṛtya-gāyana-ādi keṣu magnāḥ abhavan
mātṛ-svasā sva-svasṛ-putram aṅke samupāveśya tat śirasi hastam prasārya prāvocat prāha ca tvayā bhojanam kṛtam navā putra prāhaaham tu miṣṭānnam khāditvā samāgataḥ asmi
vāta-pitta-adhikaḥ rātrauuṣṇe caapi pibetnaraḥ
pūrva-mīmāṃsā-sūtra-kāraḥ api arthasya tad-nimitta tvāt
tat-na-karaṇe ca doṣa-saṃkīrtanam kṛtam
vāda-niyama-anusāreṇa parājitaḥ vijitavataḥ adhīnaḥ
śūla-pravāhikā-ṭopa-kapha-vāta-arśasāṃ hitaḥ
ghakāra-ādi-śakti-na-prasiddhyā tad-upasthiteḥ abhāvāt
bāṇa-puṅkhā-akṣaraiḥ vākyaiḥ jyā-jihvā-parivartibhiḥ
caitra ekamānayati maitraḥcaaparāmityatra ghaṭatva-paṭatva-ādinā eva ānayana-karma-tva-anvaya-bodhaḥ
manasi eva pra-jvalantam praṇaya-vedanā-pāvakam sahamānena vivaśatā-paravaśena hasta-upagatām api hāpitam hata-vidhinā na-mūlyam ratnam
sama-vibhakta-aṅgaḥ
vidyā-gaṃdha-vihīnaḥ vitta-śūnyaḥ ca
iyam tvadīyā sakhī api asmin eva kanyā-vinimaya-kurīti-kalpe nipatitā viṣīdati iti tu su-viditam eva bhavatyā
sopi ca sva-divya-medhayā na ati-ciram eva sarvāṇi śāstrāṇi vedān ca adhi-cakāra
vi-smṛta-sva-rājya-sukham prayāti
caitraḥ pacati bhavati ityatra tu bhavati-artha-anvitāyāḥ pāka-anvita-ākhyāta-artha-kṛteḥ prathamā-anta-arthe anvayaḥ
vrīḍā-śaṅkita-mānasa sopi na nisarati gṛhāt
mamatā amitā ca samāna-vaya-ske
gauḥbāhīkaḥ iti gauṇī-sthale api bāhīkasya śakyatā-avacchedaka-gotvena eva bodhaḥ
śīta-uṣṇa-ādīn sahataḥ kim syāt iti śṛṇu
katham punaḥ ucyate asau mama ātmā iti vibhajya deha-ādi-saṅghātam tasmin ahaṃkāram adhyāropya loka-buddhim anusaran vyapadiśati mama ātmā iti
nityānām ca karmaṇām puṇya-phalatva-śruteḥ
tat idānīm durdaivāt ugravādinām pārthakya-patha-unmādinām loka-jīvana-udbādhakānām dik-bhrāntānām yuvakānām śaraṇa-sthalam samajāyata
nṛ-pa-āśrayaḥ kaṣṭasahatva-dīkṣā
ahaṃ dāṇiṃ visamārambhaṃ parassa uvaṇṇāsaṃ parakkameṇa samīkaromi tti bhaṇia bhaṭṭā paviṭṭho evva taṃ parabalaṃ tataḥ nāma-gotra-grahaṇena samāśvāsya kula-putra-janaṃ sarvathā pradyota-pra-yogaḥ eṣaḥ
kuru-pāṇḍava-gāthā
bahu mānyate khalu tāvat balavat-jana-durlabhaḥ anunayaḥ
śuṣkāṇi kapha-vāta-ghnāni etānieṣāṃ phalāni ca
etat-upari katipaya-kṣaṇa-paryantam sarve vayam ahasāma
evam vadatā rājñā yadā mauna-bhaṅgaḥ kṛtaḥ tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ tataḥ na-dṛśyaḥ bhūtvā punaśca vṛkṣe lambamānaḥ sthitavān
para-āghātanam anna-aśraddhā-jananānām
vayam etā balāt anu-dhāvya grahīṣyāma ghoṣitam rakṣi-nivāsa-adhikāriṇā
caitra-ādi-pada-uttara-prathamāyāḥ eva caitra-ādiḥ arthaḥ
teṣāmayamabhisandhiḥ gabhīrāyām nadyām ghoṣaḥ ityatra gabhīra-nadī-tīra-vṛttiḥ ghoṣaḥ iti śābda-bodhaḥ anubhūyate
na-yācita-vastubhiḥ eva svīyaṃ jīvanaṃ yāpayati sma
cira-uparodha-samprāptaḥ
tena dhanārthinā mahatā kāyakleśena bhagavān-candra-ardhacūḍāmaṇiḥ ciramārādhitaḥ
aham api asmādṛśa-jana-yogyam kañcit brāhmaṇam anviṣyāmi
teṣām snāna-sādhāraṇyena saṃbhoga-pratibaddha-tva-abhāvena anaikāntikatvāt
rāmalālena tasya patnyā ca yathā upapādita-vastunā deśa-ja-upacāreṇa tasyā bahu-saṃrakṣaṇam kṛtam
saṃjñā-dvaya-samāveśaḥ na ā-kaḍārāt ekā saṃjñā itianuśāsanāt
sa caarthaḥ prakaraṇaiḥvibhāvyamānaḥ bhūyaḥ eva śarīra-vṛtti-hetu-vyādhi-karma-kārya-kāla-kartṛ-karaṇa-vidhi-viniścayāt daśa-prakaraṇaḥ
sarva-saṅkalpa-saṃnyāsī iti vacanāt sarvān ca kāmān sarvāṇi ca karmāṇi saṃnyasyet ityarthaḥ
sarvā-atiśaya-śobhā-ādi kaṃ śrīḥ
taṃ sva-artha-siddhau nirataṃ kadaryaṃ
rāmarudra-bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ ramaṇīya-vyākhyā tṛtīyā-vicāra-upakrama-paryantā mudritā labhyate
candanaṃ durgandha-hara-dāha-nirvāpaṇa-lepanānāṃ
ataḥ ekāgra-buddhyā śabda-koṣa-nirmāṇe manaḥ pravartayituṃ na śaknomi iti benyahūdaḥ uktavān
akarmaṇi ca karman-abhāve kartṛ-tantratvāt pravṛtti-nivṛttyoḥ vastu na-prāpya eva hi sarvaḥ eva kriyā-kāraka-ādi-vyavahāraḥ avidyā-bhūmau eva karma yaḥ paśyet paśyati
vyakti-viśeṣa-bodhe vā lakṣaṇāiti vyavahāraḥ iti nirūpitavatā grantha-kṛtā kamalāni kamalāni ityatra kamala-padasya saurabha-viśiṣṭa-kamala-vyakti-viśeṣe lakṣaṇā svīkṛtā
śṛṇu māṃsa-pradoṣa-jān
ataḥca yathā-yogam kriyā-pada-adhyāhāraḥ
krimi-vāta-ātapa-hataṃ śuṣkaṃ jīrṇam an-ārtavam
prāghuṇikeṣu ca eka drāktara sivilasarjana-upādhi-dhārī sa-prārthanam samāhūta bālakasya roga-nidāna-artham sa-yantra datta-citta samajāyata
na ca evam karman-vidhi-śruteḥ na-prāmāṇyam
andhasya kim hasta-tala-sthitaḥ api prakāśayatiarthamiha pradīpaḥ
kula-ādi kam sa-vinayam āvedya saḥ api ante gaja-anyā-uktim nikṣipati
bhārata-rāṣṭrapati-sammānitaḥ
taila-vyāpadi śastā syāt takra-piṇyāka-sādhitā
punaḥ ca antime āyuṣi vartamānasya me mahat-yātrā-avasare sāṃsārika-vastūnāṃ parigrahaḥ bhāra-bhūtaḥ eva bhavet
kimuta yajña-dāna-tapāṃsi nityāni iti
sītā iyam jala-sambhava-ālaya-ratā viṣṇuḥ bhavān gṛhyatām
bahu-rūpa-ākāra-vicitre asmin
guṇa-vācaka-gabhīra-pada-artha-gāmbhīryasya tu tīre nadī-dvārakaḥ paramparā-sambandhaḥ
sā punaḥ ambikāṃ sarva-guṇa-sampannāṃ putraṃ yācitavatī
vara-mālā-saṅgrathana-anantaraṃ mām āhvaya
vṛddha-dhenu-dānena pāpa-yuktaḥ bhavati
janāḥ caurān nigṛhya rājña samīpam ānayan rājā caurān apṛcchat vadata nikṛṣṭa-caurya-kāryasya kṛte kīdṛśam daṇḍam icchatha caurā prāvocanrājan yathā bhavān icchati tathā daṇḍayatu param patnī-dvayasya daṇḍam mā prayacchatu
te sarve śāsakīyāḥ ārakṣakāḥ iti teṣāṃ sama-vastra-darśanena eva jñāyate sma
pāka-ādi-kāryāṇi tu benyahūdasya mātā phegā karoti sma
benyahūdastu svīye kārye eva magnaḥ bhavati sma ityataḥ bālānāṃ yoga-kṣema-draṣṭā kopi na āsīt
vaktavya-bāhulyāt gahanam sphoṭa-vādam vihāyaanye dārśanikānām niruktāḥ siddhānta-bhedāḥ sva-mati-śodhanam paramam prayojanamabhisandhāya pakṣa-antara-na-karaṇa-pūrvakam vivecitāḥ śābda-taraṅgiṇyām
nalaḥ bāḍham astu adhvaryuṃ svasti-vācana-arthaṃ kimāhvayāmaḥ
tatca sarvatra naapekṣitam abheda-saṃbandha-svīkārāt ityapiuktam
tri-vidhaḥ tri-prakāraḥ tāmasa-ādi-prakāraiḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ śāstreṣu samyak kathitaḥ yasmāt tāmasa-ādi-bhedena tyāga-saṃnyāsa-śabda-vācyaḥ arthaḥ adhikṛtasya karmiṇaḥ na-ātman-jñasya tri-vidhaḥ saṃbhavati
tathā ca taṇḍula-abhinna-āśrayaka-viklṛpti-anukūlaḥ eka-caitra-na-bhinna-āśrayakaḥ vartamānaḥ vyāpāraḥ iti tad-vākya-adhīnaḥ bodhaḥ
vṛtti-viṣayasya śabda-bodhya tve śakya-pratiyogika-anvaya tvasya niyāmakatā-svīkārāt
ataḥaham bravīmi aṅga-aṅgi-bhāvam na-jñātvā ityādi
tatra yathā vṛddha-vyavahāreṇa padānām vākya-artha-bodhe hetutā svīkriyatee
rājā yuvakaṃ pradhāna-mantri-rūpe kiṃ niyuktavān
evam uktavati rājñi haṭha-sam-ārūḍhā sā rājñī sarvathā eva prāṇān hātum udyatā babhūva
bahūnām janmanām jñāna-artha-saṃskāra-āśrayāṇām ante samāptau jñānavān prāpta-paripāka-jñānaḥ mām vāsudevam pratyak-ātmānam pratyakṣataḥ prapadyate
upodikā tila-kalka-siddhā hetuḥatīsārasya
tata mahat-rāja-iṅgitena samīpa-stha ekaḥ rājan-karmacārī kathayati mohanadevam śreṣṭhin tvam kūṭa-tulā-mānena vikrīṇīsi iti janaśruti karṇa-ākarṇi kayā śrīmatām śravaṇa-gocarībhūtā iti tvam āhūta
āḥ udaka-snāna-saṅkīrtanena tatrabhavatīṃ cintayatā sā svapne dṛṣṭā bhavet
kāṣṭha-vikretā harṣita sva-sva-gṛham āgacchat hemā netre paridhāya cītkṛtya provāca
sama-duḥkha-sukham dhīraṃ saḥ amṛtatvāya kalpate
mayā catur-daśa-vidyāḥ pāṭhitāḥ kila
kadācana ca vinoda-kheda-ādīnām saṃcārin-bhāvānām anubhavaḥ me bhavati sma sarvam idam smarata
adhi-śīṅ-sthā-āsām karma iti sūtra-artha-nirūpaṇa-prasaṅge
mitra-patnī-vacanāni śrutvā siṃha kruddhaḥ san provāca kṣaṇa-mātram api aham atra na sthāsyāmi
mayā nir-dhanena sākam īdṛśaḥ viśvāsa-ghāta-pūrṇaḥ jaghanyaḥ vyavahāraḥ na ucitaḥ
tasyāḥ krīḍāyāḥ samaya-anusāraṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ araṇya-vāsaḥ na-jñāta-vāsaḥ ca kṛtaḥ
parantu tad-mate khaṇḍa-vākya-artha-bodhe eva padānām hetutā
prāṇa-ccheda-karāḥ rājñā hantavyāḥ bhūtimicchatā
manaḥ manaḥ-arthaḥ buddhiḥ ātmā ca iti adhi-ātma-dravya-guṇa-saṃgrahaḥ śubha-aśubha-pravṛtti-nivṛtti-hetuḥ ca
ṣa tri-loka-adhipatiḥ bhavitum arhasi
caitraḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmodanam pacati ityatra dhātu-arthaḥ tad-tad-vibhakti-artha-bhāvanayoḥ saṃsargeṣu ghaṭakatayā viśeṣaṇatayā ca bhāsate
tataḥ bhartrā prathamaṃ kunta-pra-hāra-janita-mohaḥ śālaṅkāyanaḥ nāma pradyotasyaamātyaḥ mā khalu mā khalu sāhasamiti bhaṇitvā taṃ deśamupasthitaḥ
nirukta-vṛtti tvam upasthiti-niṣṭha-śābda-bodha-hetu-tva-ghaṭitam
kaḥ hi saṃ-nihita-śārdūlām guhām dharṣayitum śaktaḥ
saḥ nitya-ātma-svarūpa-darśana-niṣṭhaḥ dvandva-sahiṣṇuḥ amṛtatvāya amṛta-bhāvāya mokṣāya iti arthaḥ kalpate samarthaḥ bhavati
ekaḥ tat-kathā-vaiśiṣṭayam vivṛṇvan āha aho vastu-yojanā na-sakṛt paṭhanāt api tṛptiḥ naiva jāyate
ākāśa-dundubhi-ravaiḥ sa-mahī-prakampaiḥ
tasya ca puras-varti-deśe vahni-saṃsṛṣṭa-tva-jñānam anumiti-rūpam astieva
sa-ākāṅkṣaiḥ sa-arthaka-śabdaiḥ anumiti-vilakṣaṇā śābda-pramitiḥ jāyate iti vyavasthāpya
yukta-na-yukta-vivekā abhijñā ca abhūt
dillī nagare prātaḥ tu vajra-cūrṇa-nirmitāni upari upari bhavanāni
visargaḥ visarjanam devatā-uddeśena caru-puroḍāśa-ādeḥ dravyasya parityāgaḥ
kintu dhūma-na-saṃsarga-na-grahaṇam eva
abhedasya āśrayatā-saṃbandhena dhana-pada-arthe anvayaḥ
vidhāna-sabhā-adhyakṣeṇa samācāra-patra-sampādakaṃ kiṃ kartum ādiṣṭavān
tādṛśa-śakti-grāhakam śabda-arthayoḥ tādātmyam
evam prātipadika-artha-vyatiriktaḥ sup-artha-liṅga-saṃkhyā-vyatiriktaḥ ca sarvaḥapi
asmān sarvān ādāya rākeśa sṭeśanasya nirāmiṣa-āhāra-gṛhe prāviśat
eṣā hi vayasaḥ darpāt kula-putra-avamāninī
yatantaḥ api śāstra-ādi-pramāṇaiḥ
vyāyāmanityaḥ jīrṇa-āśa yava-godhūma-bhojanaḥ
yeṣāṃ madhya-balāḥ rogāḥ kapha-pitta-samutthitāḥ
āmalaka-tiṃtriṇī-jaṃbīra-āmra-śalāṭhubhiḥ siddhān upadaṃśān api vikreṣyati
mayā mama yaḥ paraḥ bhāvaḥ tena tatam vyāptam sarvam idam jagat na-vyakta-mūrtinā na vyaktā mūrtiḥ svarūpam yasya mama saḥ aham na-vyakta-mūrtiḥ tena mayā na-vyakta-mūrtinā
mīnasya udare sthitam tam musala-bhāgam sva-bāṇa-agre niyojitavān ca
śārṅgaḥ asmi viṣṇu-kara-lagna-suvṛtta-madhyaḥ
tadā svakīya-dakṣiṇa-bāhum dadātu bhavān
asau kapotaḥ ekasya madhura-peya-vikretuḥ āpaṇasya uparitane bhāge ekaḥ vijñāpana-paṭṭaḥ saṃsaktaḥ āsīt
tasyāḥ śābda-bodha-aupayika-tva-abhāvāt
tataḥ śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṇavā-ānaka-gomukhāḥ
āgantuḥhi vyathāpūrvaṃ samutpannaḥ jaghanyaṃ vāta-pitta-śleṣmaṇāṃ vaiṣamyamāpādayati
evam ātaṅka-śaṅkā-udbhāvita-bhaya-artānām prāya sameṣām tādṛkṣāṇām viśiṣṭa-puruṣāṇām surakṣā-artham praśāsanena ārakṣiṇa niyojitā
ekaikaḥapi hieṣām āśraya-ādīnāṃ bhāvānāṃ viśeṣānāśrayate viśeṣa-a-parisaṃkhyeyatvāt
guṇānām lakṣyamāṇatva-kathanam lakṣyatā-avacchedaka-tva-abhiprāyakam vṛttau sva-avacchinna-anuyogitāka-tva-rūpa-yoga-viśeṣa-paricayāya eva
pṛṣṭa kim ayam eva mohanadeva śreṣṭhī samupasthitaḥ ayam mahat-rāja-ājñayā iti uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva sa
tad-vārtā-śravaṇa-samanantaram eva saḥ patnīm avadat priye itaḥparaṃ vilambaḥ naiva kartavyaḥ
samāne gamane pradyotasya-ava-māna-viśeṣaḥ cintyate
evañca śakya-artha-pravāheṇa atyanta-sāmīpye gaṅgāyām tīra-dharmam ghoṣa-ādhāra tvamāropya gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti prayogaḥ
yadyapi ghana-śyāmaḥ iti-ādau ghana-śabdasya ghana-vṛtti-na-sādhāraṇa-dharme lakṣaṇā
evam saṃbandhatva-garbha-tādṛśa-saṃketa-prayojyāyāḥ tīra-ādi-upasthiteḥ śābda-bodha-anukūla tvamapi kalpanīyamiti gauravamiti cet
sañjāta-gabhīra-ghāta deveśa mahīm adhipatan proccaiḥ cakranda aye mama prāṇebhyaḥ api priyatarasakhe śerasiṃha
tri-māsa-anantaraṃ nivṛttaḥ aham imaṃ grahīṣyāmi evam uktvā tasmin gate
abhihitena pada-arthena karaṇena anvayaḥ pada-artha-saṃsarga-rūpa-anvaya-dhīḥ iti abhihita-anvaya-śabda-artha-ghaṭanā bodhyā
kṛtvā putra-viyoga-ārtām bahuśaḥ jananīm mama
evañca anyaārāt iti sūtre anya-śabdaḥ śabda-paraḥ eva na anya-arthaka-pada-paraḥ
dṛṣṭvā svairam avanti-rāja-tanayāṃ pañca-iṣavaḥ pātitāḥ
tri-catur-divasa-anantaram eva daiva-durvipākāt candramaule sā
navya-nyāya-granthānām pracāra-anantara-kāla ikeṣu vyākaraṇa-mīmāṃsā-nibandheṣu navya-naiyāyikānām śābda-bodha-vicāra-paddhatiḥ evaanusṛtā lakṣyate
idam godāvarī-nikuñjam bhīru-bhramaṇa-ayogyam siṃhavattvāt itianumānam
piḍakā-koṭha-kaṇḍūnāṃ saṃbhavaḥ a-ratiḥ eva ca
grāmasya jyeṣṭhāḥ grāma-tyāga-vicāram na aṅgīkṛtavantaḥ
draṣṭuṃ me tvarate buddhī rāvaṇa-anta-karaṃ gurum
duryodhanaḥ āryau vaikarṇa-varṣadevau ucyatām asti mama eka-daśa-akṣauhiṇī-bala-samudayaḥ
kanaka-racita-daṇḍām śaktim ullālayantam
anantaram tayoḥ malla-yuddha-artham sarvāḥ vyavasthāḥ kalpitavān śivadattaḥ
pratiśyāya-mukha-nāsā-akṣi-karṇa-roga-śirobhramāḥ
gabhīra-padasya tādṛśa-nadī-tīra-lakṣaka tve tasya viśeṣaṇa-pada-tva-abhāvena tad-uttara-saptamyā ādheyatā-arthaka-tā-na-sambhavāt
pitta-śleṣma-ghnam amlaṃ ca vāta-laṃ ca ākṣikī-phalam
saṃskṛta-kālejasya prācīna-paripāṭī-ghaṭitaḥ chātraḥ abhūvam
tadā ghaṭatvena dravyatva-prameyatva-ādeḥ anumātum śakyatvena anya-labhya tvāt ghaṭaḥ dravyam
svatva-saṃsargakam puruṣa-viśeṣyakam bodham rājan-puruṣaḥ iti samasta-padāt anubhavantaḥ navya-naiyāyikāḥ samāsa-sthale nāman-arthayoḥ api bheda-anvaya-vyutpattim svīkurvanti
asmat-rājye dīnānāṃ rājan-mātṛ-kṛpā-kaṭākṣā eva nanu śaraṇam
taṃ cintayāmi nṛ-patiṃ sura-loka-yātaṃ yenaayam ātma-ja-viśiṣṭa-guṇaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ
katipaya-dina-anantaraṃ saḥ sva-gṛhaṃ prasthitaḥ
vastutaḥtu pada-pada-arthayoḥ saṃketasya saṃbandhatāyāḥ vyavasthāpayiṣyamāṇatvena na smaraṇa-prayojaka-saṃbandha-na-upapatti-leśaḥ api
laghu-śuddha-ambaraḥ sthānaṃ bhajet a-kledi vārṣikam
duh-ādeḥ gauṇakam karma nī-vaha-ādeḥ pradhānakam
a-vaikārika-vikāraḥ caiti
nirukta-smṛti-gatam ca bhāva-padam dhātu-artha-param ityatra naasti pramāṇam
tatrāpi vāṅ-manasābhyām vihita-anuṣṭhāna-pakṣe kilbiṣa-prāpti-vacanam viruddham āpadyeta
puṣpa-sāra-niryāsa-yantram api te na dhārayanti sma
satyam apriya-anṛta-varjitam yathā-bhūta-artha-vacanam
niyatam saṅga-rahitam na-rāga-dveṣa taḥ kṛtam
madhu-madhuka-rudhira-mocarasa-mṛtkapāla-lodhra-gairika-priyaṅgu-śarkarā-lājāḥ iti daśaimāni śoṇitasthāpanāni bhavanti
yam tadā hasti-sambhrama-divase kautūhalena āgate svaḥ
tad-bodhaka-mṛga-padasya prātipadikatvāt tad-uttaram dvitīyā-āpattiḥ iti vācyam
ākṛti-adhikaraṇa-nyāyena jāteḥeva pada-artha tvāt tasyāḥca nityatvāt na śābda-anubhava-kāraṇa tve virodhaḥ
ananta-vīryaḥ kamala-āyata-akṣaḥ
ante kaṇṭha-āgata-prāṇena miśra-mahodayena ekadā rahasi kailāśam āhūya proktam kailāśa tvam me śiṣya
apitu go-mahiṣa-kukkura-ādayaḥ jalam pibanti sma
nāradaḥ mahiṣāsuraṃ prāpya na-sura-rāja malaya-parvate nārāyaṇī ati-loka-sundarī
pañca-dina-anantaram vraṇaḥ na paripūrṇa
sammukham ānītā bhojya-sāmagrī-paripūrṇā sthālī kenāpi na-dṛṣṭena hastena jhaṭiti aparsāyata iva anubhūyate
tadā lākṣaṇikasyaapi śaktimattvāt mukhya-jaghanya-vibhāgaḥ na ghaṭate iti liṅga-adhikaraṇa-virodhaḥ
paścāt pṛṣṭaḥ saḥ kathitavān yat vigata-catvāriṃśad-varṣebhyaḥ ahaṃ rāmāyaṇasya nityaṃ pārāyaṇaṃ kurvan asmi
karman-vidhi-śrutivat brahman-vidyā-vidhi-śruteḥ api na-prāmāṇya-prasaṅgaḥ iti cet
vayam api ca bhuja-āyudha-pradhānāḥ
tat-upodvalaka-yukti-jātam ca nirūpayantaḥ
lilī puṣpa-vikāsa-bhāji bhagavati gabhasti-mālini
na karṇa-rogāḥ vātotthā na manyā-hanu-saṃgrahaḥ
sva-pitāmahasya siṃhāsanam ānīya ayam bālaka pra-harṣita san sva-grāmam pratinivṛtta jyeṣṭha-bhrātā nanaḥ ca āścarya-cakita sva-grāma-vāsibhi saha tasya abhinandanam kṛtavān
eṣaḥ eva pāṇḍava-vaṃśa-uddhārakaḥ sañjātaḥ
tadā yoga-abhyāsa-janitena saṃskāreṇa hriyate
kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-pratibandhya-pratibandhaka-bhāva-lāghava-gaurava-vicāra-mukhena vibhakti-artha-saṃsargaka-bodham nirākṛtya
candanapura-rājyam rājasthānasya paścima-uttara-bhū-bhāge bālukābhi sama-ākīrṇam rārājyate
yuktāiyaṃ bhoḥ taskara-pra-vṛttiḥ
tābhyām prathame varṣe lakṣa-rūpya-ka-ātman-kaḥ lābhaḥ ca arjita
pāvanatva-ādi-viśeṣasya pratītiḥna syāt
sāhitya-saṅgīta-kalā-vihīnaḥ sākṣāt paśuḥ puccha-viṣāṇa-hīnaḥ
kintu vivāha-anantaram sarvakāra-sevā-prasaṃgena tasya dūra-gamanam yadi samāpatet tadā kaḥ tatra prabhu syāt mātā nir-uttarā asthāt
tad-sevana-kramam api jñāpitavān
graha-gaṇa-caritam vā vāyu-mārgam prayāsi
evañca mukhya-artha-sambandha-prayojya-pratīti-anukūla-vyāpāraḥ lakṣaṇāiti vākya-arthaḥ iti vācyam
tasyaadhamasyaantikam iti adhama-pada-sāhityāt tathātva-sambhavāt
eṣu kaḥ vā nala-rājan-kumāraḥ iti naeva jñāyate
ittham śakti-grāhaka-pramāṇa-mūrdhanyena vyavahāreṇa padānām itara-anvita-arthe śaktiḥ itara-anvita-artha-anubhava-janaka-tva-rūpā siddhyati
yaḥ evam yoga-saṃnyasta-karmā tam ātmavantam na-pramattam guṇa-ceṣṭā-rūpeṇa dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi na nibadhnanti aniṣṭa-ādi-rūpam phalam na ārabhante he dhanañjaya
caitra-kartṛka-pāka-pratiyogikaḥ caitra-niṣṭha-abhāvaḥ iti bodhaḥ
tataḥ moha-pratyāgatena bāṣpa-pari-ākulena mukhena bhartrā bhaṇitaṃ dṛṣṭāasi ghoṣavati sā khalu na dṛśyate iti
nāśaḥ nāma pūrvasmāt hīna-janma-prāptiḥ saḥ yoga-bhraṣṭasya na asti
he na-anta-rūpa antaḥ na vidyate tava rūpāṇām
a-yuktaṃ para-puruṣa-saṃkīrtanaṃ śrotum
tasmāt ātman-vidaḥ nivṛtta-mithyā-jñānasya viparyaya-jñāna-mūlaḥ karman-yogaḥ na saṃbhavati iti yuktam uktam syāt
rambhā prasādāt eva ca tvayā saha na-tarkitaḥ ayam saṃbhāṣaṇa-saṃgama-prasaṃga samupalabdha iti api ātmana saubhāgyam manye
mahat-ātmā kathitavān pārśva-stha-giri-nirjharataḥ gṛhītvā piba
saḥ śabalā-nāmikām dhenum āhūya avadat bhakṣya-bhojya-lehya-coṣya-ādi-sahitam ṣaṭ-rasa-upetam bhojanam sajjīkriyatām iti
māsamadhīte iti vākya-artha-rūpaṇe vyutpatti-vāda-uktasya sārartham varṇayanti
tat-patana-sama-kālam eva kūṣmāṇḍa-phalāni api patitāni
etat nimittaṃ bhāvini kāle samagraḥ deśaḥ eva ādhunika-yahūdya-sainyasya nirmātā iti
ye api anya-devatā-bhaktāḥ anyāsu devatāsu bhaktāḥ anya-devatā-bhaktāḥ santaḥ yajante pūjayanti śraddhayā āstikya-buddhyā anvitāḥ anugatāḥ
prakaraṇa-upasaṃhāra-artham vibhūti-saṃkṣepam āha na tat asti bhūtam cara-na-caram caram na-caram vā
tatra sarva-sukha-lābhaḥ bhavati iti
sarva evaastuvaḥtānca sarva-bhūta-hita-eṣiṇaḥ
laghutaram ca idam dhūma-śakaṭi-sthalam
anye buddhi-caitanya-vādinaḥ
viśiṣṭa-śaktimattva-pradarśanam viśeṣa-pratiṣedhaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham
tena ghoṭaka-yāna-stha vṛddha mṛtaḥ
paruṣita-mukha-rāgau spaṣṭa-daṣṭa-adharoṣṭhau
rāma-avatāra-samaye aham vṛkṣeṣu nilīya vālinam māritavān
vidhvasta-mīna-makarāt yamunā-hrada-antāt
na-dhīta-vyavahāra-aṅgam maulam khyātam vipaścitam
rājñā preṣitā kecit anye janā rājan-sūnuḥ vīrajaḥ ca tābhyām dampatibhyām saha kiyat dūram gatā nivartana-kāle vīraja sva-svasṛ-patim prāha ita sthānāt
kva padmaṃ rūpa-gandha-āḍhyaṃ
jala-plāva-santrastānāṃ prajānāṃ dukhāni nivāritāni
hetutva-jñāne hetutā-avacchedaka-jñānam kāraṇam
uṣasi pañcavādane vasiṣṭha-kuṇḍa-śliṣṭād rāma-mandirāt nirgacchatā stotra-dhvaninā me nidrā apagatā
na-avabuddhā na-upajā-śaṅkā preman-anurakta-hṛdayā budhanī campā-vacobhiḥ na durmanāyate sma
sarva-gatam api sat nityam sadā yajña-vidhi-pradhānatvāt yajñe pratiṣṭhitam
vara-puruṣa-viśeṣaṃ naicchati stūyamānam
kāma-deva-kule mām pratipālaya
sva-deśa-bhaktaḥ kīdṛśaṃ vyavahāraṃ karoti
na hi ātmanaḥ sva-ātmani pravartaka-pramāṇa-apekṣatā
na-samīkṣya-kāriṇī vartate sarvadā kalaha-priyā sā vaiparītyena pathā pracalati
moha-viṣṭa-manas kā strī kimapi na-kāryam karoti
bhavantau parasparam militvā sva-guṇa-ava-guṇa-sambandhe nirṇayam kurutām
param parama-kārpaṇya-sūcakai sakalaiḥ api ebhiḥ upāyai gṛha-sadasyānām bāhulyena saṃvardhana-sātatyena ca gārhasthya-vyayaḥ na kām api nyūnatām āpa
nyāya-siddhānte vaiyākaraṇa-mīmāṃsaka-ādibhiḥ udīrita-avadyānām dūrīkaraṇe
aye etāni bhagavat-āyudha-varāṇi
mārga-āyāsa-parihāra-artham tām kathām śraddhayā śrṛṇotu tāvat
paṭola-tāḍaka-patra-āsavau dvau bhavataḥ
śrīmān imām kanaka-citrita-harmya-mālām
mukhya-artha-pravāhasya ghoṣa-anvaya-bādhaḥ taṭasya mukhya-artha-pravāha-saṃbandhaḥ gaṅgā-gata-śaitya-pāvanatva-ādi-viśeṣa-pratipādanam prayojanam caiti tritayam hetuḥ
dvija-vara rucitam te tṛpta-vatsa-anuyātram
pada-artha-mātra-avagāhi ca jñānam ajñāna-viṣaya-tva-abhāvāt na anubhava-rūpam
śakti-grāhaka-pramāṇa-mūrdhanyena vyavahāreṇa kārya-anvite evaarthe padānām śakteḥeva dhāraṇāt upajīvya-virodhena kārya-aṃśasya na-tyāgāt kārya-anvita-artha-viṣayakaḥ eva sarvatra vākya-artha-bodhaḥ
viparīta-guṇaiḥ deśa-mātrā-kāla-upapāditaiḥ
tat-matena parvatam vivṛtya sarit-salilasya grāma-ānayana-prayāsaḥ vyoman-talāt tārā-ānayana-prayāsa iva abhūt
bhāva-pradhāna-nirdeśa-sthale ghaṭatva-prakāraka-ghaṭatva-bodhaḥ lakṣaṇayā
anyedyuḥ yadā tau nyāyālaye punaḥ upasthāya sva-sva-pakṣaṃ prastutaḥ
kṣayāt kṣaraṇāt kṣetravat vā asmin karman-phala-niṣpatteḥ kṣetram iti iti-śabdaḥ evamśabdapadaarthakaḥ kṣetram iti evam abhidhīyate kathyate
vidārigandhā vṛṣya-sarva-doṣa-harāṇāṃ
vibhakti-artha-prakāra-boda-samarthanena prātipadika-artha-pratyaya-arthayoḥ bheda-anvaya-bodham dṛḍhīcakruḥ
kintu bhikṣuke kopa-pra-darśanam na-ucitaṃ matvā saḥ taṃ visasarja
ariṣṭānca anupāna-arthe medaḥ-māṃsa-kapha-apahān
nṛpaḥ tat-kṣaṇam eva svam aśvam āmra-vṛkṣa-abhimukha kam akarot
jambu-āmra-asthi-dadhittha-amla-bilvaiḥ sāṅgrāhikī matā
rāvaṇasya senā-patayaḥ bahavaḥ rākṣasāḥ raṇa-bhūmau prāṇān tyaktvā yama-pura-atithayaḥ abhavan
madhuraṃ sa-kaṣāyaṃ ca śītaṃ pitta-kapha-apaham
kathayantaḥ ca jñāna-bala-vīrya-ādi-dharmaiḥ viśiṣṭam mām
vicchinna-hāra-patita-aṅgada-lambasūtram
sva-ujjala-yaśasā maṇḍita-sakala-bhūmaṇḍalam parama-pratāpinaṃ
eka-artha-abhāva-pakṣe tu na-luk-samāse api śaktiḥevaiti nyāya-siddha-artha-anuvādakam eva tat vārtikamiti lāghavam
vikrama-arjita-rājyasya svayameva mṛgendratā
jana-hita-kartā agastyaḥ
hastinā-pura-pratyāgamanam
tatśrutvā marīci-vacaḥ kāpyaḥ uvāca somaḥ eva śarīre śleṣma-antargataḥ kupita-a-kupitaḥ śubha-a-śubhāni karoti
palāni dṛṣṭvā darbheṣu sva-hasta-racitāni naḥ
kaṭu-amla-lavaṇa-ati-uṣṇa-tīkṣṇa-rūkṣa-vidāhinaḥ ityatra ati-śabdaḥ kaṭu-ādiṣu sarvatra yojyaḥ
saubhāgyāt tadā su-yogya-kanyāyāḥ anveṣaṇe āsīt agastya-muniḥ narakāt pitṛ-puruṣāṇāṃ rakṣa-arthaṃ tena putra-lābhaḥ karaṇīyaḥ
śakyatayā prasiddha-itara-artha-bodham nimittīkṛtya gaṅgā-ādi-pade lākṣaṇikatva-vyavahāram ca nirvahanti
dharma-adharme-ādi-pratibaddha-jñāna-śaktitvāt
ekā ajā putra-janman-anantaram mṛtā
tathāpi śaśa-śrṛṅga-ādi-pada-janya-pada-artha-upasthiti-mūlakaḥ śaśe śṛṅga-abhāvaḥ iti-ākārakaḥ mānasa-bodhaḥ jāyate
tadā abhirāmaḥ uktavān vāṇijyam sadā api na-satya-ādi-sammiśritam eva bhavati
sva-prayojana-artham nirjalopavāsa-vratam yadi bhavān ācaret tarhi tat sva-arthāya eva bhavet
vahni-saṃsarga-buddhi-janaka tvam
damanakaḥ brūte deva saṃjīvakaḥtavaupari na-sadṛśa-vyavahārī iva lakṣyate
prathamaḥ vairasyaāyatanaṃ balasya nikaṣaṃ māna-pratiṣṭhā-gṛhaṃ
na ca ukta-doṣa-vāraṇāya nirukta-viśeṣa-kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvasya āvaśyakatveapi
bhrātṛ-mahodayaḥ dillī-sarvakāre mukhya-yantra-kalā-abhijñaḥ
tasmāt pada-viśeṣa-vācaka-tva-prakārakaḥ bodhaḥ tasmai jananīyaḥ itiabhisandhinā
na-anya-darśinaḥ tu na ātman-artham yoga-kṣemam īhante
sam-ālāpa-catura
śaśi-sūrya-netram śaśi-sūryau netre yasya tava saḥ tvam śaśi-sūrya-netraḥ tam tvām śaśi-sūrya-netram candra-āditya-nayanam
saḥ śakra-bhavanaṃ gatvā sura-ṛṣi-gaṇa-madhyagam
prāṇa-apāna-samāyuktaḥ pacāmi annam catur-vidham
tulya-priya-na-priyaḥ priyam ca na-priyam ca priya-na-priye tulye same yasya saḥ ayam tulya-priya-na-priyaḥ
nyagrodha-udumbara-aśvattha-plakṣa-lodhra-tvacaḥ śubhāḥ
kukkuṭīnām aṇḍādīnāṃ ca vikraya-upārjita-dravyeṇa ekāṃ ramaṇīyāṃ śāṭikāṃ kreṣyāmi
anya-bhāṣā-prayogaḥ api tatra niṣiddhaḥ kṛtaḥ
athavā yoga-aiśvarya-sāmarthyam sarva-jña tvam yoga-jam yogaḥ ucyate
kim ca viśanti praviśanti samyak-darśana-prāptau satyām yat yatayaḥ yatana-śīlāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ vīta-rāgāḥ vītaḥ vigataḥ rāgaḥ yebhyaḥ te yatana-śīlāḥ
vākya-artha-pratīti-icchayā uccaritatva-rūpasya śabda-gata-vākya-artha-para tvasya caanyādṛśatvena kāṣṭhe vyabhicārasya dur-nirūpa tvāt
ataḥ aham tapaḥ caran brahmarṣitvam prāpsyāmi eva iti saṃkalpya viśvāmitraḥ patnyā saha tapas-caryā-nimittam dakṣiṇām diśam anusṛtavān
yatra dharmaḥ tatra jayaḥ iti mahat-ṛṣi-vacanaṃ satyameva abhavat
droṇaḥ hanta sarve prasannāḥ smaḥ pravṛddha-kula-saṃgrahāḥ
mātuṃgā nir-vastrā satī pratyūṣe matsya-bandhana-jāle sva-śarīram āveṣṭya
tadā dṛṣṭa-adṛṣṭa-prayojanam karma pratiṣiddham api śarīreṇa kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam ityapi bruvataḥ viruddha-abhidhānam prasajyeta
tasya-anucaraiḥ-caradbhiḥ pakṣibhiḥ-aham dagdhā-āraṇya madhye caran-avalokitaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ-ca kaḥtvam
snāna-ādīnāṃ śīta-uṣṇa-ādīnāṃ ca spṛśyānām an-anupūrvya-upasevanaṃ viṣama-sthāna-abhighāta-aśuci-bhūta-saṃsparśa-ādayaḥ caiti mithyāyogaḥ
pratyāvāyasya iṣṭatva-abhāvāt pratyavāya-hetu tvasya liṅ-artha-tā-abhyupagamaḥ na svārasikaḥ
ghṛta-guḍa-dadhi-su-samṛddham dhūpita-sūpa-upadaṃśa-sambhinnam
yathā āpaṇikena ājñaptā bhojana-antaraṃ nācammā jhāmu-kāṣṭha-nirmite sva-bhartuḥ eva paryaṅke atitheḥ kṛte śayyāṃ prasāritavatī
vyāpāriṇaḥ dīpa-āvali-parva-avasare kiṃ kurvantaḥ āsan
gurutara-avajñā-pātheyam hṛdi nidhāya sā bahu-kāla-paryantam sāmānya-sthitim na alabhat
na-vyakta-ādīni bhūtāni vyakta-madhyāni bhārata
vidhūma-aṅgāra-tapteṣu svabhyaktaḥ svidyate sukham
tad-pada-artha tvamca tad-pada-prayojya-viṣayatā-āśraya tvam
ālocitam rājñā etat-śloka-mukhena eva sarvam api rahasyam udghāṭitam syāt iti
phala-antare tad-sādhana-bhūtāyām vā kriyāyām arthitva-na-upapattiḥ
dṛṣṭi-śukra-ghnaḥ kṣāraḥ
brāhmaṇaḥ asya mukham āsīt iti-ādi-śruteḥ
tat na-praṇīvatām śarvavarman-prabhṛtīnām mukhya-artha-parāṇām sthalyāmadhiśete iti-ādi-prayogāṇām sādhutāyāḥ dur-vāra tvātca
aśva-medha-sahasrāt hi satyamevaatiricyate
grāmīṇāḥ vyacārayan sva-grāma-stham paṇḍitam akārayantu
śrī-mahat-deva-puṇatāmakara-mahodayaiḥ nirmitāḥ nyāya-kaustubhaḥ khaṇḍa-catuṣṭaya-ātmankaḥ
dvija-vara-hasta-dhṛta-ambu-sikta-mūrdhā
yataḥ tena eka-viṃśati-vāraṃ pṛthivī kṣatriya-vihīnā kṛtā āsīt
nikhile api dvija-āgrahāre tat-āgamana-vārtā karṇāt karṇam prasarantī saṃvyāptā
saṃyogasya indriya-pratiyogika tvena tad-ghaṭitasya saṃyukta-viśeṣyaka-jñāna-prakāra-bhūta-dhūmatvasya indriya-saṃbandha tvamivaiti na kaḥapi doṣaḥ
teṣāṃ manana-cintana-sāmarthyam iti sarvaṃ saḥ vyasmarat
pratyāya-arthaḥ pradhānamitiapi na sup-artha-viṣaya tayā saṃkocayitavyam
sarvatra buddhi-ādi-deha-ante ātman-caitanya-ābhāsatā ātman-bhrānti-kāraṇam ityataḥ ca ātman-viṣayam jñānam na vidhātavyam
rāmaḥ śvaḥtatra bhavataḥtātasya anusaṃvatsara-śrādda-vidhiḥ
raghoḥ śāsane yajña-yāga-ādīnāṃ vighnaḥ kutaḥ
agni-saṃrakṣaṇa vatā yava-godhūma-śālayaḥ
ānaya mṛgaḥ dhāvati ityatra mṛga-kartṛka-dhāvane ānayana-karma tvasya bādhāt mṛga-viśiṣṭa-dhāvanasya bodhitam ānayana-karma tvam sa-viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena mṛge paryavasyatiiti taiḥvaktavyatvāt
tasya haste rajata-rekhā-yuktaḥ vicitraḥ veṇuḥ āsīt
vastutaḥtu bauddhayoḥeva śabda-arthayoḥ vācya-vācaka-bhāvaḥ
sādṛśya-bhinna-sambandhena śakya-saṃbandhi-artha-pratipādikā śuddhā
evaṃ vicittya saḥ avadat pañcadaśa-suvarṇa-mudrāḥ paryāptaḥ daṇḍaḥ
pakṣadharamiśra-kṛtasya śabda-maṇi-ālokasya śiromaṇi-viracitānām ākhyāta-vāda-anuvāda-nañ-vāda-ādīnām ca vyākhyānāni vidhāya
saḥ tiktaḥ mukha-vaiśadya-śoṣa-prahlāda-kārakaḥ
