klṛpta-vyutpatti-balāt iṣṭa-sādhana-yāga-anukūla-kṛti mān svarga-kāmaḥ iti śābda-bodha-svīkāraḥ api naiyāyikānām na saṃgaccheta
na-jñāta-vāsaṃ vāñchamānaḥ kaḥapi kṣatriyaḥ bhavet iti manye
vividheṣu samayeṣu ca samagacchāvahi kintu vicitrā iyam sthitiḥ ādhunikīnām ucca-kulīna-vasatīnām yat tatra nikaṭa-stheṣu api gṛha-svāmiṣu na abhūvan tādṛśā prativeśin-sulabhā sneha-sambandhāḥ yādṛśāḥ grāmeṣu
jvara-kāsa-prasaktānāṃ kṛśānāṃ mūtrakṛcchriṇām
śakti-mada-ādhmātā ye puruṣāḥ yat kiñcit kurvanti
haldīghāṭi-yuddha-anantaraṃ akabareṇa sainyam ādiṣṭam yat sirohī
yena amṛtam mātṛ-vimokṣaṇa-artham
na bāndhava-anurakta-kṛcchradvitīya-guhyajñān bahiḥ kuryāt
śanai śanai mātṛ-viyoga-dukham śaithilyam prāpa candramaule
pitāmaha eka-putra-vināśāt arjunasya tāvat īdṛśī khalu avasthā
ataḥ eva vedāntinaḥapi abhihita-anvaya-vāde lākṣaṇikānām anubhāvakatva-svīkārāt satyam jñānam na-antam brahma ityatra sarva-padānām lākṣaṇikatveapi na anvaya-anubhāvaka-tva-na-upapattiḥ iti vadanti
abhāvatva-na-viśeṣāt atyanta-pradhvaṃsa-abhāvayoḥ iva
śoka-divaseṣu miṣṭānnāni vipācayitum katham śakyate putraḥ ca āgraheṇa akathayat mat-mitra-gṛheṣu miṣṭānnāni vipāccayante kimapi syādahantu miṣṭānnam khāditum icchāmi
lavaṇaḥ rasaḥ pācanaḥ kledanaḥ dīpanaḥcyāvanaḥchedanaḥ bhedanaḥtīkṣṇaḥ saraḥ vikāsī adhaḥ-sraṃsī avakāśa-karaḥ vāta-haraḥ stambha-bandha-saṅghāta-vidhamanaḥ sarva-rasa-pratyanīkabhūtaḥ
kutaḥ sevā-vihīnānām cāmara-uddhūta-saṃpadaḥ
yathā-samayam āvayoḥ pati-patnyoḥ su-ramya-vāṭikāyām ekaḥ kusuma-samaḥ komalaḥ śiśuḥ āvirbhūtaḥ
teṣām ca deha-antaram na-kṛtvā kṣaya-na-upapattau mokṣa-na-upapattiḥ
parikramya vilokya aye ayam aṅga-rājaḥ samara-paricchada-parivṛtaḥ śalya-rājena saha sva-bhavanāt niṣkramya itaḥ eva abhivartate
pūrva-kāla-avacchinna-sva-niṣṭha-abhāva-pratiyogin-tva-sahita-ādheyatā-viśeṣa-sambandhena anvayaḥ
mat-vākyaiḥ pari-khidyamāna-hṛdayaṃ roṣāt pra-matta-akṣaraiḥ
ghṛta-māṃsa-rasa-kṣīra-hṛdya-yūṣa-upasaṃhitaiḥ
yaḥ tri-ṣaṣṭi-śata-ārasya veda-arthaṃ sa paraḥ kaviḥ
benyahūdasya bandhuḥ kaścana sva-gṛhe teṣāṃ vāsa-ādi-vyavasthāḥ kalpitavān
tataḥca tad-kartuḥ īśvarasya āyuṣ-padam idam āyuṣ-janakam bodhayatu iti-ākāraikā āyuṣ-janakaḥ etad-āyuṣ-pada-janya-bodha-viṣayaḥ bhavatu iti-ākāraikā vā bubodhayiṣā vācyā
kāraka-ādi-viśiṣṭa-kriyāyāḥ dhātu-artha tve laḥ karmaṇipā
vajrapurasya rājan-kumārī candrakalā ca na-pratimā-sundaryau iti śrutavān āsīt śivadattaḥ
anya-nimittatve ca svataḥ abhāvāt na-parama-arthatva-prasaṅgaḥ
pippalīmūlaṃ dīpanīya-pācanīya-ānāha-praśamanānāṃ
sva-pratiyogi-vācaka-tva-sambandhena tasya pada-niṣṭha tveapi
rocanaṃ dīpanaṃ vāta-kapha-daurgandhya-nāśanam
samāse tu samāsa-ghaṭaka-pada-śakti-graha-sattve eva viśiṣṭa-artha-bodhaḥ jāyate iti lakṣaṇayā nirvāhaḥ saṃbhavati
na ca pada-śravaṇa-na-antaram anvaya-viśeṣe jijñāsāudeti
kecana kāryāṇi anyeṣāṃ viṣaye kaṣṭa-naṣṭa-dāyakāni bhavanti
kiñcit-kāla-anantaraṃ saḥ uktavān priye bhavatyā śīghra-atiśīghraṃ hībrū-bhāṣāyāḥ abhyāsaḥ karaṇīyaḥ
bandipaṇḍitaṃ sa-aṣṭāṅga-praṇāmaṃ pūjayiṣyāmi iti sa-vinayaṃ proktavān aṣṭāvakraḥ
śarīram kevalam karma kurvan āpnoti kilbiṣam iti ca śarīra-sthiti-kāraṇa-atiriktasya karmaṇaḥ nivāraṇāt
yajña-ādi-karma karaṇīyam
jana-śūnye mahat-vidyālaya-mārge ananta-mahat-samudre niḥsaṅganaukā iva tiṣṭhan monuḥ cītkurvan āsīt payas-himam payas-himam
tasmāt na-spṛśya-varṇa pradhānasya anena kāryeṇa ati prasannaḥ abhūt
guravaḥtarpaṇāḥ vṛṣyāḥ kṣīra-ikṣu-rasa-pūpakāḥ
śrīkṛṣṇaḥ tu tri-kāla-jñaḥ
na ca dvi-niṣṭha-tva-abhāvāt evaabhedasya na saṃbandhatvamiti vācyam
aham taiḥ vinā-bhūtaḥ kim kariṣyāmi rājya-sukha-ādinā iti
śāla-kaṭphala-kadamba-padmaka-tumba-mocarasa-śirīṣa-vañjula-elavāluka-aśokāḥ iti daśaimāni vedanāsthāpanāni bhavanti
mayā saṃsārasya sarva-atiśāyi-mūlyavatā vastunā paripūrṇatāṃ nītaḥ ayam
apitu ghakāra-uttara-akāra-uttara-ṭakāra-uttara-akārasya vācakatvam na kevala-akārasya itiarthaḥ vācyaḥ tatca na na-iṣṭam
paurāṇāṃ sukha-vāsa-arthaṃ tatra ārāma-ādi-nirmāṇaṃ kāritavān
asau sakalena api ciraṃ-upārjita-vittena svarṇaṃ krītavān
paryākulai-kṛta-buddhiḥ arjunaḥ uvāca
svāmi-bhaktāḥ dṛḍha-niṣṭhāvantaḥ ca ete yuvakāḥ śivarājasya kṛte prāṇa-arpaṇa-artham api siddhāḥ āsan
pra-koṣṭha-rakṣakeṇa kathitam yadrogī svasthaḥ bhūtvā adhunā eva gata
prathamā-prakṛti-arthaḥ kasmin prathamā-arthe viśeṣaṇatayāanvetiiti vācyam
sama-duḥkha-sukhaḥ svasthaḥ sama-loṣṭa-aśma-kāñcanaḥ
na ca ayam gauḥ iti-ādeḥ sa-vikalpa-pratyayaḥ vācaka-śabda-sāmānādhikaraṇyena artha-avagāhi tvāt śabda-artha-tādātmyam siddhyatiitiuktamiti vācyam
uttara-vākyena api abheda-saṃsargaka-bodha-janakena eva bhāvyam
tat-prabhāvaḥ ca deveśasya nagara-grāma-bhūmim api aspṛśat
ataḥ śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ tataḥ na-dṛśyaḥ bhūtvā yathā-pūrvam vṛkṣasya śākhām ālambitavān
na-phala-ākāṅkṣibhiḥ yuktaiḥ sāttvikaṃ paricakṣate
rāmaḥ sa-santoṣam lakṣmaṇasya anusaraṇam aṅgīkṛtya vasiṣṭha-mahat-ṛṣeḥ divya-astrāṇi ānīyantām iti ādiṣṭavān
ā-janman-samabhyastaḥ ca iti yātrā-artham vihitaḥ ca iti na pāda-cāraḥ asmān vyathayati
tatra eka-agram manaḥ kṛtvā yata-citta-indriya-kriyaḥ
na-śakye tātparyam śakyāt na-śakya-upasthitim
naindriyaṃ bādhate dhūmaḥ mātrā-kāla-niṣevitaḥ
tava dyūta-parājaya-rājya-bhraṃśa-bhāryā-viyoga-ādi-sakala-duḥkhānāṃ kāraṇam aham eva
bhavatu tāvat asmin śaile prāṇān parityajāmi marut-prapātaḥ hi sarva-artha-sādhakaḥ
guru-mata-anuyāyinaḥ tu
uṣṇa-vīryaiḥ a-lābhe tu kauśeya-āvika-śāṭakaiḥ
na ca kaḥ gacchati rājā gacchati iti-ādau kavi-kṛta-svabhāva-varṇana-ādau ca pada-arthānām anvaya-bodha-janana-sāmarthyam klṛptam
nīti-śāstra-vicakṣaṇāḥ
astu yathākathañcit kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvaḥ
eka-varṣam yāvat bālasya asya nānā-vidha-rakṣaṇa-upāyān sādhayan rāyamahodaya bālam saṃrakṣitavān
na-phala-ākāṅkṣibhiḥ yajñaḥ vidhi-dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ ijyate
imāṃ kanaka-pratimāṃ kasyacana divya-sundara-rājakumārasya hastayoḥ samarpayituṃ sā na samarthā
brahmacārī tataḥtasyāḥ śarīra-upa-bhuktāni dagdha-śeṣāṇi ābharaṇāni pariṣvajya rājā mohamupagataḥ
ekasmin vāk-mana-vyāpārai paraspara-ākarṣaṇa-vardhanā īpsā vartate
tat tu dhanu-jyā-sphālanāt jātena antarganta-vraṇena katicit dina-anantaraṃ sva-prāṇān tyaktavān
rājan-pūruṣāḥ amātyaḥ prasthitaḥ iti kaścit amātya-bhṛtyaḥ kanyāpura-rakṣaṇa-artham na abhyāgataḥ
rājā kalatra-darśana-arhaṃ janaṃ kalatra-darśanāt pariharatiiti bahu-doṣam utpādayati
atha śabda-artha-saṃbandham na-jānatām śabda-sāmānādhikaraṇyena artha-pratītiḥ uta naiti sandehaḥ evaastu
tathā indriyebhyaḥ param manaḥ saṃkalpa-vikalpa-ātmakam
yasya svanam pralaya-sāgara-ghoṣa-tulyam
na-ādi-madhya-antam ananta-vīryam ananta-bāhum śaśi-sūrya-netram
vyāghra-anusāra-cakitā hariṇī iva yāsi
teṣu dvā-daśa-varṣīyaḥ chatrasālaḥ api āsīt
rudhira-kalita-gātraḥ srasta-saṃrakta-netraḥ
vākya-artha tvena pūrvatvātpūrvamupasthitiḥasaṃbhāvinī cet śābda-bodha-aupayika-smaraṇa-prayojaka tvam naasya anya-niṣṭha-saṃbandhasya
tatra yadā taiḥ naukāpattanaṃ prāpya naukā-ārohaṇa-artham udyuktaṃ tadā tatratyaḥ adhikārī tadānīm eva ātmanā prāptam ājñā-patraṃ darśitavān yat deśatyāgāya na anumantavyaḥ benyahūdaḥ
na-iṣṭa-cintanena kiṃ bhavati
na arhati mānaṃ sva-jana-dveṣī
iṣṭa-varṇa-gandha-rasa-sparśaṃ vidhi-vihitam anna-pānaṃ prāṇināṃ prāṇi-saṃjña kānāṃ prāṇamācakṣate kuśalāḥ
asmin samaye madhurapura-grāme dhūmaśakaṭi-viśrama-sthāna-sannidhāne eva nandarāma-vaṇijaḥ samudghāṭyamānaḥ āpaṇaḥ asti
yathā-prasiddha-na-vidvat-puruṣa-viṣayatvāt śāstrasya
tasmāt na dṛṣṭa-mithyā-jñāna-nimittasya aham-pratyayasya deha-ādi-saṃghāte gauṇatvam kalpayitum śakyam
sva-manas-toṣāya saḥ vividhān paśūn apālayat sva-kṛṣi-kāryam kṛtvā saḥ viśrāmam karoti tathā ebhi paśubhi krīḍati
madanaphalaṃ vamana-āsthāpana-anuvāsana-upayogināṃ
mama prasannatāyāḥ kāraṇam tu mahat-viṣṇu-bhaktasya ambarīṣasya darśanam
sandaṣṭa-oṣṭhaḥ caṇḍa-saṃrakta-netraḥ
deva-dvija-guru-prājña-pūjanam śaucam ārjavam
kāraka-saṃkhyā-viśiṣṭa-kriyā-kāla-yoga-abhidhāyi tvamitiaparam
mṛtam vā jīvitam vā tam ānetum tat-āvāsa-saṅketa-sthalam saṃsūcya grāhayitum ca ya kopi janaḥ lakṣarūpyaka-puraskāreṇa praśāsanena puraṣkariṣyate iti
svarga-artham āhava-mukha-udyata-gātrahomāḥ
yatra padasyaekaḥarthaḥ tatra śakti-kalpanāyāḥ abhihita-anvaya-vāda-anvita-abhidhāna-vādayoḥ tulyatveapi
sārdha-pañcavarṣa-deśīyaḥ benjhiyonaḥ prathama-kakṣyāyāṃ praveśaṃ prāpnot
dharma-artha-kāma-mokṣāṇām prāṇāḥ saṃsthiti-hetavaḥ
śaradi puṣpyanti saptan-cchadāḥ iti vākya-artha-vimarśa-avasare
tip-ādi-antam ākhyātam iti na-sandigdham brūte
sṛṣṭānāṃ śabdānāṃ pariśīlanaṃ kṛtvā sā ca hībrū-bhāṣā-samitiḥ nirṇayati sma yat kiṃ te śabdāḥ yogyāḥ
ataḥ tvam nir-artha-ka-cintanaṃ parijahīhi
na ca gavi aśva-sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīti-abhāvaḥ tayoḥ upāya-upeya-bhāva-abhāvāt
karaṇa-sandhābandha-prahāraiḥ yuddha-viśeṣaiḥ siddhim gacchāvaḥ
madhya-ahna-samaye vardhamānema vāyu-vegena anyāni api bahūni phalāni adhaḥ patitvā bhagnāni
rakta-pradoṣa-jāḥ rogāḥteṣu rogeṣu caauṣadham
bharataḥ hanta trai-lokya-sākṣiṇaḥ khaluete
tenālīrāmaḥ sahasā sva-kara-gṛhītena sādhoḥ kareṇa pra-mattasya śirasi prahāram akārayat
evañca saṃbandha-sāmānya-saṃsargaka-kāla-prakāraka-bhāvanā-viśeṣyaka-bodhe
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na-hiṃsā-cārakaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ asti
na astikaḥ api kadācit puṇya-kārye na-saktaḥ san api koṭi-adhipatitvam prāpya sarva-vidha-sukhāni anubhavati
etāni api iti prakṛta-saṃnikṛṣṭa-arthatva-upapatteḥ
vyaktiśa paricayam prāpya tā sva-sva-sthāneṣu ca sam-preṣitā
mahat-rājena pra-mattaḥ janaḥ pra-matta-avāse preṣitaḥ ādiṣṭaṃ ca
mātṛ-guṇa-anurūpā āsīt
ekaḥ maśakaḥ bhin bhin śabdaṃ kurvan ekaṃ balīvardam upetya abravīt yuṣmākaṃ vṛṣabhāṇāṃ dehaḥ ati-viśālaḥ su-puṣṭa-avayavaḥ ca
dhātu-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kam bodham pratipannāḥ
vidāhaḥcaannapānasya tikta-amla-udgiraṇaṃ klamaḥ
vākya-artha-avagama-tātparyeṇa prayuktāni padāni sva-artha-smaraṇa-dvārā anvaya-bodham janayanti
na ca adhama-pada-artha-paryālocanayā anumāpakatvamapi sambhavatiiti vācyam
dhana-praṇāśa-śokāt avaruddha-kaṇṭhena tena sarvam abhāṇi
ataḥ ghaṭatva-anvita-śābda-tva-avacchinnam prati ghaṭa-pada tvena kāraṇatvamāvaśyakam
tau eva saṃnyāsa-karman-yogau jñāna-tad-upāya-sama-buddhitva-ādi-saṃyuktau sāṃkhya-yoga-śabda-vācyau iti bhagavataḥ matam
tasyām ca tasya gṛha-saṃketa dūrabhāṣa-kramāṅka-ādi-sarvam aṃkitam abhūt
na a-vigata-klamaḥ na an-āpluta-vadanaḥ na nagnaḥ upaspṛśet
anyaṃ kamapi upālambhaṃ śrotuṃ śaktaḥ saḥ veda-pāṭha-viṣaye tu na-sahana-mūrtiḥ eva
sva-janma-bhūmeḥ gauravasya svātantryasya ca rakṣā-artham te svīyān prāṇān api sa-harṣam utsṛṣṭavanta
sarveṣām api avadhānaṃ tatra akṛṣṭam abhavat ityataḥ benjhiyonaḥ api na tathā khedam anubhūtavān patrikā-sañcālana-sthaganena
evam śiras-ghātam ghnatī sā bālā sat-dharma-bala-udbhūtam iva balam avāpya katipayaiḥ eva kṣaṇaiḥ viṃśati pañcaviṃśati vā puruṣān jaghāna
prācī-diśa-adhipate he indra pratyakṣībhūya māmanugṛhāṇa
videśīya-pakva-annānām āsvāda-hetave kṣudha-āturāḥ atithayaḥ aham ahamikayā khādyeṣu peyeṣu ca tatparatāṃ pradarśayāmāsuḥ
tīrtha-yātrā-arthaṃ prasthitaḥ ekaḥ siddha-puruṣaḥ mārge samāyātasya ekasya sad-gṛha-sthasya atithiḥ abhavat
pūrva-para-sandarbha-paryālocanayā bhāṣya-tātparya-ṭīkā-ādi-paryālocanayā ca anyādṛśa-artheṃ tad-sūtra-tātparya-avadhāraṇāt
tasya eva vyavasāya-tuṣṭa-hṛdayaiḥ tat-vikrama-utsāhibhiḥ
arśaḥ śopha-udara-ghnaṃ tu sa-kṣāraṃ māhiṣaṃ saram
yadā yasmin kāle te tava moha-kalilam moha-ātmakam na-viveka-rūpam kāluṣyam yena ātman-na-ātma-viveka-bodham kaluṣai-kṛtya viṣayam prati antaḥkaraṇam pravartate
tatra ca siddharājam upasthātukāma sa sahasā iva svasya tat-sabhā-praveśam duṣkaram iva matvā kāṃścit tat-adhyakṣān upātiṣṭhat
na-mita-utsāhena gacchasi
saptame tu anna-kāle tathāvidhānāmeva śālīnāṃ dvi-prasṛtaṃ su-svinnam odanam uṣṇa-udaka-anupānaṃ tanunā tanu-sneha-lavaṇa-upapannena mudga-yūṣeṇa bhojayet
putra-putryoḥ-bhedaḥ bhavati iti tayā kadā api na anubhūtam
ucca-adhikāriṇām sabhya-ācaraṇa-saṃhitā-anurūpam ca tasya nagarasya ucca-adhikāriṇam gṛhe gatvā katham abhivādanam karaṇīyam
deśaḥca saundarya-sampat-ādi-nikhila-guṇa-khaniḥ
rāvaṇa-vināśa-anantaraṃ rāma-rājyaṃ tena prasthāpitam
yadā sarve devāḥ na-sāvadhāna-cittāḥ āsan tadā akasmāt bali-rājena svargaṃ paritaḥ paridhiḥ kṛtaḥ
evañca ghaṭa-pada-janya-maitra-jñāna-viṣayaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti jñānam bodhyatva-rūpa-śakti-viṣaya kamiti tena śābda-bodha-āpādanam saṃbhavatiiti vācyam
bhoḥ vayasya samudra-pattana-sāra-bhūtaḥ tādṛśaḥ artha-sañcayaḥ kva gataḥ
tathā deha-antara-prāptiḥ dhīraḥ tatra na muhyati
pañca-varṣa-antaram pitāmahī divaṃ-gatā
tasmin kāle ekaḥ markaṭaḥ api sa-ātma-jaḥ tatra samāyātaḥ
saḥ netre nimīlya rāma-nāma-jape sva-manaḥ kendritavān
śarkarā-kṣīra-sarpīṃṣi sarveṣāṃ viddhi bṛṃhaṇam
saṃvādi-pravṛttau saṃsṛṣṭa-artha-jñānam eva kāraṇam
tad-apekṣayā ca na prakṛti-tātparya-viṣaya tvam guru-bhūtam iti vācyam
tṛṣṇā-atīsāra-śūla-ārtāḥ śvāsinaḥ hikkinaḥ kṛśāḥ
vastutaḥ yatra etat sainyaṃ calati sma tatra sainya-vāsa-arthaṃ ekaṃ nagaram eva nirmitaṃ bhavati sma
mahat-muneḥ vālmīkeḥ āśramaḥ tamasā-nadī-tīre āsīt
śrutvā vraje vipula-vikrama-vīrya-sattvam
kañcukīyaḥ atha ca tayā a-nāhūta-upa-sṛtayā bharataḥabhiṣicyatāṃ rājye itiuktam
praśānti-aiśvarya-īhā-mūḍhatā-svabhāva-darśanāt caturṇām
etāṃ yojanāṃ vicārayantau tau ati-pra-muditau āstām
kāma-ātmanaḥ svarga-parā janma-karma-phala-pradām
tādṛśa-samudāyasya arthavattve nāmatvāt tad-arthasya ādheyatā-sambandhena ghoṣa-nāman-arthe anvayasya nāman-arthayoḥ iti vyutpatti-viruddha tvāt
prāṇa-āpāna-gatī mukha-nāsikābhyām vāyoḥ nirgamanam prāṇasya gatiḥ
na-udvega-karam prāṇinām na-duḥkha-karam vākyam satyam priya-hitam ca yat priya-hite dṛṣṭa-na-dṛṣṭa-arthe
kopa-āviṣṭena mahat-rājena aṣṭa-dina-anantaraṃ tasya śūla-āropaṇaṃ ādiṣṭam
tataḥ śīla-śauca-ācāra-anurāga-dākṣya-prādakṣiṇya-upapannān upacāra-kuśalān sarva-karmasu paryavadātān sūpa-audana-pācaka-snāpaka-saṃvāhaka-utthāpaka-saṃveśaka-auṣadha-peṣakān ca paricārakān sarva-karmasu a-pratikūlān
pratyayānām sva-prakṛti-artha-anvita-sva-artha-bodhaka-tva-vyutpatteḥ
vidahat mukha-nāsā-akṣi saṃsrāvī saḥ kaṭuḥ smṛtaḥ
nija-prakhara-buddhimattayā tenālīrāmaḥ bahūn puraskārān sammāna-ādi kaṃ prāyaḥ alabhata
mudraṇa-ālaye akṣara-saṃyojana-ādi-kāryaṃ kurvantaḥ karma-karāḥ tena sūcitāḥ yat taiḥ hībrū-bhāṣayā eva vaktavyam
tam api jñātvā eka-pāda-prahāreṇa cūrṇa-ikṛtaḥ saḥ api dānavaḥ bhūtvā tataḥ eva mṛtaḥ
śakya-sambandhi-pratīti-icchayā uccaritatva-paryavasitam śakya-sambandhini tātparyam tu na lakṣaṇā
śveta-mūtra-netra-varcas tvaṃ ca
loka-ānanāya kamala-a-mala-locanāya
bhasma-kuṇḍala-ādikam vikṛti-karma
te api suta-sparśa-jena ānandena amṛta-āsikte iva sukhasya sīmānaṃ na vidāñcakratuḥ
girim abhigaccha sa-nīra-nīra-da-ābham
nāgam mṛga-indraḥ iva pūrva-kṛta-avalepam
itthaṃ niśamya tava bhojana-ādi-sevayā jīvitena mayā asya gaṇita-granthasya nāma bhāmatī kriyate
ugra-jala-vegāṃ saritam avagāhituṃ paraśuṃ ca anveṣṭum asau sāhasaṃ na babhāra
dānam priya-vāk-sahitam jñānam na-garvam kṣamā-anvitam śauryam
vyoman-mārgīya-vibhinna-sādhanai sañcāra-sādhanāni āśritya tayā tat-viśrama-sthalasya anveṣaṇā kṛtā yatra śrāntā klāntā duṣṭa-atyācāriṇa apahṛta-bālānām api nidrā sañcorya eva suṣuptā
paṭa-ādi-viṣayaiṇī api īśvara-icchā na paṭe ghaṭa-pada-janya-bodha-viṣaya tvamavagāhate tathā sati syāt visaṃvāditva-prasaṅgāt
kintu mandira-dāyitva-nirvahaṇam yadā prārthitam tadā śivaḥ tat tiraskṛtavān
na-mānitva-ādīnām jñāna-sādhanānām bhāvanā-paripāka-nimittam tattva-jñānam
na hi caitraḥ piṭhare odanam pacati ityatra caitra-piṭhara-ādi-pada-arthānām vākya-arthe saṃbandha-na-upapattiḥ asti
eṣaḥ āryaputraḥ harṣa-vismaya-phulla-nayanaḥ itaḥ eva āgacchati
saṃyojayitumicchāmi bāla-bhāva-samutsukaḥ
taṃ tam eva iti kaunteya sadā tad-bhāva-bhāvitaḥ
indriyāṇām hi yasmāt caratām sva-sva-viṣayeṣu pravartamānānām yat manaḥ anuvidhīyate anupravartate tat indriya-viṣaya-vikalpanena pravṛttam manaḥ asya yateḥ harati prajñām ātman-na-ātma-viveka-jām nāśayati
kusumbha-bilva-āruka-mūlaka-atasī-nikocaka-akṣoḍa-karañja-śigrukāḥ
itthamca caitraḥ pacati iti vākyāt pāka-anukūla-kṛti mān ekatva-viśiṣṭaḥ caitraḥ iti prathamā-anta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-ka eva bodhaḥ svīkartṛmucitaḥ
tatra dhūma-śābda-bodhe jāte dhūmenaanumīyate vahniḥ na hiatra dhūma-padasya vahnau lakṣaṇāmabhyupagacchanti
phāl̤akemahodayaḥ yadi evaṃ niścitaṃ tarhi kañcana citra-nirmita-gṛhaṃ gacchatu
na tu atiriktaḥ vācya-vācaka-bhāvaḥ tatra pramāṇa-abhāvāt
yena śābda-bodhasya śabda-viṣayaka tvam sūtra-kāra-abhimatam iti kalpyeta
ūrṇa-roma-anvitaḥ ayam meṣaḥ jvalitum lagna
na caevam sati ghaṭa-padasya eva ghaṭa-vācaka tvam na kalaśa-ādi-padānām
mandaṃ vahamānaḥ suma-gandha-vāhī pavamānaḥ
kanaka-bhūṣaṇa-saṃgrahaṇa-ucitaḥ
kiñca te mām īśvaram ātman-para-deheṣu sva-dehe para-deheṣu ca tad-buddhi-karma-sākṣin-bhūtam mām pradviṣantaḥ
hībrū-senā-patiḥ
kim nu khalu na-eka-kapaṭa-buddheḥ kṛṣṇasya upāyaḥ
na pauṣkaraṃ rohiṇīkaṃ śākaṃ kapotān vā sarṣapa-taila-bhraṣṭān madhu-payobhyāṃ sahaabhyavaharet
vīta-moha-rajaḥ-doṣa-lobha-māna-mada-spṛhaḥ
duryodhanaḥ vayasya karṇa gurujana-praṇāma-avasāne prāpta-kramam upabhujyatāṃ vayasya-visrambhaḥ
nirrghātaiḥ tumula-svana-pratibhayaiḥ kiṃ dāryate vā mahī
tena sa-bhrūkuṭi-bhaṅgam aham prati-bodhitaḥ yat prativeśitvāt saḥ na mat-virodhe kiṃcana vivakṣati kintu mayā nanditā-sācaryam pari-tyājyam
tathā cet etasyām bhayam-kara-rātrau asmin ghore śmaśāne vividhāni kaṣṭāni bhavatā sammukhīkaraṇīyāni bhaveyuḥ iti bhāti mama
evañca dhātu-arthasya kṛtau anukūlatā-saṃbandhena anvayaḥ eva pākena iti-ādi-vivaraṇa-anukūlam bhavati
asti hi karman-saṃnyāsasya phala-abhisandhi-tyāgasya ca tyāgatva-sāmānyam
tataḥ ca śreṣṭhin-varya naijam vyavasthāpakam āya-vyaya-ādi-saṃdhārakam munīma iti bhāṣāyām buddhimallam āhūya mantraṇām ārebhe
varṣā-śīta-ucita-aṅgānāṃ sahasā eva arka-raśmibhiḥ
ebhyaḥcaeva a-pathya-āhāra-doṣa-śarīra-viśeṣebhyaḥ vyādhayaḥ mṛdavaḥ dāruṇāḥ kṣipra-samutthāḥ cira-kāriṇaḥ ca bhavanti
tatra dravyāṇi guru-khara-kaṭhina-manda-sthira-viśada-sāndra-sthūla-gandha-guṇa-bahulāni pārthivāni
prati-akṣa-pramāṇam vilokya rājāpi tat svīcakāra
na tu siṃha-kāryam agnikāryam vā gauṇa-śabda-pratyaya-nimittam kiñcit sādhyate
madhura-amla-lavaṇa-kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāya-kṣārāḥ
tatra āsīt benyahūdasya tāvatāṃ dinānāṃ pariśramasya pratiphala-svarūpaḥ hībrū-śabda-koṣasya prathamaḥ bhāgaḥ
evam varṣa-dvayam atītam param deveśasya pitāmahaḥ smāram smāram sva-dainya-udantam pūrva-vibhavam ca ekadā divaṅgataḥ jāta
vivikta-sevī araṇya-nadī-pulina-giri-guha-ādīn viviktān deśān sevitum śīlam asya iti vivikta-sevī
prāyaḥ mṛduvahāḥ gurvyaḥ yāḥca pūrva-samudra-gāḥ
tatra bhū-tale ghaṭaḥ naasti ityatra ghaṭa-viśeṣyaka-bhū-tala-vṛtti-tva-abhāva-prakāra-bodha-vādinām
mayā api tādṛśi eva mahat-nagara-sulabhā manas-pravṛtti śanai śanaiḥ aṅgīkṛtā abhūt
stana-taṭa-valgana-khinna-sanna-madhyā
kirīṭinam kirīṭam nāma śiras-bhūṣaṇa-viśeṣaḥ tat yasya asti saḥ kirīṭī tam kirīṭinam
bhārata bharata-anvaya-ja
api ca kṣata-abhihata-daṣṭa-dagdha-bhagna-śūna-pracyuta-avamūtrita-parisarpita-mardita-cchinna-bhinna-viśliṣṭa-udviddha-utpiṣṭa-ādīni pācayati āgneya-svabhāvāt
bhīmasenaḥ ehiehi putra pitṛ-sadṛśa-parākramaḥ bhava
anyatva-anvaya-pratiyogi-vācaka-pada-na-samabhivyahārāt
prathamaḥ miṣṭa-anna-vyavasāyī sva-vipaṇyām kim alekhayat
bhūtika sarva-rājan-maṇḍalam apohya dvayoḥ sthāpitayoḥ kam prati viśeṣaḥ
yadi tathā ajñāsyat tarhi tasmin samaye sva-vivāha-viṣayam saḥ na avadiṣyat eva
vāsantyā patiḥ mādhavanātha sat-śīla dhanavān rūpa-guṇa-sampanna vāsantyā anurūpam eva āsīt
sā ca proccai prahasya punaḥ avādīt na asmi kim ātman-rakṣaṇa-kṣamā
ataḥ na āvayoḥ gṛha-janā ajānan yat mama kiṃcit tātkālikam sakhyam sainya-adhikārin-duhitrā nanditayā saha saṃjātam iti
pārṣṇīṃ yāapi bhavat-prayāṇa-samaye tasyāḥ vidhānaṃ kṛtam
bādhaka-pratyaya-na-upapatteḥ
sā tu devī mat-mātṛ-sadṛśī vartate
tataḥ loka-saṃgraha-artham prārabdha-karmatvāt karmaṇā saha eva na-saṃnyasya eva karma saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ ityarthaḥ
tad-vacasā bhū-pati-mukha-kamalaṃ smitena ārājata
vyapadeśivat-bhāvena tādātmya-saṃbandha-paryavasitena kriyā-janya-viklṛtti-rūpa-phala-āśraya tvāt
yadi ca lakṣaṇā-sthale na śakya-artha-parityāgaḥ
pitroḥ mātāmahasya ca āśīrvādaṃ prāpya śubhadine uttara-dik-abhimukhaḥ prasthitaḥ
haṃsī priya yauvana-unmeṣa-śālinaḥ niṣadha-rāja-kumāra udvāha-arthaṃ sūtradhāriṇī bhava iti asmat-svāminaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ājñā
rāya-mahāśaya-pārśva-gatena rājñyā sevakena uktam darśanam abhilaṣantī tatra bhavatī bhavat samīpam upasarpati iti
tathā ca na-prasiddha-artha-bodha-aupayika-śakteḥ eva lakṣaṇā-padena vyavahṛtāyāḥ śakyatā-avacchedaka-āropa-mūla-śakya-sambandha-bhedāt gauṇītva-ādinā vibhāgaḥ kṛtaḥ iti bodhyam
mama patiḥ eka-patnī-vrata-sthaḥ iti uktavatī
evaṃ sva-rājya-sthāpanasya śubha-ārambhaḥ jātaḥ
saubhāgyena sapta-dina-anantaram eva sthitiḥ eṣā samāgāta
pada-upa-saṃgrahaṇa-kāraṇam vibudhya śreṣṭhin-vara kapardikāmalla na-vāk-manā tatra kṣaṇam api sthātum prabhu
sā candra-kalā vat prati-aham pravardhamānā sarva-guṇa-sampannā ca āsīt
tīrthāśramasurasthāne śāstra-vijñāna-hetunā
tasya grāma-vāsinaḥ sarala-svabhāva-yuktāḥ śāntāḥ maitrī-bhāva-sampannāḥ ca āsan
catuḥ-daśa-varṣāṇi yāvat vanam prati rāmasya preṣaṇam
tathāpi bhūmi-krayaṇa-viṣaye saḥ bhāskarasya abhiprāyam kim-artham pṛṣṭavān
bhoḥ bhoḥ nyagrodha-devatāḥ yadi ayam bālaḥ loka-hita-artham kaṃsa-vadha-artham vṛṣṇi-kule prasūtaḥ cet
bāhyā tvak-snāyu-māṃsa-utthā kaṇḍara-ābhā mahā-rujā
prakaṭita-smita vat mukhamiti bodha-na-antaram kusuma-tulya-saurabha-vattva-bodhaḥ jāyate
tau nirgatau yebhyaḥ te nir-māna-mohāḥ māna-moha-varjitāḥ
kaṭu-amla-lavaṇa-atyuṣṇa-tīkṣṇa-rūkṣa-vidāhinaḥ
ākhyāta-artha-bhāvanā vyāpāra-rūpā vyāpāriṇamākāṃkṣate
śeṣāṇi rūpyakāṇi api ahaṃ loka-sevā-maṇḍalāya eva preṣayāmi eṣāṃ rūpyakāṇām ahaṃ kiṃ kariṣye
śānti-karma-ucitam gṛham
tad-pratītau eva tad-pratītiḥ tad-na-pratītau tad-na-pratītiḥ itiaṃśamādāya dṛṣṭāntaḥ saṃgacchate
śārdūlasiṃhaḥ tu valgām ākṛṣya jala-bhrama-pari-jihīrṣayā kiñcit apasṛtya tiryag gantum iyeṣa
anvaya-nirūpita tvena śakti-hetu tāyāḥ na-aṅgīkāreṇa tad-bhedena nānā-artha-tva-āpatteḥ na-sambhavāt
iti a-sātmya-indriya-artha-saṃyogaḥ prajñāparādhaḥ
iti bhūṣaṇa-sāra-granthaḥ spaṣṭamevaācaṣṭe tiṅ-anta-rahitam api vākyam
mahat-ātmā gorakṣanāthaḥ sva-tapasyā-phalaṃ dātuṃ yogya-pātram anviṣyan kāśīṃ prāptaḥ
rājan-kumāra aham asmi sva-laghu-rājyasya rājā
apabhraṃśāt go-ādi-rūpa-artha-bodhe api gāvī-śabdāt bodhaḥ bhavatu
ekasmin eva māse āskara tathā bhārataratna-puraskāraṃ prāpya tena citra-paṭa-sṛṣṭyām adbhutaḥ itihāsaḥ nirmitaḥ
prati-śākhā-bhedena hi na-antāḥ ca buddhayaḥ
na-itara-sādhāraṇena brāhmeṇa tejasā samujjvalan pīta-ambara-dhārī
tri-divasa-anantaraṃ pratyāgantuṃ sva-patnīṃ nācammāṃ pratiśrutya sa gatavānāsīt
tāsāṃ mūrtīnāṃ madhye āsīnaḥ mūrti-pratimaḥ mūrti-kāraḥ cirābhyastahastābhyāṃ dṛṣadi ākāra-pra-dāne vyastaḥ āsīt
viṣayatā-mātra-saṃsargatve pāka-na-niṣpatti-sthale pacatiiti prayoga-āpattiḥ
mṛga-vṛtti-karma tāyāḥ saṃsargatayā bhānāt na mṛga-padāt dvitīyā-āpattiḥ
gandhāḥca aguru-patra-ādyā dhūmaṃ mūrdha-virecane
teṣāṃ guṇānām upayogaḥ kathaṃ sva-rāṣṭra-rakṣaṇaṃ kartuṃ śakyate iti sarvaṃ pratāpena teṣu aṣṭa-varṣeṣu jñātam
nir-aparādha-janatāyāḥ ca hatyā kiṃ naitikaṃ karma asti
atha nirdiṣṭa-dine yajñadattena saha kahoḍaḥ śāstra-carcā-arthaṃ rāja-sabhāṃ prāptaḥ
rāṇāpratāpena aṅgīkṛtāṃ raṇa-nītiṃ prajā-anurañjanam api agre gatvā chatrapatiśivāji-mahat-rājaḥ api nityam anusṛtavān
mahāt-rājaḥ aicchat yat vartamāna-nyāya-vyavasthāyāṃ prācīna-nyāya-praṇālyāḥ uttamāḥ aṃśāḥ sammilitāḥ bhaveyuḥ
tatyathā dāha-auṣṇya-pāka-sveda-kleda-kotha-kaṇḍū-srāva-rāgāḥ yathā-svaṃ ca gandha-varṇa-rasa-abhinirvartanaṃ pittasya karmāṇi
yuvakaḥ ca anya-dvāreṇa vāṭikām prati vi-nir-gata
tasmāt tuṣāra-samaye snigdha-amla-lavaṇān rasān
upapatteḥ ca sat-asat-ādi-śabdaiḥ brahma na ucyate iti
kāla-adhvan-deśānām na-karmanka-kriyā-yoge kaiścit karman-pratyaya-artham vibhāṣayā karmatvamanuśiṣyate
tasmāt samāsasya prātipadika-saṃjñā-siddhaye śakti-svīkāraḥ āvaśyakaḥ
kiñcit dūraṃ gatvā pannaḥ sva-vāhaka-gardabhaṃ sthāpayitvā gardabhān gaṇayāmāsa
sa-kṣaudraḥ ca abhayā-prāśaḥ prāyaḥ rūkṣa-anna-sevanam
atha vā kṛtam atyanta-vigarhita-dainya-avalambena
siṃha-tvag-bhṛt kopi siṃhaḥ na bhavati
ataḥ saḥ anantaraṃ viraha-agni-madhye dināni yāpayati sma
mahat-rāja asti punaḥ jñāyate kevalam putra-saṃkṣaya-kārakaḥ kula-vigrahaḥ bhaviṣyati iti
śakram pṛccha purā nivātakavaca-prāṇa-upahāra-arcitam
pārśva-stham eva cala-citra-gṛham āsīt
mārga-āyāsa-parihāra-artham tām śraddhayā śṛṇotu tāvat iti
guru-laghu-śīta-uṣṇa-snigdha-rūkṣa-ādīnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ sāmānya-viśeṣābhyāṃ vṛddhi-hrāsau
āryaputra-virahitā rākṣasa-rāja-bhavanam ānītā na-iṣṭāni na-arhāṇi yathā-manoratha-pravṛttāni vacanāni śrāvyamāṇā jīvāmi manda-bhāgā
bhagaṇa-yavanikāḥ taḍit-pannagī-vāsa-valmīka-bhūtāḥ nabhas-mārga-rūḍha-kṣupāḥ
ādhi-vyādhi-dhsparītāpāt adya śvaḥ vā vināśine
vibhāvinī kadāpi sva-jananī-bhrātrā-ādīnām carcā api karttum na aśaknot
kasmin khalu prakupitaḥ kamala-āyata-akṣaḥ
svīyasya udyānasya koṇe tasyāḥ śarīraṃ nikhāya pratyāgatau dampatī su-dīrgha-kālaṃ yāvat kiṅkartavyatāmūḍhatvam anubhūtavantau
evaṃ rūpa-guṇa-cāritryasya ekā kathā prakhyātā
naapi pāṇini-saṃketa-sambandhena sup-pada vattvam
antaḥ ca manasaḥ prati-pakṣa-bhāvanayā rāga-ādi-malānām apanayanam śaucam
śikṣitasya api tasyā pituḥ ā-jīvikāyā dṛḍhaādhāra bhāvāt kṛchrena ayāpayat sā sva-bālya-avasthām
sūryaḥ sva-bhāva-rucimān iva bhāti karṇaḥ
śatru-parābhavaḥ iti-ādi-viṣayān punaḥ ācāryaḥ pāṭhitavān
upaśāntaḥ saḥ kathaṃ bandipaṇḍitasya vaśīkṛtaḥ kathaṃ krūreṇa tena mama patiḥ jale majjitaḥ janaka-mahat-rājaḥ brahma-jñānī iti samastaḥ lokaḥ praśaṃsati
madya-māṃsa-ucitānāṃ ca madyamevaanuśasyate
ikṣu-kāṇḍekṣu-ikṣuvālikā-puṇḍraka-caturthāḥ kāṇḍa-āsavāḥ bhavanti
aditim na-eka-vāram aham apṛccham manuṣyā svabhāvena skhalana-śīlā jāyante
tathā krīḍituṃ sva-śarīra-vakratva-kāraṇāt na-śaktaḥ aṣṭāvakraḥ maharṣeḥ aṅke upaviṣṭaḥ kevalaṃ darśanena ānandati sma
tava vara-guṇa-cintā-vīta-lāvaṇya-līlam
tataḥ saḥ kośa-adhikāriṇam ādiśat caturdaśānām varṣāṇām kṛte sītāyai yāvat apekṣitam tāvat bhūṣaṇa-śāṭikā-ādikam preṣayatu iti
adya punaḥ madīya-āvāsāt caturtha-talīya-kakṣyāyā svakīya-ālinde sthitaḥ aham prativeśa-sthe tasmin bhavane na-āyāsam eva dṛṣṭi-pātam akārṣam
aparatra ākhyāta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kam ca bodhamupapādayanti
ekadā meṣa-pālena kenāpi kāryeṇa saptan-aha-avadhi kvacit gantavyam āsīt
tathā ca madhya-sthita-taddhitasya pacataki iti bhāgasya prātipadika-saṃjñā syātiti vācyam
eṣāeva saraṇiḥādṛtā bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ kāṣṭham bhasma kriyate ityatra bhasma-pada-uttaram dvitīyā-vāraṇe
prājña-ajñayoḥ viśeṣaḥca svastha-ātura-hitaṃ ca yat
adhiyajñaḥ sarva-yajña-abhimāninī viṣṇu-ākhyā devatā
ghaṭa-nirūpita tvena śakti-avagāhi-jñānāt eva śābda-bodhaḥ iti śakti-jñāna-niṣṭha-kāraṇatāyām viṣayatayāavacchedakatvam ghaṭa-ādeḥ eva naanvayasya
raktapitta-atisāra-ghnaṃ kṣaya-kāsa-jvara-apaham
śāstreṇa api brāhmaṇa-ādīnām sattva-ādi-guṇa-viśeṣa-apekṣayā eva śama-ādīni karmāṇi pravibhaktāni
sva-niṣṭha-karaṇatā-nirūpakau
tasmāt prathama-gṛhītā anvate śaktiḥ anya-labhya-tva-lāghava-tarkābhyām tyajyate
aham punaḥ nitya-śuddha-buddha-mukta-svabhāvatvāt na-āvaraṇa-jñāna-śaktiḥ iti veda aham he param-tapa
śoka-upavāsa-vyāyāma-rūkṣa-śuṣka-alpa-bhojanaiḥ
tad-prāmāṇikatvam ca eka-artha-bhāva-vādin-mate
na ca prathamam anvita-artha-jñāne sākṣāt kāraṇatvam gṛhītamiti tad-virodhaḥ iti vācyam
śalya-cikitsā-ālayam dṛṣṭvā saḥ ayam su-mahat-āścarya-cakitaḥ atiṣṭhat
aye ayaṃ mahat-rājaḥ mahatī-devyā sumitrayā ca suduḥsahamapi putra-viraha-samudbhavaṃ śokaṃ ni-gṛhya ātmānaṃeva saṃsthāpayantībhyāmanvāsyamānaḥ tiṣṭhati
na ca tarhi vārtika-ādau pada-artha-jñāne smaraṇa-vyavahāraḥ tatra tatra kathamupapadyata iti vācyam
sevyaiḥ pradhāna-guṇa-karma-phalaiḥ nimittaiḥ
sapta-varṣa-anantaram saḥ tatra samāyāta
avimārakaḥ bhaye api yadi tādṛśam nayana-pātra-peyam vapuḥ
tadā vaikuṇṭheśvara-mahat-ṛṣiḥ ām
te ca prakṛti-saṃbhavāḥ bhagavat-māyā-saṃbhavāḥ nibadhnanti iva he mahat-bāho
sa-bala-yoṣitaḥ tapas-balam vilokya haṭhāt eva stambhita saṃsāra
saubhrātra-vyavasita-lakṣmaṇa-anuyātram
liyū pratijñām cakāra sva-vacanasya pari-pūrti-artham
damayantī amba mat-pati-devaḥ yāvatmāṃ parigṛhṇāti
budhanyā pati-kalyāṇa-kāmanām
śābda-dhī-prayojakaḥ bodhya-bodhaka-saṃbandhaḥ vṛttiḥ
samaḥ mokṣaḥ gatimatāṃ vāyoḥ karma a-vikāra-jam
vṛtti-hetoḥ bhiṣak-māna-pūrṇān mūrkha-viśāradān
taiḥ asthibhiḥ ekaṃ bhayaṅkara-vajra-āyudhasya nirmāṇaṃ kurvantu
skandha-uccāraṇa-namyamāna-vadana-pracyoti-toye ghaṭe
tatra kā paridevanā kaḥ vā pralāpaḥ na-dṛṣṭa-dṛṣṭa-pranaṣṭa-bhrānti-bhūteṣu bhūteṣu ityarthaḥ
timira-gahana-bhīmam vartate ca ardha-rātram
prajāpatiḥātmanaḥ vapāmudakhidat iti-ādi-arthavādānām ivaasyaapi sva-arthe prāmāṇya-abhāvasya iṣṭatvāt
pada-bodhyaḥ śakyaḥ pada-artha-bodhyaḥ lakṣyaḥ iti tāntrika-maryādā
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat aye rājan bhavān āstikaḥ uta na āstikaḥ iti eva na jñāyate mayā
ārakṣiṇaḥ tatra upetya ajā-sahitāṃ mālā-kāra-patnīm anayan
ghaṭatva-karmatvasya tu lakṣya-kriyā-niṣṭha-saṃsarga-anubhavam prati sākṣāt janaka-jñāna-viṣaya-tva-rūpam lakṣakatvam bodhyam
na ca tatra nitya-agnihotra-rūpa-vācya-artha-sādṛśyena gauṇyā vṛttyā karman-viśeṣe agni-hotra-śabda-pravṛtteḥ upapatteḥ na tatra śaktiḥ kalpyate iti vācyam
rākeśena uktam astiyat daśa-dina-anantaram tvam parāvartiṣyase atra
jhillī-jhaṅkāra-nāditā gabhirā araṇyānī
pācakāḥ tu dūṣita-antaraṅgā anna-ku-arthanām vidadhati
na-ati-bahu-āśinaḥ caeva mṛdu-koṣṭhāḥ tathaiva ca
vyutpatti-antara-kalpanā-apekṣayā
bhavataḥ hāva-bhāva-ādi kam
vyaṅgya-artha-garbhita tvāteva mahat-kavīnām vāṇī sarvataḥ vijayate
anyathā na-eka-kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-kalpanā-gauravāt
vidvad-jana-sannipātaṃ caabhisamīkṣya pratibhayamiva kāntāram adhva-gāḥ pariharanti dūrāt
agni-sākṣi-pūrvakam kāñcit pariṇīya tām tiraḥ-kṛtya anyām pariṇayati
tasyām ghaṭa-śābda-dhī tvasya sattvāt ghaṭatva-dhī-nirūpita-śakti tvenaeva śakti-jñānam kāraṇam lāghavāt na tu saṃbandha-ādi-nirūpita-śakti tvena gauravāt
duḥkham iti eva yat karma kāya-kleśa-bhayāt tyajet
tataḥ sva-harmyam gatvā smara-ākula-matiḥ tasyāḥ kṛte dūtīm preṣitavān
adya aṣṭamaḥ divasaḥ āsīt para-loka-gamana-divasaḥ
kṣetra-kṣetrajña-saṃyogaḥ īdṛśaḥ bhūta-kāraṇam iti āha
mayāuktam sarva-śāstrārtha-pāragaḥ sarvajñaḥ nāma cakravākaḥ
sa-dhātuḥ iti tṛtīyā-arthe prathamā iti tad-bhāṣya-kāraḥ nirūpayati
evam tad-kāle buddhi-siddha-aṅkura-utpattiḥ jāyate iti vākyena bodhyate iti na kaḥapi doṣaḥ
adhunā tu tad-jñāna-sādhana-gaṇam na-mānitva-ādi-lakṣaṇam
vastutaḥtu pada-janyam pada-artha-jñānam smṛti-anubhava-vilakṣaṇam eva svīkriyate
rāmasya tu viśāla-akṣī pūrṇa-indu-sadṛśa-ānanā
vārtikam dṛṣṭvā sūtra-kṛtaḥ apravṛtteḥ na tum-arthāt iti sūtra-na-upapattiḥ api
saḥ mūkasya kṛte guḍa-svāda-varṇanam iva āsīt
atha kanaka-sūtra-anusaraṇa-pravṛttaiḥ rājan-puruṣaiḥ tatra taru-koṭare kṛṣṇa-sarpaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vyāpāditaḥca
yadā kadā pradhāna-cikitsakena kaścana sahāyaka-drāktaraḥ vraṇa-parīkṣā-ādi kartum preṣyate sma
vistīrṇa-rāja-bhavana-āpaṇa-gopura-aṭṭām
vāmanasya vacana-anusāreṇa bali-rājaḥ bhūmi-dāna-arthaṃ haste jalapātraṃ gṛhītavān
saḥayam an-upaśayāt pañcavidhaḥ trividha-vikalpaḥ bhavati a-sātmya-indriya-artha-saṃyogaḥ
bhaṭṭācāryāḥcaime śābdika-kṛte karman-kāraka-vibhajane na-svarasaṃ manvānāḥ prakāra-antareṇa vibhāgam kurvanti
tatyānā yāvat śaśaka-pāśa-pārśvam āgacchati tadā paśyati yat tasmāt pāśāt ścūkā nirgatā
kroda-uddhūta-halāt pralambamathanād bhītena mucyeta vā
om iti uktavati ca śreṣṭhin-varye param na-santoṣam iva anvababhūvu vyavasthāpaka vipra-vara kārpaṇya-avatāra śreṣṭhitā-kalaṅka-svarūpa kapardimallaḥ ca
nairantaryeṇa bhagavat-karma-ādau yathā-ukte arthe samāhitāḥ santaḥ pravṛttāḥ ityarthaḥ
na-apekṣitām amanyatāsau budhanīm sva-gārhasthya-paridhau
dhīrasya āśrama-saṃ-śritasya vasataḥtuṣṭasya vanyaiḥ phalaiḥ māna-arhasya
ceṭī avihavākaraṇaṃ ṇāma a-vidhavā-karaṇaṃ nāma
karmatva-arthaka-dvitīyāyāḥ ādheyatva-vāci-tā-vādin-naiyāyika-paddhatim adhyāste
naṣṭam niśā-cara-kulam punaḥ uddhariṣye
tathā puṇyānām na-ārabdha-phalānām syāt saṃbhavaḥ
bhartṛdārikā ca lajjā-bhaya-madanaiḥ abhitāḍyamānā santāpena mugdhā apagata-cetanā iva saṃvṛttā
icchā-dveṣa-samutthena dvandva-mohena bhārata
tayoḥ ca sarva-karma-saṃnyāsa-pūrvakāt ātman-jñānāt na anyataḥ nivṛttiḥ iti tat upadidikṣuḥ sarva-loka-anugraha-artham arjunam nimittai-kṛtya āha bhagavān vāsudevaḥ na-śocyān gītā
śatru-rājebhyaḥ sva-rājya-rakṣaṇaṃ
grahaṇī-arśaḥ-vikāra-ghnam arditā-aruci-nāśanam
tri-koṭi-saṅkhyākāḥ devāḥ vānara-rūpam prāptavantaḥ āsan
sahasā tatra śveta-aśva-saṃyuta śveta-ratha samupasthita
tathā caupasthite tad-tad-jñāne eva padasya kāraṇatāmavadhāvayati
dharma-adharma-supuṣpaḥ ca sukha-duḥkha-phala-udayaḥ
vāk-manas-atītam brahmā api bahavaḥ vāk-viṣaya tām nayanti
na bāla-vṛddha-lubdha-mūrkha-kliṣṭa-klībaiḥ saha sakhyaṃ kuryāt
śruta-dṛṣṭa-kriyā-kāla-mātrā-jñāna-bahiṣkṛtāḥ
idam tu pūrva-kathā-prasaṃgena uktam asmābhiḥ yad ayam mohana kevalam prativeśina suvarṇa-kārasya gṛham antarā na kutrāpi gacchati sma iti
cikitsā-sūtra mātraṃ ca siddhi-vyāpatti-saṃśrayam
evaṃ jīmūtavāhanena sva-prāṇa-tyāgaṃ kṛtvā sarpāṇāṃ jīvana-rakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam
etat niśamya rājan-puruṣau kiṃ kartavya-vi-mūḍhau jātau
tatra su-gama-mārgāṇām nirmāṇam api akurvan kuddālikayā
ityatra asti-pada-adhyāhāraḥ api naāvaśyakaḥ
gadādhara-bhaṭṭācāryāt arvācīna-paṇḍita-racita-grantheṣu uktam nyāya-siddhāntam pratipādayanti
teṣām ahaṃ sama uddhartā mṛtyu-saṃsāra-sāgarāt
tasmāt paṅka-ja-padāt padmatva-viśiṣṭa-upasthitaye tad-padasya tatra śaktiḥiva samāsa-padanām api tatra tatraarthe śaktiḥāvaśyakī
sa-snehaṃ dīpanaṃ vṛṣyamuṣṇaṃ vāta-kapha-apaham
kiṃcittataḥ laghutaraṃ śiśire kapha-vāta-jit
sva-jāmātṛ-rājyam draṣṭum icchāmi
prabhūta-kaṭu-yuktāni tasya āsye gālayetmuhuḥ
rājasūya-yajña-anantaraṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ sāmarthyaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍava-viṣayiṇī dveṣa-bhāvanā tasya manasi adhikā dṛḍhā jātā
vikrośanti na-vaśāt iva ucchrita-guhā-vyātta-ānanāḥ parvatāḥ
bhagavān bho rājan vṛṣṇi-pāṇḍava-nāthasya abhimanyoḥ pūjāṃ bhayātiti lokaḥ jñāsyati
tayoḥ siddhi-na-siddhyoḥ api samaḥ tulyaḥ bhūtvā kuru karmāṇi
śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-yuktaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ dhruvasya śirasi hastaṃ sthāpayan uktavān vatsa dhruva
niśi vicaranti sa-rāga-lobha-mohāḥ
rujā-varṇa-samutthāna-sthāna-saṃsthāna-nāmabhiḥ
utkṣiptām sa-anukampam salila-nidhi-jalāt eka-daṃṣṭra-agra-rūḍhām
kākebhyaḥ dadhi rakṣatāmityatra dadhi-upaghātaka-mātre kākatva-āropaḥ
caitraḥ na pacati ityatra pacati-pratipādya-pāka-viśiṣṭa-kṛteḥ nañ-artha-abhāve
aham tāvat vañcitaḥ kūṭa-kapaṭa-śīlayā
bālakaḥ prabhāte samudra-upa-kaṇṭhe vyavasāya-sthalam prāpa yatra pūrvataḥ eva vyavasāyī tam pratīkṣate sma
pāka-anukūla-kṛti māncaitraḥ iti prathamā-anta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kaḥ bodhaḥ
nīla-rūpe śaktasya nīla-padasya tad-viśiṣṭe lakṣaṇām svīkṛtyaeva abheda-anvaya-bodha-nirvāhaḥ iti nauktasya karmadhāraya-prayojaka tvamiti vācyam
mitraiḥ dattam dvitīya-vivāha-prastāvam etat-artham eva asau na anumene
sā tebhyaḥ ānanda-vārtām ānītavadbhyaḥ ratna-vajra-ādikam vitīrṇavatī
ataḥ vāṇijya-vyavahāra-jñāne tau viśeṣa-kutūhala inau jātau
imām sāgara-paryantām himavat-vindhya-kuṇḍalām
na kevalaṃ gṛha-kṛtya-ādi-viṣayān
kalā-kārāḥ tiṅ-artha-nirūpaṇa-avasare svayam khaṇḍana-yuktibhiḥ bheda-prapañcasya māyikatvam vistareṇa nirūpya
mām ekam sarva-ātmānam samam sarva-bhūta-sthitam īśvaram acyutam garbha-janma-jarā-maraṇa-varjitam aham eva ityevam śaraṇam vraja
imām gṛhṇīṣva rāja-indra sarva-loka-namaskṛtām
parantu kriyā-kāraka-saṃsarga-avagāhī śābda-bodhaḥ kāryatā-viṣayakaḥ
bhaṭaḥ jayatu mahā-rājaḥ sajjāḥ khalu rathāḥ nagara-praveśa-abhimukhāya
kāmāḥ ca sarve śrauta-smārta-karmaṇām phalāni
vidyāt pitta-mada-āviṣṭaṃ rakta-pīta-asita-ākṛtim
yata-citta-ātmā cittam antaḥkaraṇam ātmā bāhyaḥ kārya-karaṇa-saṃghātaḥ tau ubhau api yatau saṃyatau yena saḥ yata-citta-ātmā
ataḥ abheda-prakāraka-bodhaḥ eva svīkartumucitaḥ iti vācyam
yatantaḥ ca indriya-upasaṃhāra-śama-dama-dayā-hiṃsā-ādi-lakṣaṇaiḥ dharmaiḥ prayatantaḥ ca
laghu-ūṣṇa-tīkṣṇa-viśadaṃ rūkṣaṃ sūkṣmaṃ kharaṃ saram
sarvam api padārtha-jātam jaṭhara-koṣa-āgāre sa-rabhasam nyakṣipyat
dvitīyasmin eva dine vyāpārāya daśa-pañcadaśa-varṣebhyaḥ videśe kṛta-pravāsaḥ tasyāḥ patiḥ rātrau pratinivṛttaḥ
phegā api pautrayoḥ yoga-kṣema-viṣaye itopi datta-avadhānā abhavat
tat-vidya-sevā vijñānam ātmā-ādīnāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
caitraḥ pacatiiti vākyam tu ākhyāta-artha-kṛti-prakārakam samavāya-saṃsargakam bodham janayati
etathi maraṇāyaathavā bala-varṇa-tejaḥ-vīrya-uparodhāya a-laghu-vyādhaye ṣāṇḍhyā caiti
teṣām śāsanam prajā-hita-artham eva āsīt
tulye nindātmasaṃstutī yasya yateḥ saḥ tulya-nindā-ātman-saṃstutiḥ
evam sthite api bhavataḥ kārya-sādhanā-icchā tu na kṣīṇā
ārogya-rakṣā-pravidhau prajānām
spaṣṭamcaidamabhihitam siddhānta-lakṣaṇa-vicāra-śeṣe darśitamca niyama-na-ghaṭitam saṃbandhatvam iti dīdhiti-vyākhyāna-avasare śrī-gadādhara-bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ
etādṛśam kāryam kartum kim bhavataḥ lajjā na bhavati kṣatriya-kula-jātāḥ kadā api kārya-sādhanā-artham vāma-mārgam na āśrayanti
aśvattha-udumbara-plakṣa-nyagrodhānāṃ phalāni ca

na-tula-śakti-sampannaḥ
kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-kalpanā-lāghavena bhāvanā-mukhya-viśeṣya-ke bodhe siddhe
sainyānāṃ śauryaṃ dṛṣṭvā ete sainikāḥ raghu-mahat-rājasya eva iti jñāyate sma

janma-bandha-vinirmuktāḥ padam gacchanti anāmayam

na ca strī-liṅga-viśiṣṭa-kṛti-bodhakasya praśnasya tādṛśa-liṅga-viśiṣṭa-kṛti-bodhakam evauttaram
tasyāḥ sva-rājya-svapna-pūrti-artham eva mahat-rājena sva-jīvanaṃ samarpitam āsīt
samaya-anusāreṇa tasyāḥ svayamvara-yojana-arthaṃ cintitavān mahat-rājaḥ
saḥ yadā kadā viśeṣa-kārya-vaśāt rājan-sabhāyām agacchat
anna-pāna-indhanaiḥ caagniḥjvalati vyeti caanyathā
pañcaviṃśatim aśva-ārohān ca sva-rathasya pṛṣṭhata nītvā tasya eva sahasraliṅga-saras-tīram jagāma
guru-ūṣṇa-snigdha-madhurāḥ bala-upacaya-vardhanāḥ
tat-na-sattve sarva-abhāva-prasaṅgaḥ iti cet
aham caṇḍa-pravāta-laṇḍitaḥ iva varaṇḍaḥ parvatāt dūram āropya pātitaḥ asmi
prayoktuḥapi tad-samāna-viṣayakaḥ prayoga-hetu-bhūtaḥ śakyatā-avacchedaka-āropaḥ itiāśayena śakyatā-avacchedaka-āropaḥ lakṣaṇā iti grantha-antare vyavahāraḥ upapadyate
maharṣi-ramaṇaṃ kiṃ kurvantaṃ girijā-gṛha-svāminaḥ apaśyan
mumukṣoḥ sarva-karma-saṃnyāsa-vidhānāt
vartamāna-kāla-ika-bhāvanā iti bodhaḥ
sarvam mudrā-dvayam sa-arddha-paṇa-pañcakam ca jātam
kāryakrama-samāpane sampūrṇa-kakṣa kara-tala-dhvanibhi guñjita
ataḥ nārada-garva-bhaṅgāya viṣṇuḥ udyuktaḥ abhavat
ajñānam ca na-viveka-jñānam kartavya-na-kartavya-ādi-viṣaya-mithyā-pratyayaḥ
khānayetśayanasyaadhaḥ karṣūṃ sthāna-vibhāga-vit
na japa-homa-adhyayana-bali-maṅgala-kriyāsu śleṣma-siṅghāṇakaṃ muñcet
kuṇṭhā tu sva-pārśva-sthānāt tīvra-dhārām churikām niṣkāsya
nāman-ākhyāta-upasarga-nipātāḥ
vismaraṇaśīla bhulakkaḍa pramoda prati-aham eva pānthavāse hoṭala svīyam nivāsa-pra-koṣṭhakam vismarati sma
evameva kavīnām artha-viśeṣa-varṇanā-rūpaḥ vākya-sandarbhaḥ api dṛśyate
bhṛti-karmaṇi vartamānasya ya mahān kleśaḥ tat-leśaḥ api yadṛcchā upanatam anna-ādi-phala-ādi vā yathā-iccham bhuñjānasya kāle śayānasya me na asti
paraṃ te kadācit vipat-jāla-badhdāḥ
apare tu prayoktuḥ abhiprāya-viśeṣa-jñāne lakṣya-tīra-ajñānāt avaśyam jñeyaḥ
droṇaḥ kathaṃ dharma-vañcanā iti mā tāvat bho gāndhāra-viṣaya-vismita śakune
purāṇe ca varṇinām āśramiṇām ca loka-phala-bheda-viśeṣa-smaraṇāt
janma-pradhvaṃsābhyām prāk ūrdhvam ca na-upalabdheḥ kāryasya ghaṭa-ādeḥ mṛt-ādi-kāraṇasya ca tat-kāraṇa-vyatirekeṇa na-upalabdheḥ na-sattvam
na na-pramāṇa-buddhyā gṛhyamāṇāyāḥ karman-hetutva-upapattiḥ
na hi sva-ātma-viṣayam dveṣam ākāṅkṣām vā paraḥ paśyati
staḥ ityatra tīratvena bhāsamānasyaapi tīrasya mīna-anvayi-pravāha-upasthāpaka-gaṅgā-padena evaupasthāpitatvāt tad-anvaye api dvandva-sādhutā-nirvāhāt
evam ca sarvatra janyatāyām tad-tad-viṣayaka-tva-avacchinna-tva-avagāhi-śakti-bhramāt śābda-bodha-kalpanam na-samañjasam
kārya-vidhi-jñaḥ niścintaḥ
śiṣyeṇa api sarvam daṇḍa-kamaṇḍalu-ādikam uttārya skandhakarpaṭena proñchitau pādau

etat niśamya krodha-vihvalaḥ bhū-paḥ ādiśat yat udyānasya kṣati-pūrtaye tenālīrāmaḥ pañca sahasraṃ svarṇa-mudrāḥ arpayatu gāvaḥ ca rājakīya-paśu-śālāyāṃ preṣyantām
evañca smārakatvena klṛptābhyām gaṅgā-pada-pravāhābhyām eva śābda-bodha-upayoginyāḥ tīra-upasthiteḥ sambhavāt
antata sat-na-sat-viveka-nipuṇaḥ api sthavira vatsām eva nirṇetum ājñāpayat
sāeṣā naḥ mahat-rāja-mātaraṃ mahat-devīm āśrama-sthām abhi-gamya anujñātā tatrabhavatyā rāja-gṛham eva yāsyati
na-sat-kārya-vāda-nirūpaṇa-avasare buddhi-siddham tu tadasat nyā
saṃnyāsī udatarat he puṇya-ātman mama kāma-krodha-ādayaḥ bandhu-janāḥ mṛtāḥ
svalpe eva samaye sa-aśru-nayanā devara-patnī āgatya sva-bharttuḥ dur-ācārāya tāṃ kṣamāṃ yācitavatī
parantu na-nirīkṣita-rūpeṇa bhadravarmā api tayā saha nadī-vihāra-artham prasthitavān āsīt
mahāmattottarāuhīāhiṭṭhido paccuggado so kidaahatthī tataḥ kaṇṭhīrava-pari-jñāna-nimittaṃ pari-vṛttāḥ ca vayam
kīdṛśasya maharghasya dhūma-vartikā-prakārasya
pradhāna-rājñī-rūpe asmin prāsāde sa-sukham jīvana-yāpanam kuru
lakṣa-patiḥ hāram vinā eva sva-gṛham vi-nir-gata
yaḥ nava-yukti-vi-cintana-caturaḥ
itaḥ pūrvam eva lakṣmaṇaḥ śeṣa-śayyā-rūpam sītā lakṣmī-rūpam ca prāpya viṣṇoḥ āgamanam pratīkṣamāṇau āstām
yaḥ api deha-ādi-vyatirikta-ātma-vādī ātmānam eva kevalam kartāram paśyati
sneha-pūra-kaṇṭhena avādīt tat kim mām parīkṣitum samāgata rājan
tenālī taṃ sva-gṛhe māsa-catuṣṭayam asthāpayat prati-dinaṃ sūryanārāyaṇasya purataḥ aṣṭa-aṅga-praṇipāta-pūrvaṃ daṇḍavat praṇāmaṃ kartuṃ niradiśat
taṃ madhura-amla-lavaṇa-snigdha-uṣṇaiḥ upakramaiḥupakrameta
rasa-asṛk-māṃsa-medaḥ-jān doṣān hanti bibhītakam
idam tu kāryakrama-āyojana-svarūpeṇa niścīyate
na ca nadī-pada-śakya-arthasya tīre sākṣāt sambandhaḥasti
śābdika-ratna-ākaraḥ
na-vyakta-ādīni na-vyaktam na-darśanam na-upalabdhiḥ ādiḥ yeṣām bhūtānām putra-mitra-ādi-kārya-karaṇa-saṃghāta-ātmakānām tāni na-vyakta-ādīni bhūtāni prāk utpatteḥ
teṣāṃ tu mala-prasāda-ākhyānāṃ dhātūnāṃ srotāṃsi ayana-mukhāni
tat etat ubhayam agni-somau sarvam iti paśyataḥ anna-doṣa-lepaḥ na bhavati
iti śrīmad-bhagavadgītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde dhyāna-yogaḥ nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ
gṛha-kārya-jātam api kṛtvā mātu sāhāyyam karoti
navya-naiyāyika-na-abhimatam api apabhraṃśānām vācakatvam nyāya-sūtra-bhāṣya-kārayoḥ abhimatameva
samāsasya na-śakta tve citra-gum ānaya iti-ādau dvitīyā-artha-karma tvena citra-go-svāminaḥ anvayaḥ na syāt
yadyapi bauddha-bāhyayoḥ abheda-adhyāsaḥ bauddha-artha-vādibhiḥ svīkṛtaḥ
na tu vivekinām anyaḥ aham deha-ādi-saṃghātāt iti jānatām tat-kāle deha-ādi-saṃghāte aham-pratyayaḥ bhavati
dina-dvaya-prayāṇaṃ kṛtvā kahoḍaḥ uddālaka-āśramaṃ prāptavān
śakya-artha-jñāna-abhāvena śakya-saṃbandha-rūpa-lakṣaṇā-graha-na-sambhavāt
niṣadhān gatvā akṣa-hṛdaya-vidyayā puṣkaraṃ jitvā punaḥ asmad-rājyaṃ prāpnumaḥ
dāna-uddeśyaka-tva-saṃbandhena pākasya bhāvanāyām anvaya-svīkārāt
utpanna-samyak-darśanasya karman-yoga-abhāva-vacanāt
svapneapi utpanna-sa-sparśaḥ roma-harṣaṃ na muñcati
nanu vākya-artha-avagamam prati abhidhīyamāna-pada-arthasya karaṇatve pada-arthasya atirikta-pramāṇa-tva-āpattiḥ
daśānām lakāra-artham ca nirṇīya tiṅ-anta-nirūpaṇam samāpitam
aneke yahūdyāḥ isrel-gamana-vicāraṃ kurvantaḥ santi saḥ uktavān
tava gamane mama maraṇam bhaviṣyati iti pratyayaḥ maraṇam vinā punarjanman-na-sambhavāt
atha svayaṃ-kṛtā-aparādhena agni-dagdhaḥ abhūt
samāja-saṅghaṭana-upadeṣṭṛn pari-hasanta eva yāpayanti kālam

naapi uttara-vṛtti-tva-pūrva-vṛtti-tva-anyatara-sambandhena prakṛti-viśiṣṭa tvam
anya-na-iṣṭa-cikīrṣuḥ nā sva-na-iṣṭaṃ samupekṣate
yatra ekasmin vākya-arthe paryavasanne vākya-artha-antara-bodhaḥ tatraeva vākya-bhedaḥ
vicāra-dhārāṃ ca saḥ citra-paṭa-sṛṣṭyai pradattavān
saḥ abravīt paśya idānīṃ mama prakhara-kiraṇa-jālasya prabhāvam ityuktvā bhāsvaraḥ bhāskaraḥ pra-caṇḍābhiḥ bhābhiḥ sakalaṃ bhuvanaṃ didhakṣan iva didīpe
viveka-prakāśa-bhāve tad-abhāvāt
yajña-yāgādiṣu pradhāna-puro-hitaḥ bhūtvā tatra prāptayā dakṣiṇayā dhana-kanaka-dhānya-ādi-saṅgraham api avardhayat
dṛḍhayā vāṇyā sā uktavatī māṃsa-majjā-rakta-ādibhiḥ dhātubhiḥ yukte mānuṣe śarīre śucitvasya kā vārtā strī vā puruṣaḥ vā
ekaḥ adhyātma-mārga-janaḥ gīta-upadeśa-anusāreṇa māna-apamānayoḥ daśāyām api krodha-rahitaḥ bhavituṃ kaṭhināṃ sādhanāṃ kṛtavān
yatra yatra tat-citā-bhasma uḍḍīya gatam tatra ghṛṇā
adhunā vidyā-vinaya-sampannaḥ aṣṭāvakraḥ deha-saundaryeṇa api virājate sma
tat sukham sāttvikam proktam ātman-buddhi-prasāda-jam
evaṃ bali-rājaḥ sva-vacana-pālana-arthaṃ vāmanāya sva-rājyam ayacchat
karman-yoga-niṣṭhāyāḥ parama-rahasyam īśvara-śaraṇatām upasaṃhṛtya
rājadhānīm upetya tena mantrī ādiṣṭaḥ yat rājyasya pramukha-rājan-mārgāṇāṃ samīpe lauha-jālena ācchāditānāṃ kūpānāṃ nirmāṇaṃ kāryatām
anantaram eva rakṣā-sūtra-bandhanam kariṣyāmi
tyaja kula-gata-śaṅkām sādhyatām svam tam etat
na ca kevalaṃ hita-āhāra-upayogāt eva sarva-vyādhi-bhayam atikrāntaṃ bhavati
īśvara-arpaṇa-buddhyā anuṣṭhīyamānam ghaṭana-rūpam yoga-arthatvāt yogaḥ ucyate guṇataḥ
tasya vijayaḥ bhūyāt iti manasā āśāsānāḥ sva-sva-sthānāni gatāḥ
bāla-kṛṣṇaḥ manasi vyacārayatbrahmaṇā sva-māyā vi-ni-yojitā

bhakti-japa-arcanā-ādau bhagna-viśvāsaḥ asau ekasmin dine pāṣāṇe prakṣipya tāṃ pratimāṃ babhañja
prathamā-anta-viśeṣyakaḥ bodhaḥ
tat kāryaṃ tvarāṃ vinā yadyapi dvi-tra-dinebhyaḥ pūrvam api samāpayituṃ śakyam
āḍhakī kapha-pitta-ghnī vāta-lā kapha-vāta-nut
rāmasya ādeśasya anu-guṇam lakṣmaṇaḥ dvāra-rakṣaṇa-kārye pravṛttaḥ jātaḥ
tataḥ harṣa-kampita-śarīraḥ vividhābhiḥ bhāvanābhiḥ yugapat āveśyamānaḥ kathamapi ātmānaṃ samāśvāsya bandinaṃ pṛṣṭavān kimāha bhavān mama sutaḥ aṣṭāvakraḥ bhavantaṃ vāde parājitavān vā kvāsti saḥ taṃ draṣṭum utkaṇṭhate mama hṛdayam
kṣaṇena eva saḥ rājña sam-akṣam eva senā-pati-karavālam khaṇḍaśa kṛtavān
sītāpura-nagarasya vikraya-karā-dhikārī śrīmān ādarśadharaḥ āryaḥ nija-kārya-ālaye ekasya caturtha-śreṇī-karmacāriṇaḥ riktaṃ sthānaṃ pūrayituṃ pratyāśināṃ sākṣātkāraṃ karoti
janman-bandha-vinirmuktāḥ janma eva bandhaḥ janman-bandhaḥ tena vinirmuktāḥ jīvantaḥ eva janman-bandhāt vinirmuktāḥ santaḥ
parā-apare kṣetra-kṣetrajña-lakṣaṇe
tad-sādhikāyāḥ abhāva-ādi-sādhāraṇyāḥ bhāvanā iti anugata-pratīteḥ śapatha-eka-nirṇeya tvāt
tathā ca sarva-karma-saṃnyāsam vakṣyati sarva-karmāṇi manasā ityādinā
śuṣka-prāyam dhānya-kṣetram dhārā-sāra-varṣayā haritam sañjātam
kolaṃ kulatthāḥ suradāru-rāsnā-māṣā-tasī-tailaphalāni kuṣṭham
gām badhāna iti-ādau ānayana-na-pratītyā vyabhicārāt
jāti-abhidhāna-śaktāt vyaktau na-śaktāt padāt vyakteḥbhānam na yujyate na-samarthā na-śaktāt kārya-utpattau atiprasaṅgāt
na-paraḥ-para-sambhūtaṃ kim anyat kāmahaitukam
tad-paraḥ api na-jita-indriyaḥ syāt ityataḥ āha saṃyata-indriyaḥ
na-anyā-bhaktiḥ
yaḥ hi āditaḥ eva saṃnyasya karmāṇi jñāna-yoga-niṣṭhāyām pravṛttaḥ
jāti-svabhāva-paryālocanayā jāti-bhāsaka-sāmagryāḥ eva vyakti-jñāna-janaka-tva-aṅgīkārāt kāraṇa-abhāva-ukteḥ na-saṃgata tvāt
evaṃ kāyena vācā manasā kāryaṃ kṛtvā saḥ catur-daśa-vidyāsu pāraṅgataḥ abhavat
mātāmahyaḥ ca pālana-poṣaṇa-ādi-bhāraḥ samāpatitaḥ
dhātu-artha-mātram ca kāla-abhidhāna-viśiṣṭam
nityaṃ ca sama-citta tvam iṣṭa-na-iṣṭa-upapattiṣu
prati-rātram saḥ sva-sainya-balam viśramayitum ādideśa
guru-dakṣiṇā-arthaṃ yāvad āvaśyakaṃ tataḥ adhikaṃ kautsaḥ na icchati sma
tathā ca samāsa-ghaṭaka-pada-śakti-jñānam vinā viśiṣṭa-artha-bodhāt lakṣaṇayā viśiṣṭa-artha-bodha-nirvāhaḥ saṃbhavati
maunam sarva-artha-sādhanam
ataḥ bodha-janaka-tā-nirvāhaka-saṃbandhaḥ tattvena icchā-viṣaya tvamiti na kaḥapi doṣaḥ
dṛśi-dhātoḥ dhāvana-kartṛ-mṛga-karmanka-darśane
na-vinaya-viṣaye eva tasya na-sahanā āsīt
parāvṛttaṃ tīrtha-yātri-dalaṃ mahat-ātmane kim adadāt
satvaram mālākāram āhūya udyānasya sarvavidham-nāśa-kāraṇam apṛcchat
uraḥ mukulita-stanam jaghanam aṃsa-bandha-uddhuram
prakṛta-artha tvam ca na kevalam prakṛti-janya-upasthiti-viṣaya tvam
mohanasya kārāt muktim śrutvā tasya udāryam jānāna sva-aparādham ca manvānaḥ haradeva lajjayā avanata san kṣamā-yācanā-artham tat-samīpam āgata
sevakaḥ tasya anena vyavahāreṇa lajjitaḥ sva-kṛtye atīva paścāttapan punaḥ punaḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ caraṇayoḥ nipatya tataḥ sva-kṛta-aparādhāya kṣamām ayācata
vrata-prabhāveṇa śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-yuktaḥ śrīhariḥ tasyāḥ purataḥ pratyakṣībhūtaḥ
paryante tu te palāṇḍu-śalka-garbhe kimapi anyad na-āsādayanta iva viṣaṇṇāḥ capeṭa-tāḍitā bālakā iva nivartante
bhavane andhakāraḥ syāt prakāśaḥ vā parantu jānan api ka nu khalu viṣam bhuṅkte sa-patnī-rūpām durvāra-vipadam kā nu khalu ramaṇī prasahya āmantrayate iyam budhanī na akṣaram paricinoti
bhavanta paścimāyām diśi vaṃśa-vṛkṣa-kuñjeṣu sva-halāni prāpsyanti
yadi ca tatra saṃsarga-grahaḥ eva na jāyate parantu na-saṃsarga-na-grahaḥ evaitiucyate
daśamūlīśṛtā kāsa-hikkā-śvāsa-kapha-apahā
nirdhanena ṛṇa-svīkāra-cintā na karaṇīyā api iti
dīrgha-vartma-pariśrāntam nadīadrivanasaṃkulam
snaihika-vairecanika-upaśamanīyānāṃ dhūmānāmanyatamaṃ sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā
dīyatām kiṃcit iti-ādi-mithyā-vyapadeśaiḥ tān viluṇṭhanti
jerūsaleṃnagara-āgamana-anantaraṃ prathame sabbat parvadine syāmuyalaḥ sāmānyaḥ janaḥ iva prārthanā-mandiraṃ gatvā tatra torā dharma-granthaṃ paṭhitvā prārthanāṃ kṛtavān
utthāya kṣata-ja-āplutaḥ saḥ sahasā roṣa-anala-uddīpitaḥ
su-dūra-sambandhavantaḥ bāndhavāḥ ca tasmin bṛhati yojanā-kārye niyojitāḥ
sarve janāḥ lajjā-avanata-mukhāḥ tūṣṇīm eva tasthu
lakṣyamāṇāitiasya vāhīke go-śabda-prayoga-hetu-jñāna-viṣayaḥ arthaḥ
yasminarthe na prasiddhaḥ tatra lakṣakatvena vyavahriyate tīra-ādau gaṅgā-padasya pracura-prayoga-abhāvāt
mathurānāthīyāt ākhyāta-vāda-dīdhiti-vyākhyānāt tad-kṛtam sup-artha-vicāra-abhidhānam bodha-grantham
kintu mātā uktavatī svarga-prāpti-arthaṃ puṇyaṃ karaṇīyam
satyam yathā-dṛṣṭasya yathā-śrutasya ca ātman-anubhavasya para-buddhi-saṃkrāntaye tathā eva uccāryamāṇā vāk satyam ucyate
kenaeṣaḥ hasti-grahaṇa-udyatena yūthe prayāte kalabhaḥ gṛhītaḥ
vaidya-mahodayaḥ ca nāḍī-parīkṣā-anantaram uktavān na asti eva kaścana roga
muṣṭi-prahāra-capeṭā-pātana-upacāra-anantaraṃ tābhyāṃ svīkṛtaṃ yat śatru-rājyasya gupta-carau tau tenālīrāmāt āśaṅkitau āstām
a-śabda-śravaṇaṃ ca
vasiṣṭa-mahat-muneḥ
laṇḍan-nagara-sthe kasmiṃścit eva saṅghasya adhyakṣatvena citaḥ abhavat
na-vyakta-nidhanāni eva punaḥ na-vyaktam na-darśanam nidhanam maraṇam yeṣām tāni na-vyakta-nidhanāni
iti śrīmad-bhagavadgītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde jñāna-vijñāna-yogaḥ nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ
bhāva-svabhāva-nityatvam api caasya
agre hībrū-punarutthāna-abhiyāne mahatīṃ bhūmikām api saḥ niravahat
ekadā meṣaḥ ayam bahu-dina-anantaram daitya iva mahānase prāviśat
tathāpi pañca-nimeṣa-abhyantare te aśvaārohiṇaḥ śakaṭa-samīpam āgatāḥ eva
sa naḥ pāyātapāyebhyaḥ yoga-ānandana-kesarī
yogyena sākṣāt saṃbandhena tad-tad-pada-arthasya tatra tatraanvayam svīkurvantaḥ
sarva-karaṇa-rahitam ityarthaḥ
atha tad-vāraṇāya pramā-ātmanka-jñāna-nirūpita-nirukta-viṣayatā vattvam saṃbandhatvamitiucyate iti cet
ataḥ jñāna-gatam pratyakṣatva-anumititva-ādikam na jātiḥ
janmani garbha-vāsa-yoni-dvāra-niḥsaraṇam doṣaḥ
kṣata-vi-kṣatā gṛdhrī tu mṛtā eva
smarāmi guru-deva bhilla-strī-saṅgāt eva saḥ patitaḥ
kailāśa vinayena nata-vadana eva tadapi nivedayāmi idam sarvam etat-artham āyojyata yad vayam sarve api nava-nava-śabda-anveṣaṇa-vyasana itayā bhavatām atīva ākulā abhūma
vastutaḥ arjunaḥ etāvān śūraḥ asti yat bhavatyāḥ kadāpi raṇa-raṅga-gamanasya kāpi āvaśyakatā naiva bhavati iti
tṛptiḥ paritoṣaḥ hi yasmāt na asti me mama śṛṇvataḥ yuṣmad-mukha-niḥsṛta-vākya-amṛtam
ataḥ etasyāḥ samasyāyāḥ parihāram na-pūrva-darpaṇasya sāhāyyena prāptum śaknumaḥ vayam
ātmān-āropita-mahimānaḥ
samūhasya ca pratyeka-na-atirikta tvāt ghaṭa-viṣayaka-tva-avacchinna-śābda-bodha-niṣṭha-janyatā-nirūpita-janakatvam śaktiḥ
prāṇa-apāya-bhītiḥ tam abādhata
sa-nūpurā mekhalā-nāda-hāsā
tat anyasya iti kalpanā-na-upapattiḥ
anye pari-janāḥ samudra-yātrā-artham nirgatā
tena punaḥ api sva-lakṣya-prāpti-arthaṃ sa-vinayaṃ patraṃ preṣitam
tāvatāeva tasya sarva-viṣayaka-tva-nirvāhāt
tataḥ tenālīrāmaḥ ekaṃ lauha-kāram ākārya tena laghu-vaṃśa-daṇḍaṃ lauha-patra-jaṭitam akārayat
ekadā kṛṣṇa-nagara-rājaḥ kṛṣṇacandraḥ svayaṃ tatra taṃ sammānayituṃ prāptaḥ
prāṇa-yātrā-artham api paryāptam annam na āsādayāmi
viśvavidyālaye āṃgla-bhāṣā-pra-adhyāpakaḥ
daśa-pañcadaśa-dināni yāvat tena prastareṇa āhata-pādāḥ api pathikāḥ taṃ prastaraṃ naiva apasāritavantaḥ
vrajati nabhasi śīghram megha-vṛnda-anu-yātrā
parantu harivallabhavat naete naiyāyika-pakṣa-pātinaḥ iti bodhyam
su-dūrāt āgatāya patye jala-pāna-ādikaṃ vismṛtya sā taṃ nirdhārite sthāne upāveśayat
pratyavāya-hetu-tva-abhāvāḥ ca liṅ-arthaḥ
ādye pada-antara-vaiyarthyam
tāsām ca āvāsa saudha-sīmā-antargate mahat-udyāne kārpaṭika-gṛheṣu ṭaiṇṭeṣu vihita
prakṛtānām yoginām praṇava-āveśita-brahman-buddhīnām kāla-antara-mukti-bhājām brahman-pratipattaye uttaraḥ mārgaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti yatra kāle ityādi vivakṣita-artha-samarpaṇa-artham ucyate
kṛṣi gaurakṣya vāṇijyaṃ vaiśya-karma sva-bhāva-jam
ubhaya-paṅkti-gatānām prāsādānām gavākṣa-antara-gatā dīpa-prabhā eṣā
payasiardhodake cchāge hrīvera-utpala-nāgaraiḥ
ekadā mādhavanātha vāsantyā bhūya bhūya anunīyamāna sa-kopam abhāṇīt prathamam gatvā sva-bandhu-rājam nivartaya
tathāpi parama-sammāna-sukha-arhaḥ rājan-putraḥ tvam na-arha khalu amuṣya nir-ādarasya
eṣaḥ ariṣṭavṛṣabhaḥ nāma dānavaḥ piṇḍa-ikṛta-nirghāta-rūpaḥ bhūmi-talam khara-puṭaiḥ likhan
sva-karmaṇā bhagavataḥ abhyarcana-bhakti-yogasya siddhi-prāptiḥ phalam jñāna-niṣṭhā-yogyatā
caitraḥ kīdṛśaḥ iti praśna-vākyam hi caitra-viśeṣyakam jijñāsita-dharma-avacchinna-prakārakam abheda-saṃsargakam bodham prasūte
yadā tu asmātvākyāt nīla-viśiṣṭa-ghaṭa-karmanka-jñāna-śābda-bodhaḥ tadā ghaṭa-padasya nīla-viśiṣṭa-ghaṭe lakṣaṇā
prati-ekaṃ janaḥ na-ujjhita-maryādaṃ mūrkha-kṛtyāni kartuṃ svādhīnaḥ
prasādasya ayam viṣayaḥ yat sarvakāra eṣu dineṣu evaṃ-vidha-sthaleṣu saṃskṛtasya suruci-pada-prayogam ārabdhavān api
kim idam na-śobhanīyaṃ kṛtyam iti vicārya mṛgayuḥ mūlyam ādātuṃ pra-bala-javena tam anvadhāvat
kuśala-vārtā-ālāpasya anantaram viśvāmitreṇa kiñcit kālam viśrāmam kṛtaḥ
vividha-varṇa īyaiḥ upetasya rājyasya pālanam asi-dhārā-vratam iva
divya-astra-prayoge tasya mahat prāvīṇyam āsīt
pratyayānām prakṛti-artha-anvita-sva-artha-bodhaka-tva-vyutpatteḥ
pitta-laṃ baddha-viṭ-mūtraṃ na ca carman-prasevāt pañca-saptati-rūpyakāṇi ākarṣya tasmai dadau praveśapatrāṇi ca trīṇi tasmāt gṛhītāni
tad-tad-vṛtti-jñāna-janya-upasthiti-na-vyavahita-uttara-śābda-bodham prati tad-tad-vṛtti-jñāna-janya-upasthiteḥ hetutvam vaktavyam
vyaiyākaraṇāḥ api nīlamidam na raktamiti vākyam itara-nivṛtti-tātparyaka-mastya-ādi-rahitam abhyupagacchanti
tasya guru-kula-vāsaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ ca jñātvā tuṣyanti sma
tadā devadatta-vyakteḥ aikyāt bheda-ghaṭita-sādṛśyasya na-sambhavāt īdṛśaḥ devadattaḥ iti vākyam apa-arthakam syāt
bhāvanā-viśeṣya-virahāt itianena bhāvanā-viśeṣyakaḥ bodhaḥ tatra na tu bhāvanā-viśeṣaṇaka-itara-viśeṣyakaḥ bodhaḥ iti labhyate
mārge prāptāni naikāni saṅkaṭāni sva-buddhi-kauśalena niḥsāritavān
gaḍha-deśa-adhipatiḥ api sva-camū-pateḥ tasya parākrama atiśayena prasannaḥ tam dāna-mānābhyām bahu saccakāra
aṅgatā-grāhaka-liṅga-ādīni śruti-kalpanayā aṅgatām bodhayanti
prakṛtiḥ nāman-dhātu-bhedena dvi-vidhā
tat siddham vākya-artha-avabodha-na-vyavadhānāt
asmākaṃ rājā virāṭaḥ ekacchatra-pṛthivī-patiḥ bhavatu
sup-artha-karmatva-ādikam sva-nirūpaka-dhātu-artha-karaṇaka-tva-ādi-paramparā-saṃbandhena bhāvanāyāmevaanveti
saḥ ca na-vidvān ubhau tau na vijānītaḥ iti vacanāt viśeṣitasya ca viduṣaḥ karman-ākṣepa-vacanāt ca katham saḥ puruṣaḥ iti
rāhu-vaktra-antaragatā candra-lekhā iva śobhate
kṣetra-kṣetrajña-saṃyogāt tat viddhi bharata-ṛṣabha
pippala-vṛkṣa-harita-patrāṇi kim akurvan
smṛtena tīreṇa tīra-anvaya-bodhaḥ
vividha-yantra-yojana-anantaram tena niścitam yat rogiṇaḥ mastiṣke daurbalyam āgatam asti
tasmāt yaḥ kaścana karmī saṃnyasta-phala-saṃkalpaḥ bhavet saḥ yogī samādhānavān na-vikṣipta-cittaḥ bhavet
sūrya-asta-samaye taiḥ śoṇa-nadasya tīram prāptam
saḥ ayam adhyāsa-svarūpaḥ kṣetra-kṣetrajña-saṃyogaḥ mithyā-jñāna-lakṣaṇaḥ
ākhyāta-artha tvam ca śakti-lakṣaṇā-anyatara-saṃbandhena ākhyāta-pratipādya tvamiti vācyam
hreṣā-śabda-anumitasya aśvasya na-avagata-guṇa-viśeṣasya
tasmin pātre eka-śāka-parṇaḥ lagnaḥ āsīt
ataḥ eva vajra-cūrṇa-nirmāṇāya lakṣam rūpyakāṇi dātum sajjaḥ jātaḥ saḥ
saḥ tu na-saṃbhoga-malina tayā gṛhasya na-sānnidhyāt kauṭumbikānām durārakṣaḥ
guru-caraṇānām saṃskṛta-śodha-kṣetre avadānam mama guro rāmadayālo kāvya-yātrā āghāta ityādi-lekhān kaiścit śodha-chātraiḥ lekhāpitān tasya kare nidhāya prāha iyam kācana sāmagrī asmat-sakāśam api samāgatā
tatra vākye bhāva-pradhāne ākhyāta-artha-pradhāne
vāta-laṃ kaṭu-tikta-amlam dhis adhaḥ-mārga-pravartanam
vidyā-abhyāsa-samāpteḥ anantaram śiṣyāṇām prati-gamana-samaye guruḥ gajendraḥ sva-śiṣyāṇām yogyatā anu-guṇam kim api vastu upāyana-rūpeṇa dadāti sma
anīti-pavana-kṣiptaḥ kāryārabdhau sa nimajjati
ekaḥ ūrustambhaḥ iti āma-tridoṣa-samutthaḥ
tatra cira-kāla-upārjitaḥ priya-suhṛt me manthara-abhidhānaḥ kacchapaḥ dhārmikaḥ prativasati
agniḥ bhadramukha etāḥ hi mahendra-niyogāt bharata-śatrughna-puraḥsarāḥ prakṛtayaḥ bhavantam upasthitāḥ
ata eva mama sthāne apara samarthatara ravikumāra-ādi-sadṛśa su-yogya-śiṣya yadi niyojyeta
santi hiṛteapi a-hita-āhāra-upayogāt anyā roga-prakṛtayaḥ
śābda-bodha-aupayika-vṛtteḥ eva lakṣaṇātvāt
na-artha-paramparā-abhibhūta saṅkaṭāt dārikayā abhirakṣitaḥ dvi-traiḥ dinai prakṛtim āpanna parama-kṛtajñatā-ākulaḥ tasyai dhanyavādāt muhuḥ muhuḥ vyatānīt
nāman-arthayoḥ abheda-anvaya-vyutpatteḥ rājan-padasya rājan-sambandhini lakṣaṇām svīkṛtya tasya puruṣa-nāman-arthe abheda-anvayaḥ gadādhara-bhaṭṭācārya-saṃmataḥ samīcīnaḥ
ghaṭa-viṣayaka-anubhava-janake ghaṭa-pade miti-mātṛ-viṣayaka-anubhava-janaka tvamapiasti
tat-samaye rāmanāthaḥ guṇaśīlasya svabhāva-ādi-viṣaye tān pṛṣṭavān
dāna-upabhoga-hīnena dhanena dhaninaḥ yadi
parama-artha-tattvam ca vāsudeva-ākhyam param brahma-abhidheya-bhūtam viśeṣataḥ abhivyañjayat
yadi api ātman-vināśa-nimittaḥ mohaḥ na saṃbhavati nityaḥ ātmā iti vijānataḥ
tasmāt viśeṣitasya na-vikriyā-ātman-darśinaḥ viduṣaḥ mumukṣoḥ ca sarva-karma-saṃnyāse eva adhikāraḥ
devatā-ādi-viṣaya-jñāna-yajña-phala-tulyam asya phalam bhavati iti tena adhyayanena aham iṣṭaḥ pūjitaḥ syām bhaveyam iti me mama matiḥ niścayaḥ
na ca vastutaḥ na-ādi-bhūta-bodhakatvasya
jñāna-vayas-vṛddhaḥ bhīṣmaḥ yadā śara-pañjare āsīt
pāyasaṃ kṛśarāṃ sarpiḥ kāśmarya-triphalā-rasam
sneha-sveda-vidhiḥ tatra vartayaḥ bhojanāni ca
daśame dine tena nija-maraṇa-vārtā prasāritā
ataḥ pada-artha-niṣṭhaḥ lakṣaṇā-vyāpāraḥ pade āropyate iti kecana vadanti
yad-vṛtti-kārakatvam sva-anvayi-kriyā-pratipādakena padena vṛttyā pratipadyate tattvam prathamā-prayojakam abhihitatvam itiuktam bhāṭṭadīpikāyām
bhartṛn-caraṇa-kamalam dhyāyantyā tathā katham api nisārita saḥ avadhi
bali-palita-khālityam āpādayati
samudita-vara-cāpa-bāṇa-pāṇim
tatca paśyan vyutpitsuḥbālaḥ ghaṭa-ānayana-kartuḥ pravartakam kāryatā-jñānam vartate
prakṛti-naṭī nava-nava-veṣā
praśastaṃ baddha-viṭ-mūtraṃ viṣa-śleṣmā mayaarśasām
latā-gṛha-antaritaḥ bhūtvā etena mad-vastreṇa ācchādayitvā tān āhariṣye
na-ārabdha-phalānām puṇyānām karmaṇām kṣaya-na-upapatteḥ ca
antardadhāna-candra-labdha-avakāśaḥ avatarati iva prāsādāt andhakāraḥ
iyamca vyavasthā śābdikānām na-pradhāne duha-ādīnām pradhāne nī-hṛ-kṛṣ-vahām
padena pada-artha-smṛti-janane upayujyamānaḥ pada-tad-arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ vṛttiḥ
sva-paricārikayā vadhya-sthāna-adhikṛtaṃ prati vārtāṃ preṣayāmāsa paredyuḥ prathamatayā yaḥ tvām upagacchati
tataḥ tad-lāvaṇya-guṇa-ākṛṣṭena mayāapi tatpaścātjhampaḥ dattaḥ
svayaṃ ca pravāsa-avasare api śabda-koṣa-nirmāṇa-kāryam anuvartayituṃ śaknomi iti tasya vicāraḥ āsīt
kṛteḥbodhe kṛti-āśrayasya kartuḥ upasthiti-saṃbhavāt pāka-kartṛ-tva-avacchinno-dhārmika-jijñāsā apiupapadyate
sva-vacana-kṛta-doṣaḥ badhyatām eṣaḥ śīghram
tathā ca na eka-pada-samabhivyāhāre pañcamī-āpattiḥ iti vācyam
tila-māṣa-kulattha-uda-sannibhaṃ pitta-vidradhī
api auṣadha-vidhāna-jñaḥ tasya siddhiḥyadṛcchayā
he vidvān bhavān guru-dakṣiṇā-rūpeṇa kiṃ dātum icchati
tasmāt śabda-vṛtti-na-viṣayasya api pratiyogi-saṃbandhasya pratiyogitvasya śābda-bodhe bhānāt śabda-vṛtti-viṣayasya eva śābda-bodha-viṣaya tvamiti niyamaḥ na-prāmāṇikaḥ
evaṃ vicintya kautsaḥ raghu-mahat-rājaṃ prati prasthitavān
kāñcukīyaḥ katham a-deśa-kālaḥ nāma
naiyāyika-mata-nirūpaṇa-avasare
abhedena go-pada-artha-anvita-duhyamāna-pada-arthasya saptamī-arthe vartamāna-kāla-vṛtti tve
tathāpi sva-kārya-viṣaye tasya manasi kāpi śaṅkā na āsīt
grāma-mukhāt ābhya saudha-paryantam kadalī-stambha-nirmitāni dvārāṇi anekāni nirmitāni
na paryuṣitam anyatra māṃsa-haritaka-śuṣka-śāka-phala-bhakṣyebhyaḥ
cakṣuṣ-indriya-pratiyogika tvātca
sarvam idam varṣa-dvaya-anantaram eva bhūyāt iti rākeśena sūcitam yataḥ triṃśad varṣāṇi atītya na kaḥ api rājakīye mahāvidyālaye pra-adhyāpaka-padam labdhum śaknute sma
cira-abhyasta-patham yāti
haste vidyamānāḥ rekhāḥ pariśīlya saḥ kheda-miśritena svareṇa bhavatyāḥ haste santāna-prāpti-artham rekhāḥ eva na santi iti uktavān
tataḥ vimuktaḥ sva-śarīra-rakṣaṇe yaśaḥ pradātuṃ suhṛdāṃ ca jīvitam
atra padminī-śabda madhu-pa-śabdaḥ ca kāñcit na-laukikīm suṣamām puṣṇīta
uddeśyatā-avacchedaka-kākebhyaḥ vidheyatā-avacchedakayoḥ aikya-aparihāreṇa
śākya-ādi-bhiḥ vidasya prāmāṇye viplāvite veda-vākya-artha-vicāra-rūpa-mīmāṃsā-ādi-parijanasya kṛtyameva naasti
śrṛgālaḥ bhayāt akampata kintu ātmānam avasthāpya sa-vinayam abravīt deva bāhya-āḍambara-pradarśane mama ruciḥ nāsti
pāka-ādeḥ nirukta-vrajana-artha tayāeva tad-vācaka-padāt caturthī-upapatteḥ
na-anya-labhyaḥ śabda-arthaḥ iti nyāyāt
vṛtti-vārtika-kṛtaḥ tu mukhya-artha-sambandhena śabdasya pratipādakatvam lakṣaṇā
akabarasya ākramaṇena rāṇāpratāpaḥ nityaṃ sva-vasati-sthānasya parivartanam akarot
upasthitāya tasmai saḥ sva-sāmarthya-anusāreṇa sampāditena sa-rasa-bhojanena saha sādhāraṇīṃ rūkṣāṃ sthūlāṃ roṭīṃ bhakṣaṇāya adadāt
tatra evam ca prāk dāra-parigrahāt puruṣaḥ ātmā prākṛtaḥ dharma-jijñāsā-uttara-kālam loka-traya-sādhanam putram
śābda-bodhe śakti-janya-upasthiti-lakṣaṇā-janya-upasthityoḥ kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvasya kalpena
mama patyuḥ svāsthya-prāpti-artham kim karaṇīyam iti vadatu iti
tad-abhāvasya ca prasiddhatvāt katham bodha-na-upapattiḥ
tiṅaḥca āśraya-paryavasita-kartṛ-karman-arthaka tām
ārabdham kāryam pari-tyaktum na-icchan trivikramaḥ punarapi vṛkṣasya samīpam gatvā śākhāyām lambamānam śavam skandhe āropya yathā-pūrvam śmaśāna-abhi-mukham prasthitavān
para-brahman-ānanda-sa-brahmacārī-śḍh rasa-asvādaḥ kavi-vākyāt vyañjanayāeva jāyate
sarva-jñāna-vimūḍhān tān viddhi jānīhi naṣṭān nāśam gatān na-cetasaḥ na-viveka inaḥ
kāmaḥ eṣaḥ krodhaḥ eṣaḥ rajas-guṇa-samudbhavaḥ
pañca-krośa-anantaram vāma-bhāge ekayā pagaḍaṃḍikayā mat-uṭajam prāpsyasi
strī-janena adya sahasā pra-harṣa-vyākula-kramā
tathā ca ādhunika-saṃketa-sthale bodhakatva-jñānasya vyabhicārāt na bodhakatvam śaktiḥ
sevaka-anusevakaiḥ nānā-vidha-vāhanai
sad-gṛha-sthāt sva-vastu siddha-puruṣaḥ kadā gṛhītavān
iti uktvā vaidyaḥ tatkālam eva sva-dravya-puṭakāt ekam viṣa-māraṇa-auṣadham niṣkāsitavān
bhagavān jānāti yat mama antakaraṇasya antimā prārthanā tadā sā iyam iva abhūt yat ā-maraṇam me hṛdaye tasya smṛtiḥ akṣuṇṇā tiṣṭhet yasya darśana-sama-kālam eva mama kaiśaurye cirantanam ekam jyoti pra-jvalitam abhūt
laghu-śīta-rūkṣa-khara-viśada-sūkṣma-sparśa-guṇa-bahulāni vāyavyāni
antya-pada-uccāraṇa-na-antaram tāvat-pada-viṣayakam ekam smaraṇam jāyate
gṛhe tu hībrū-bhāṣayā eva sambhāṣaṇam iti niyamaṃ ḍeborā kaṭhoratayā pālitavatī āsīt ityataḥ anya-bhāṣā-prabhāve satyapi tadīyā hībrū-bhāṣā svacchatayā niṣkalaṅkatayā ca rakṣitā āsīt
spaṣṭā caiyam rītiḥ putrīyatiiti vākya-janya-bodha-nirūpaṇa-avasare vyutpatti-vāde
svīya-siddhānta-virodhena bhaṭṭācārya-saraṇyā teṣām śābda-vicāra-pracuram vistṛtam sandarbham racayāmāsuḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ api yudhiṣṭhirasya sad-guṇa-viṣayaṃ paricitavān
sā ca pratyak-samudra-gamanavat karmaṇā sahabhāvitvena virudhyate
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ vṛddhasya me jīvita-niḥspṛhasya nisarga-saṃmīlita-locanasya
rājyasya hita-cintayā kīdṛśaṃ kaṣṭaṃ sahate puro-hita-varaḥ
phala-avacchinna-vyāpāre vyāpāra-avacchinna-phale ca dhātoḥ śakti-dvayam
ārya kula-putra-janasya śīla-paritoṣa-upajīvinī gaṇikā khalu aham
rājan-guruḥ taṃ ati-mahat-arghaṃ paridhānaṃ dhārayituṃ dattavān
samāja-diś-darśana-arthaṃ na-eke granthāḥ racitāḥ
paraṃ bhavān etāḥ mūrtīḥ vipaṇana-kendre kathaṃ na vikrīṇīte vikrayeṇa bahu-dhana-lābhaḥ bhavitā
bāleṣu mañcatva-āropāt mañca-pada-pravṛttiḥ hasantiiti pada-antara-prayogāt vijñāyate iti
yathā bhagavataḥ vāsudevasya kṣatra-dharma-ceṣṭitam na jñānena samuccīyate puruṣa-artha-siddhaye
sa pradhāna-sacivam ādiśat rājan-paramparā-anusāram asmai bhūyiṣṭhaṃ puraskāra-ādi kaṃ dīyatām
teṣāmavayavān pratyakṣa-anumāna-upadeśaiḥ sādhayitvā namaskṛtya vāyave yathā-śakti pravakṣyāmaḥ vāyuḥ tantra-yantra-dharaḥ
deha-agni-doṣa-bhaiṣajya-mātrā-kāla-anuvartinā
saṃsāra-sāgara-uttāla-taraṅgān samīkurvan iva dināni yāpayati
rājan-pada-śakya-arthasya svatva-saṃbandhena puruṣa-nāman-arthe anvayaḥ navya-naiyāyika-saṃmataḥ sādhīyān
gaṅgā-pada-śakya-pravāha-saṃbandhasya tīre sattvāt
tatuktamabhiyuktaiḥ pada-vākya-ratna-ākāre
yoga-kṣema-ārādhanam
yadi tatra kācit su-dṛḍhā vyavasthā kriyeta tadā sīmā-anta-vāsinī prajā nir-bhayā sukhinī ca bhavet
tad-pāṇi-patitā ghaṇṭā vānaraiḥ prāptā
ataḥca tad-kriyā-kartṛ tvam tad-kriyā-anukūlā tad-kriyā-viṣayiṇī ca yā kṛtiḥ tadvattvam
prathama-bhāvīni padānyatilakṣyam pada-artheṣu vākya-artha-bodhana-śakti-svīkārasya na-yukta tvāt
tayoḥ antareṇa gacchatā nandagopa-putreṇa aghaṭṭayatā sa-mūla-viṭapam cūrṇa-ikṛtau
kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-antaram kalpanīyam
tad-na-antaram dhāvantam śvetamantam śṛṇomi iti śābdayāmi iti vā anuvyavasāya-abhāvāt
dhātoḥ phala-avacchinna-vyāpāre vyāpāra-avacchinna-phale ca śakti-dvayam svīkurvanti navyāḥ
tad-sūtra-bhāṣya-kārasya api na śābda-bodhasya śabda-viṣayaka tvamabhimatam
etāni caturakṣarāṇi vartante iti vadan eva rūpasiṃha para-loka-a-tithiḥ jāta
kevalam tat-āgamana-sūcanā mama samīpe preṣaṇīyā
ṛtusenasya senā su-yogya-senānyā nirdeśane svīyam parākramam prādarśayat
tathā jaya-parājaya-phala-upabhoge
vayam tu vīṇā-pāṇeḥ devyāḥ prasādāt sarvatra eva na-pratihata-prasarāḥ
iti paribhāṣayā atideśa-sthale sarva-kārya-abhāvāt karman-saṃjñā-prayuktaḥ karmaṇaḥ lakāraḥ na bhavatiiti vyutpatti-vāda-vyākhyātṛṇām saraṇiḥapi na hṛdayam-gamā
dravya-saṃyoga-karaṇa-bāhulyāt
nitya-prāyaścittayoḥ naimittikatva-na-viśeṣāt
māṃsa-mūtra-purīṣa-asthi-nirmite asminkalevare
brāhmaṇaiḥ dāna-grahaṇa-kāmanayā ebhiḥ sva-keśāḥ eva vāriṇā klinnāḥ kṛtāḥ
āśrama-vikalpa-samuccaya-vidhānāt ca śruti-smṛtyoḥ
ante anya-deva-ādibhiḥ saha āgataḥ brahmā tasmai mahat-ṛṣi-nāmakam upādhim dattavān
idam godāvarī-nikuñjam bhīru-bhramaṇa-yogyam siṃhavattvātityatra yadi śvan-bhīroḥ na-vīrasya bhramaṇa-ayogya tvam sādhyate
hṛdayaṃ kapha-hṛd-roge suptaṃ stimita-bhārikam
baṃdhu-strī-bhṛtya-vargasya buddheḥ sattvasya caātmanaḥ
rātri-bhojana-ante mahān-rājena rajata-mañjūṣāyāṃ rasagullā nāma miṣṭānnaṃ nidhāya phiradausa-sakāśe preṣitam
tathā api patyuḥ eṣā ati-dāna-śīla tā tasyai na rocate sma
pramāda-ālasya-nidrābhiḥ pramādaḥ ca ālasyam ca nidrā ca pramāda-ālasya-nidrāḥ tābhiḥ pramāda-ālasya-nidrābhiḥ tat tamaḥ nibadhnāti bhārata
sarva-artha-sādhikā kā asti
tai saha na kimapi yātrā-vastun-jātam āsīt iti vilokanena pratīyate sma yat ete kasyacana svāgatāya samāgatā
yadā punaḥ ayam samyak-jñāna-prāpti-upāyatvena
rājyasya pratiṣṭhite saṃskṛta-mahāvidyālaye vibhāga-adhyakṣa-pade sthāpitasya asya vetanam api puṣkalam saṃjātam asti eṣu dineṣu
kuṣṭha-ailavāluka-kaṭphala-samudraphena-kadamba-niryāsa-ikṣukāṇḍa-ikṣvikṣuraka-vasuka-uśīrāṇi iti daśaimāni śukraśodhanāni bhavanti
isrel-deśe pracalatāṃ bahūnāṃ yahūdya-saṅghaṭana-kāryāṇām artha-sāhāyyaṃ saḥ karoti sma
trayaḥ śothāḥ bhavanti vāta-pitta-śleṣma-nimittāḥ
sva-nāsikā-agra-saṃprekṣaṇam eva cet vivakṣitam
saṅgharṣa-janita-kolāhalāt bhītaḥ gardabhaḥ utplutya sarvaṃ pṛṣṭha-sthaṃ bhāraṃ bhūmau nipātya dūraṃ palāyitaḥ alakṣitaḥ ca jātaḥ
guṇa-vṛtta-nibaddhasya ca puruṣasya yā gatiḥ
sannyāsinaḥ sarva-aṅga-parityāga inaḥ bhavanti
viśvāmitra sa-harṣam evam sākṣāt kāmadhenu-sutā vartate bhavatām āśrame tarhi bhagavan tasyā atra kā āvaśyakatā sā tu asmat-rājan-prāsādeṣu ucitā
iṣṭa-na-niṣṭa-deha-prāptiḥ karman-jam phalam karmabhyaḥ jātam buddhi-yuktāḥ samatva-buddhi-yuktāḥ santaḥ hi yasmāt phalam tyaktvā parityajya manīṣiṇaḥ jñāninaḥ bhūtvā
tayoḥ krīḍāyāḥ harṣa-dhvaniḥ sampūrṇa-go-kule bhramati sma
āyāsaḥ sarva-a-pathyānāṃ
parantu asmin samaye bhavatī atra katham vidyā-ālaya-samayaḥ khalu eṣaḥ benyahūdaḥ apṛcchat
ye tu parama-artha-darśinaḥ sāṃkhyāḥ
yat padam sarvasya avabhāsakam api agni-āditya-ādikam jyotiḥ na avabhāsayate
saṃbandha-sāmānya-saṃsargaka-śābda-bodhe jāte
bhūtānāṃ bhāva-abhāva-karaḥ
diṣṭyā asmākam iyam āśā na ati-dūra-vartinī āsīt
prabhāte kṛṣakā vṛṣabhai saha sva-sva-kṣetreṣu gatā kintu na āsan tatra teṣām halāni
api tu ghaṭe eva ghaṭa-pada-boddhavya tvamavagāhate
ata parastāt sā asmākam sarala-saṃyukta-parivārasya saṃskārai atīva prabhāvitā jātā
sve sve yathā-ukta-lakṣaṇa-bhede karmaṇi abhirataḥ tad-paraḥ saṃsiddhim sva-karma-anuṣṭhānāt na-śuddhi-kṣaye sati kāya-indriyāṇām jñāna-niṣṭhā-yogyatā-lakṣaṇām saṃsiddhim labhate prāpnoti naraḥ adhikṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ
bhavatām palāyana-anantaram sihaḥ mām avadat tvam kīdṛśam na-abhijñam mahat-mantrin-pada-artham ānītavān
yaugandharāyaṇaḥ sva-gatam evam eṣā sā magadha-rāja-putrī padmāvatī nāma
sat-śabda-pratyaya-na-viṣayatvāt asattva-āśaṅkāyām jñeyasya sarva-prāṇi-karaṇa-upādhi-dvāreṇa tad-astitvam pratipādayan tad-āśaṅkā-nivṛtti-artham āha
yathā haṃsaḥ nīra-kṣīra-vivekaṃ dhārayati tathā eva pratāpaḥ guṇa-doṣān samyak rītyā jñātuṃ śaknoti
yaḥ vacana-gata-siddhim api na jānāti
mārga-āyāsa-parihārāya phala-āhāra-ādikaṃ ca dāpitavān
mām karmaṇi dṛṣṭa-aneka-na-artha-yukte pāramparyeṇa api na-ekāntika-śreyaḥ-prāpti-kāle niyuñjyāt
tasmāt vidhi-pratiṣedha-śāstram na-vidvat-viṣayam iti siddham
ayam kaḥ iti-ādau vidheya-vācaka-kim-śabdasya
mātrā-sparśāḥ tu kaunteya śīta-uṣṇa-sukha-duḥkha-dāḥ
bhūṣaṇa-sāra-vyākhyāyām kāśikāyām
nava-kuvalaya-nīlaḥ matta-mātaṅga-līlaḥ
visaṃvādi-pravṛttau iva iṣṭa-bheda-na-grahaṇam kāraṇam
atha kasyāṃ velāyāṃ prati-āgata-prāṇaḥ svāmī
etādṛśa-anumiteḥ pūrvam go-karmanka-tva-grāhaka-abhāvena sādhya-grahasya asaṃbhavāt
ayi bho para-vastu-lobhena kim
jvara-asṛkpitta-vīsarpa-kuṣṭha-pāṇḍvāmaya-bhramān
eka-adhikaraṇa tvam ghaṭa-ādi-viśeṣya-abhāve na yuktam iti cet
iti vākya-adhīna-śābda-bodha-nirūpaṇena śakti-vādasya upakramaḥ teṣām śābda-vicāra-kutūhali tām vyanakti
nija-ājñā-pālana-yogyam saṃsādhya puna śastra-hatasya tasya rakta-pānam kariṣyati
citta-vṛtti-nirodhaṃ kṛtvā dhruvaḥ tādṛśaṃ sthira-padaṃ prāptum icchati yat bhavat-kule kenāpi na prāptam
yuṣmat-pāṇi-grahaṇāt ārabhya varṣa-paryantam maraṇa-āsannām sthitim eva bhajamāna āsam
gabhīra-nadī-tīra-anvita-ādheyatva-bodhaḥ na syāt
saṃbandha-vaśa-prāptasya iti ca
bhoḥ kimnu khalu samāgate sarva-rāja-maṇḍale virāṭaḥ naāgacchati
mama śara-paridagdha-toya-paṅkam
pṛthvī mātā teṣām imāṃ nir-ādhāra-vārtāṃ na asahata
svinna-atisvinna-rūpāṇi tathā atisvinna-bheṣajam
kiñca śakti-vādinaḥ api gaṅgā-pada-janyā tīra-smṛtiḥ tīra-śābda-bodha-anukūlā iti saṃmatam
paktā bhavati hemante mātrā-dravya-guru-kṣamaḥ
na api śruta-hāni-na-śruta-parikalpanāyām kaścit viśeṣaḥ upalabhyate
sabhya asau nitarām cakita pramodasya abhi-mukham ā-nakha-śikham vīkṣate sma
maheśāna śūlin jaṭā-jūṭa-dhārin
prāṇaiḥ api bhavataḥ ājñā-pālana-arthaṃ siddhāḥ vayam iti
viśeṣaṇa-pada-uttara-vibhaktīnām abheda-arthaka tā
kṛtvā surān tān hata-śatru-pakṣān
mantriṇā pṛthivī-pāla-cittam vighaṭitam kvacit
vānaraḥ punaḥ śabda-karaṇāya akathayat bakaḥ adhunā pra-ucca-svareṇa śabdam akarot
tat uktiṃ niśamya vṛkaḥ vana-abhi-mukhaṃ gantum ārabhata avadat ca tava eva astu śṛṅkhalā-bandhanam idam
adyaasmi mahat-rājena upādhyāya-amātya-pra-kṛti-jana-samakṣam ekaprakāra-saṃkṣiptaṃ kosala-rājyaṃ kṛtvā
sarvataḥ-pāṇi-pādaṃ tat sarvataḥ-akṣi-śiraḥ-mukham
bahu mūtra-purīṣa-ūṣmā tridoṣaḥtueva pāṭalaḥ
prātipadika-artha-sūtra-arthaḥ
vidyamānayoḥeva ghaṭa-bhūtala-ādyayoḥ saṃyoga-ādi-saṃbandha-ādi-darśanena na-vidyamāne atīta-ghaṭe vidyamāna-smaraṇasya saṃbandha-saṃbhavāt
rātrau aham śayanīye sānandam ardha-nimīlita-netra patnyā saha kiñcit ālapan horārdham tiṣṭhāmi
ahaṃ puṣpa-sāra-vikretṝn militum icchāmi
atha te ye anyathāto viduḥ anyarājānaḥ te kṣayyalokā bhavanti iti-ādi-śrutibhyaḥ ca
iti śrīmad-bhagavadgītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde tārakabrahmayogaḥ nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ
āyuktaḥ yuvakam puraskāram dattvā udyāna-pāla-kāryam api kartum ādideśa
dvi-pathaṃ na ati-kālaṃ vā kṛcchra-sādhyaṃ dvi-doṣa-jam
a-kṛta-dūta-sampreṣaṇam na-vidita-āgamanam na-mitra-sambandhinam katham nu khalu mām avagacchet tatrabhavān rāghavaḥ
kim tat karma kaunteya sa-doṣam api tri-guṇa-ātmakatvāt na tyajet
etat ca dhanaṃ sva-abhilaṣita-rītyā vyayīkartuṃ bhavān sa-adhikāraḥ asti ityapi tayā saṃsthayā sūcitam āsīt
kim saṃketaḥ śābda-bodha-kāraṇam uta saṃketa-jñānam
nir-spṛhaḥ sarva-kāmebhyaḥ nirgatā dṛṣṭa-adṛṣṭa-viṣayebhyaḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā yasya yoginaḥ saḥ yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ iti ucyate tadā tasmin kāle
doṣaḥcaekaḥ samutpattau dehaḥ sarva-auṣadha-kṣamaḥ
kārakeṇa kriyā-anukūla-vyāpāra vatābhavitavyam
tathā a-vyakta-rasaṃ vidyātaindraṃ kāraṃ himaṃ ca yat
yathā-prakṛti caāhāraḥ malāyana-gada-auṣadham
rujā-nistoda-bahulā sūkṣma-chidrā ca jālinī
vātikīṃ paittikīṃ tṛṣṇā-dāha-moha-mada-jvaraiḥ
yoga-mārge pravṛttaḥ saṃnyāsī sāmarthyāt prāpya gatvā puṇya-kṛtām aśvamedha-ādi-yājinām lokān
mama mukha-pidhāna-mātreṇa vā bhavān etat satyaṃ nigūhituṃ na śaknoti yat bhavādṛśaḥ krūraḥ
vyākaraṇasya adbhuta-adbhuteṣu dhātu-rūpeṣu sandhiṣu samāseṣu tasya pratibhā tathā pravavṛte yena hi loka-vi-lakṣaṇānām vākyānām saḥ hi sṛṣṭim akārṣīt
na-ati-dūre sthitāyām śilāyām upaviṣṭavān
paraṃ dvi-kāla-pāyī syātahnaḥ kāleṣu buddhimān
utsanna-kula-dharmāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janārdana
evam gabhīrāyām nadyāmiti bhāgasya gabhīra-nadī-tīra-vṛttau lakṣaṇā svīkriyate
tatra vādi-prativādinoḥ pituḥ ekam eva nāma dṛṣṭvā guru-mahat-rājena tam etasya rahasyam apṛcchat
tayoḥtu pratyayaḥ prādhānyena iti vacanāt dhātu-artha-viśeṣya tayā ākhyātayā siddhaḥ
apareṇa prati-utpannam-itināmnā matsyenaabhihitam bhaviṣyatarthe pramāṇābhātvātkutra mayā gantavyam
purovāta-ātapa-avaśyāya-atipravātān jahyāt
na hi na-prāpta-viṣaya-ākāṅkṣā brahman-vidaḥ upapadyate
tu-śabdaḥ pakṣa-vyāvṛtti-arthaḥ na kevalebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ
tadvat ca kārya-karaṇa-vyāpāreṣu na-vyāpṛtaḥ anyaḥ tad-vilakṣaṇaḥ teṣām kārya-karaṇānām sarva-vyāpārāṇām sāmīpyena draṣṭā upadraṣṭā
na ayam lokaḥ sarva-prāṇi-sādhāraṇaḥ api asti yathā uktānām yajñānām ekaḥ api yajñaḥ yasya na asti saḥ na-yajñasya tasya
citra-padasya go-pada-lakṣaṇā-tātparya-grāhaka tve citra-pada-go-padayoḥ eka-vākya tā lakṣaṇasya vyapekṣā-sāmarthyasya abhāvena samāsaḥ eva na syātityapi na
tathāpi saḥ bhūta-āviṣṭaḥ iva ā-dinaṃ patrikā-kārye śabda-koṣa-nirmāṇa-kārye vā ātmānaṃ vyāpārayan duḥkhaṃ vismarati
catuḥ-daśa-varṣāṇi araṇye yāpayitvā prati āgatya aham bhavatā meliṣyāmi iti uktam rāmeṇa
duhyamāna-abhinna-go-dohana-samāna-kāla-īna-gamana-āśrayaḥ iti bodham varṇayanti
nañ-artha-eka-deśa-pratiyogitva-anvayi-ādheyatva-vivakṣayā ghaṭasya na iti prayoga-āpattiḥ iti manyate
śrutiśravā avaśyam loka-kalyāṇa-kārakasya rājña darśanam kariṣyāma
heṣante mandura-sthāḥ turaga-vara-ghaṭāḥ bṛṃhanti kariṇaḥ
vijayanagara-bhū-pālaḥ kṛṣṇadevarāyaḥ yadā yasmin pradeśe kārya-arthaṃ vihartuṃ vā yāti sma
anyathā ghaṭamānayaiti vākyāt śabda-vṛtti-viṣayasya paṭasyaapi bodha-āpatteḥ
na hi sva-nāsikā-agra-saṃprekṣaṇam iha vidhitsitam
asmad-bhaktāḥ ca uttamām parama-artha-jñāna-lakṣaṇām bhaktim āśritāḥ
atyantam puṇya-śālinaḥ atra anna-kṣetra-pari-cālakā yeṣām sthāna-kṛtena dravya-vyayena śataśa chātrāḥ dīnāḥ api vidyām arjayanti
yāvat dhyāna-yoga-ārohaṇa-samarthaḥ tāvat gṛhasthena adhikṛtena kartavyam karma
prāṇa-parityāge sati mahat-arha-vastra-paridhānena kaḥ lābha sādhāraṇena vastreṇa eva yadi kāryam calati cet tarhi vyartham eva vartate mṛta-śarīre mahat-arha-vastra-dhāraṇam
sa sīmā-anta-vāsibhyaḥ su-guptām ekāṃ yuktiṃ prakathya tataḥ nirgataḥ
ākhyāta-artheṣu kasya guṇatvam kasya prādhānyamiti vicikitsāyām ākhyāta-artha-saṃkhyā-ādi-apekṣayā bhāvanāyāḥ prādhānyam bodhayati nirukta-matam iti tu na yuktam
kārya-kramasya ante taiḥ daśa-sahasra-ḍālarmitamūlya-yutaṃ deya-ādeśa-patraṃ tasmai samarpitaṃ yena saḥ agre nirbādhaṃ svīyaṃ lekhana-kāryam anuvartayet iti teṣām āśayaḥ āsīt
kintu sarva-vyāpinā bhagavatā eva asmākam pūrva-janma-puṇyaiḥ tasmāt mocitā vayam iti kaḥ ayam viparīta-nyāyaḥ mahāśaya
śrīmān vibhūṣaṇa-maṇi-dyuti-rañjita-aṅgaḥ
prajā-hita-rataḥ prajānāṃ hite rataḥ
evam ātman-na-ātmanoḥ sat-na-satoḥ ubhayoḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhaḥ antaḥ nirṇayaḥ sat sat eva na-sat na-sat eva iti
sarvam eva agnihotra-ādikam karma śabda-samarpita-devatā-viśeṣa-saṃpradāna-ādi-kāraka-buddhimat kartṛ-abhimāna-phala-abhisaṃdhimat ca dṛṣṭam
mukha-dvārā dūṣita-mala-niḥsāraṇena eva ahaṃ jīveyam
patnī mālā sarva-gṛheṣu jala-siñcanam pātra-mārjana-ādi-kāryeṣu sāhāyyaṃ kṛtvā yatkiñcit prāptavatī
ayamca niṣkarṣaḥ vaiyākaraṇa-bhūṣaṇa-sāra-kāśikāyām pradarśitaḥasti
na tathā rājan-yajamāna-ādīnām sva-vyāpāraḥ na upalabhyate
rasana-vidyā-vidaḥ rasikāḥ iti ca ālaṃkārikān dārśanikāḥiti naiyāyikānca vyavaharanti
tyakta-vyāyāma-cintānāṃ saṃśodhanam a-kurvatām
tathā anvaya-bodha-prayojikāyāḥ tayoḥ
āmantritānām kṛte cāya-pāna-ādi kam
pitari pramīte mādhavasiṃha gaḍhavāla-rājyasya senā-pati-padam prāpnot
dayārāmaḥ yadā kamapi dīnam bālakam apaśyat tadā saḥ sva-bālya-kālam smarati sma
sāmpradāyika-kalahasya ādhikyasya kāraṇāt rājakīya-ādeśa-anusāraṃ nagare niṣedha-ājñāyāḥ karphyū ghoṣaṇā kṛtā
janman-antara-kṛtaḥ dharma-ādi-saṃskāraḥ maraṇa-kāle abhivyaktaḥ svabhāvaḥ ucyate
eka-bhāryā-vrataṃ śreṣṭham ekā bhāryā hi saukhya-dā
kintu ahaṃ veda-abhyāsa-nirataḥ
tamuvāca bhagavānātreyaḥ dhānya-phala-mūla-sāra-puṣpa-kāṇḍa-patra-tvacaḥ bhavanti āsava-yonayaḥ agniveśa saṃgraheṇaaṣṭau śarkarā-navamīkāḥ
marīciḥ nāma marutām marut-devatā-bhedānām asmi
tatuktam samāse khalu bhinnāeva śaktiḥ paṅka-ja-śabda vat
dhūma-pada-upasthita-dhūmena vahneḥanumātum śakyatvena anya-labhya tvāt
udareṣuatha caarśaḥsu gulmi-kuṣṭhi-kilāsiṣu
guṇa-aguṇa-parijñānaṃ
atha tathā etām na-pratiruddha-prasarām asya kavitva-śaktim tathā dharme eka-para tām para-rahasya-udghāṭana-vidhura tām ca na-lakṣya nitarām druta-antaḥkaraṇa rājā bhūyo bhūyaḥ asya pāda-tale luloṭha
vayam same api bālā tasya rūpa-śīla-guṇaiḥ ākṛṣṭā jijñāsava iva tasyām gṛham gata-āgati kam akurma
ke janaka-ādayaḥ janaka-aśvapati-prabhṛtayaḥ
iti śrīmat-bhagavat-gītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde viśvarūpa-darśanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ
prauḍhāvasthāyām ca bahu-kāla-anantaram vivāhaḥ tasyāḥ samabhūt iti-ādi
vṛddha-daiva-jña-nara-hariṇā mārga sandarśita
prajvalita-agni-śikhāsu devībhiḥ sva-prāṇānām āhutiḥ dattā
ati-bala-sukha-śāyī pūrvam āsīḥ hari-indraḥ
mahat-ūrmi-mālām manasā api dus-tarām
pūrva-abhighāta-sarujaḥ api anubhūta-duḥkhaḥ padmāvatīmapi tathāeva samarthayāmi
praduṣṭa-bahu-tīkṣṇa-uṣṇaiḥ madyaiḥanyaiḥca tadvidhaiḥ
nanu prayoga-atiprasaṅga-vāraṇe datta-dṛṣṭīnām naiyāyikānām śābda-bodha-varṇana-paddhatiḥ vastu-anurodhinī api na anuśāsana-anurodhinī
druma-ālayam pakva-phala-ambu-bhojanam
divya-astraiḥ sura-daitya-dānava-camū-vidrāvaṇam rāvaṇam
yathā sā prāṇa-rakṣā-arthaṃ palāyamānā eva adṛśyata iti
yuvati-jana-sahāyaḥ rājan-mārga-pradīpaḥ
abhihitena pada-arthena karaṇena anvayaḥ saṃsarga-bodhaḥ iti abhihita-anvaya-vādam urarīkurvanti
tatra tad-avagāhi-jñānasya bhramatvam
tattva-abhāve ca ghaṭaḥ jāyate iti kartṛ-ākhyāta-prayogaḥ kathamupapadyate iti āśaṅkā-parihārāya tad-sūtram pravṛttam
deveśaḥ ca śānti-senāyā sama-vibhaktena dalena saha sarvadā jāgaruka sva-grāma-nagara-kṣetra-rakṣaṇam kartum udyukta divā-niśam vyacarat
śastraṃ śāstrāṇi salilaṃ guṇa-doṣa-pravṛttaye
tathāanyāḥ piḍakāḥ santi rakta-pīta-asita-aruṇāḥ
vidyut-latā-kapila-tuṅga-jaṭā-kalāpam
viṣa-sveda-atiyoga-ārtāḥ stambhanīyāḥ nidarśitāḥ
ācārya-uttamaḥ śrīmān rāmacaṃdra-mahat-udayaḥ mama guruḥ iti paraspara-paricayam kṛtvā raṃganātham samāliṃgitavān mukuṃdaḥ
tataḥ nṛ-paḥ apṛcchat yadyevaṃ tarhi brūhi śiśirasya śreṣṭhatama-miṣṭa-annasya kiṃ nāma puro-hitaḥ babhāṣe śīte tu apūpāḥ
