tame varṣe kasmiṃścit dine benyahūdaḥ śubha-vārtāṃ prāptavān yat tadīya-cintanā-anusāraṃ dvi-sahasra-varṣāṇām anantaraṃ sarva-prathamaḥ hībrū-mātṛ-bhāṣikaḥ śiśuḥ tasya gṛhe jātaḥ
madhyama-vṛddha-pravṛttiḥ ca saṃvādīnīiti tayā saṃsṛṣṭa-artha-jñānam anumātum śakyate eva
rahasye vivṛte tau kaśā-ghāta-pūrvaṃ sva-padāt cyāvitau abhūtām
na ca bodhakatva-jñānāt iva arthe pada-bodhya-tva-jñānāt iva śābda-bodha-udayena bodhakatvamiva
jāgatīyaṃ nānā-veṣa-dharā
mayi arpita-manas-buddhiḥ saṃkalpa-vikalpa-ātmakam manaḥ
karmatayā darśana-kriyāyām anvaya-svīkāreṇa pada-eka-vākya tvam dhāvanasya darśana-karma tvam ca iti ubhayam api siddham bhavati
bhadre avahitā bhava śīta-candana-nilayam malayam prayāsyāvaḥ
saḥ vibhakta-aneka-ātma-viparīta-darśibhyaḥ viśiṣyate saḥ eva paśyati iti
tathā na-sat-jana-goṣṭhīṣu patiṣyasi patiṣyasi
pavana-pṛthvī-guṇa-atirekāt kaṣāyaḥ iti
putraḥ tarhi śāsakāḥ kiṃ kurvanti teṣu kiṃ deśa-rakṣā-bhāvanā na asti
rāsa-līlā-prasaṃgena vipralambha-śṛṅgāram uddīpayan sarveṣām api janānām manāṃsi sa āvarjayati
vidyādharaḥ saudāmani puṣpitānām nagānām ṣaḍ-bhāga-grahaṇam asmākam dharmaḥ
te tu ālocanā-śakti-rahitāḥ
tasmāt a-cira-utthitāṃ vidradhīṃ śastra-sarpa-vidyut-agni-tulyāṃ sneha-virecanaiḥ āśuevaupakramet sarvaśaḥ gulmavatcaiti
dhṛtā anya-strī-rūpam kṣiti-pati-gṛhe vā nivasati
na-iṣṭa-phala-hetoḥ ca nivartitaḥ asmi iti
riṃkcara-vāṣpa-śvasanam kuru
iti uktvā samīpa-vartinaḥ cināra-nāmaka-pādapa-viśeṣasya mūle sthāpitam tasya āyata-daṇḍam uddhṛtya tasmai pradadau
yogam ca karman-anuṣṭhāna-lakṣaṇam anutiṣṭha iti uktavān
tasmāt na-jñātasya viśeṣaṇa-viśeṣya-saṃsargasya viṣayatāeva pramāṇa-prayojyā bhavatiiti na pramāṇa-janyam jñānam
na-dharmaḥ-abhibhavāt kṛṣṇa praduṣyanti kula-striyaḥ
deha-ādi-vyatirikta-ātma-darśinaḥ rāga-dveṣa-ādi-prahāṇa-apekṣa-dharma-adharma-pravṛtti-upaśamāt mucyante iti na kenacit pratyākhyātum śakyam nyāyataḥ
evam nigadantyā mama roṣa-arakta-locana-dvandvāt nisṛtā rakta-sphuliṅgā
vīramatiḥ tu sva-svāminam mṛtyu-mukha-praviṣṭam iva matvā madhya eva tām tathā atāḍayat yathā chinna-mūlā latā iva sā sahasā iva bhūmau apatat
āsāṃ hṛd-nābhi-basti-jāḥ paripakvāḥ sānnipātikī ca maraṇāya
sphijau yasya samānāḥ saḥ sama-vibhakta-aṅgaḥ iti kathyate
śrauta-nitya-karma-rahitatvāt iti
śāpa-kāraṇa taḥ ahalyā vāyu-mātram sevamānā na-dṛśya-rūpeṇa eva vasantī āśrame samādhi-sthā jātā
baṃga-prāntasya pratiṣṭhitaḥ sāmājikaḥ ayam bhinna-śikṣaṇa-saṃsthānām sañcālakaḥ sañjātaḥ
iha tu puruṣakāra-sāra-sākṣī
eṣā mayā prakāśyate iti kriyā-kāraka-prayojanam
sāmānyataḥ tad-viṣayaka-śābda-bodhe vṛtti-jñāna-janya-tad-upasthiteḥ hetutva-svīkāre
yadi hi īśvarasya ātman-bhūtāḥ te matāḥ na-bheda-darśitvāt
ātman-kalpita-tantu-jāla-niviṣṭā lūtā iva sā ekākini eva yāpayati dinam
bhavān dharma-ācaraṇa-śīlaḥ kṛta-parama-īśvara-sākṣātkāraḥ ca vartate
daśaratha-putraḥ yadā vana-vāsa-arthaṃ daṇḍaka-araṇyam āgataḥ tadā agastyasya darśana-arthaṃ tasya āśramaṃ gataḥ
yathā jala-sūryakaḥ sūrya-aṃśaḥ jala-nimitta-apāye sūryam eva gatvā na nivartate ca tena eva ātmanā gacchati
ghaṭatva-aṃśe nir-vikalpaka-pratyakṣa-ātmankam vākya-na-janyam śvetaḥaśvaḥ dhāvati iti-ākārakam śābda-jñānam padam vināapi jāyate iti vyatireka-vyabhicāraḥ syāt
nirīkṣaṇena viditam abhavat yat śākānāṃ pacane prayujyamānāyāṃ rājikāyāṃ kṛṣṇa-varṇa-pāṣāṇa-cūrṇasya miśraṇam asti samrāje ādeśena rājikāḥ vikretāraḥ viṃśatiḥ āpaṇikāḥ nigṛhītāḥ abhavan
ubhau api pravara-uccāraṇa-pūrvakaṃ kahoḍam abhivāditavantau
kim vā na naśyati na-pratiṣṭhaḥ nirāśrayaḥ he mahat-bāho vimūḍhaḥ san brahmaṇaḥ pathi brahman-prāpti-mārge
sva-svāmin-bhāva-saṃbandhena rājan-viśiṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ sva-svāmin-bhāva-saṃbandhena bhāryā-viśiṣṭaḥ iti bodha-tātparyeṇa rājan-puruṣaḥ bhāryāyāḥca iti na prayujyate
dinakaravarmā tasya eka-mātra-putraḥ
bālye eva saḥ mātṛ-pitṛ-viyogam prāptavān āsīt
nijasya tu mukhaṃ vāta-pitta-śleṣmaṇāṃ vaiṣamyam
kukkuraḥ ca dhāvitvā ākheṭa-arthaṃ niḥsṛtānāṃ bhīma-arjuna-ādīnāṃ samīpe prāptaḥ
tasya jñānaṃ viśālaṃ gambhīraṃ ca iti viditvā munayaḥ api tad-āśramam āgatya dharma-brahma-daiva-ādiṣu viṣayeṣu sva-saṃśayān nivedya aṣṭāvakrasya mukhāt parihārān labdhvā santuṣṭāḥ gacchanti sma
sarva-bhūta-rataḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu rataḥ
na caevam svīkurvanti ākhyātāt kartṛ-bodha-vādinaḥ vaiyākaraṇāḥ mīmāṃsakāḥ vā
iti abhiyukta-ukti-virodhaḥ iti vācyam
na ca tīratvenaupasthite śakya-sambandha-jñānasya āvaśyakatvena niyata-upasthitikasya tīratvasyaabhāne kim niyāmakamiti vācyam
kadācit ayam purāṇa-patha-anuyāyī dhauta-dhāra paṇḍitaḥ api āṅgalīm bhāṣām jānānaḥ bhavet iti śaṃkā tu tayoḥ abhūt kintu sa-āścaryam tau parasparam smitavantau
nitya-naimittikānām anuṣṭhīyamānānām sarva-karmaṇām ātman-saṃbandhitayā prāptasya phalasya parityāgaḥ sarva-karma-phala-tyāgaḥ tam prāhuḥ kathayanti tyāgam tyāga-śabda-artham vicakṣaṇāḥ paṇḍitāḥ
vedeṣu hi ku-tārkika-racita-ku-tarka-viplāvita-prāmāṇyeṣu
kṛtvā sva-vīrya-sadṛśaṃ paramaṃ prayatnaṃ krīḍā-mayūram iva śatrum a-cintayitvā
rājan-bhavana-samīpe eva tasya vāsāya rājñā vyavasthā kalpitā
guru-mahat-udaya yasya tat dhanaṃ vartate saḥ puruṣaḥ tat dhanaṃ svīkartuṃ na eva abhilaṣati
sva-nārī-jīvanam dhanyam manyamānāyā me vapuḥ harṣeṇa romāñcitam babhūva
buddhimatāṃ ca svālakṣaṇya-anumāna-yukti-kuśalānām an-uktārtha-jñānāya iti
teṣu ca paṃkti-agre lajjayā veṣṭitā dhṛta-śveta-paridhānā saralatāyā mūrtiḥ iva pra-sphuṭita-yauvana-aṃgī dhūrjaṭeḥ ārādhane tapas-līnā āparṇā iva bālā āsīt
pārivārika-vicāra-upakrame prāyaśaḥ vibhāvinī vivāha-viṣayaḥ eva abhavat carcā-bindu
sā vīramati roma-kaṇṭaka-aṅkitā
svapna-marīci-udaka-māyā-gandharva-nagara-samatvāt
vivāhasya varṣa-traya-anantaram lalāṭa-lipyā yat kimapi kṛtam tena kavi-kula-guro raghuvaṃśatṛtīyasargastham
mandai-bhavanti maṇi-dīpa-hatāḥ pradīpāḥ
tāpasī magadha-tapas-vana-vāsinī
ekadā maṃgalasiṃhena vicāritam janā prati-varṣam tīrtha-yātrā-artham gacchanti
gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti-ādau gaṅgā-pada-upasthāpitaḥ pravāhaḥ sva-saṃbandhin tīram smārayati
puruṣā striyaḥ ca ubhe api kaṭhora-śrama-sādhyām astra-śastra-dīkṣām sa-ullāsam gṛhītavanta
rajjvā yayā ayam stambhe nyabadhyata tasyā granthīn nipuṇam sva-kara-ruha-agraiḥ viślathayitum prāyatata
tāṃ śilāmatha kurvīta kauṣeya-āvika-saṃstarām
dīpta-anala-arka-dyutim na-prameyam
na tasya kāma-īpsutva-bahula-āyāsa-kartṛtva-prāptiḥ asti
megha-āgamāt manaḥtāpāt deśa-kāla-viparyayāt
sīmā-su-rakṣā-vyājena taiḥ sīmā-anta-grāmā dhvastāḥ kṛṣi-bhūmayaḥ vināśitāḥ tatratyā janatā ca atyācāraiḥ prapīḍitā
patiḥ pratyuvāca param madīya-badarī-vṛkṣe mā gaccha
samīpe ca śānta-gambhīra-mudrayā kiśorī sthitā ekaḥ ca rakṣā-puruṣa kiśāryā pṛṣṭha-deśam adhyāste
ayam nanu lalita-gambhīra-ākṛti-viśeṣaḥ
tataḥasau bhikṣuḥ tatkṣaṇāt suvarṇa-pūrṇa-kalaśaḥ bhaviṣyati
kim meru-mandara-kulam parivartayāmi
deha-ādi-saṃghāta-ātman-darśana-abhimāna-abhāvāt teṣām
nairāśyaṃ pratipannaḥ veṅkaṭaḥ sva-niketanaṃ prāpya upāya-cintane tatparaḥ abhavat yena tasya bhūri-śrama-upārjitaṃ dravyaṃ punaḥ prāptaṃ syāt
anicchan api kāle eka-niyantrita-gatiḥ gacchāmi tvām parityajya na ca nirgacchanti amī prāṇā
damanakaḥ saṃjīvaka-samīpam gatvāabravīt are vṛṣabha eṣaḥ rājñā piṅgalakena araṇya-rakṣā-artham niyuktaḥ senā-patiḥ karaṭakaḥ samājñāpayati satvaramāgaccha
etāni api bhavadbhiḥ loka-sevā-maṇḍalāya dattāni lekhanīṃ parāvartayan ṭaṇḍana-mahānubhāvaḥ udatarat bandhu-vara mama sapta ātman-jāḥ santi
mayā yadā hīraka-prāpti-patraṃ darśayitum uktaḥ
evam go-viṣayatā api go-pada-prayojyā iti
pitā vatsa deśa-rakṣā-artham ete bali-dānaṃ kurvanti
brahmā eva tena gantavyam brahma-karma-samādhinā
amba pituḥ rogasya apa-nayana-artham vidyutsañcālitam-dvīpe sthitasya tulasī-sasyasya mūlam āvaśyakam
rājāślādyām avanti-nṛpateḥ sadṛśīṃ tanū-jāṃ kāla-krameṇa punaḥ āgata-dāra-bhāraḥ
drava-snigdha-śīta-manda-mṛdu-picchila-rasa-guṇa-bahulāni āpyāni
darśita-unmatta-kṛtyaḥ api hasasi
vyutpitsu-jana-bodhāya tathā sva-mati-śuddhaye
samāna-guṇa-abhyāsaḥ hi dhātūnāṃ vṛddhi-kāraṇam iti
sārivā-śarkarā-pāṭhā-mañjiṣṭhā-drākṣā-pīlu-parūṣaka-abhayā-āmalaka-bibhītakāni iti daśaimāni jvaraharāṇi bhavanti
mahābhārata-yuddha-sthale ekā garbhiṇī gṛdhrī api kenacit bāṇena āhatā nyapatat
maru-sthale maru-udyānam iva manas-ramā-ramāṃ prati eva nayana-vikṣepaḥ jātaḥ paraṃ śuṣka-saikatam iva pratīyamānaṃ tasya kṣīṇatvam na-dṛṣṭam eva
tam na-mānitva-ādi-gaṇam jñāna-sādhanatvāt jñāna-śabda-vācyam vidadhāti bhagavān
asmat-ruci-anukūlām sāṭikām dadhānām tvam svayam eva ādarśaya
tasmāt sa-putra-dāraḥ tvam
dvitīyaḥ abravīt etayā pāpi-ṣṭhayā kati mūṣakāḥ mūṣikāḥ ca udara-sthī-kṛtā iti gaṇayituṃ na śakyate
yat asmin varṣa-utsave vana-vāsinaḥ mūrti-kārasya kalāyāḥ sammānaḥ bhaviṣyati tat nirmitāṃ vṛṣṭi-devyāḥ pratimāṃ rājan-bhavana-udyānasya madhya-vedikāyāṃ pratiṣṭāpayiṣyāmaḥ
vṛnda-araṇya-gate sama-pramuditā gāyanti kecit sthitāḥ
madhyāhne dāsā dāsyaḥ ca kṛṣi-kārya-artham kṣetra-bhūmim gatā
brahma-ṛṣi-rūpeṇa bhavān śvapākaḥ
janaka-mahat-rājasya śāsane sarvepi ītidūrāḥ bhīti-muktāḥ sukhena jīvanti sma
tava pitā nitarāṃ kārya-vyāpṛtaḥ adhunā tu nirataḥ syāt anyasya dur-vicāra-pūrṇasya lekhasya sajjīkaraṇe
yat śaurya-kīrtaya kramaśaḥ tadānīntana dillī-īśvara-karṇau api aspṛśan
sarasa-hṛdayaḥ vivekānandaḥ karuṇā-mūrtiḥ kārya-ācaraṇa-dakṣaḥ ca
kapha-śukra-anila-haraṃ kaṇḍū-koṭha-vināśanam
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat he rājan bhavān kasmaicit kiñcana vāk-dānam kṛtavān asti iti mama bhāti
adhika-dhanena mama kiṃ vā prayojanam guru-dakṣiṇā-arthaṃ yāvat āvaśyakaṃ tāvat eva paryāptam
prātaḥ dharma-śālā taḥ prasthāya sāyaṃ-kāla-samaye tau ekam araṇyam praviṣṭavantau
tathā ca itara-viśeṣaṇa tayāapi bodhakatva-jñānasya śābda-bodha-kāraṇa tve ghaṭa-padam na ghaṭa-dhī-janakam iti jānataḥ ghaṭa-pada-janya-maitra-jñāna-viṣayaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti jñānāt śābda-bodha-āpattiḥ iti vācyam
sva-gupta-kalām śikṣayiṣyāmi
yadi ghaṭa-śabdasya bāhya-sattā-viśiṣṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ vācyaḥ tadā ghaṭa-śabdena eva bāhya-sattāyāḥ bodhanāt ukta-arthānām na-prayogaḥ iti nyāyena astiiti prayogaḥ na syāt
tathā duḥkheṣu adhyātman-adhibhūta-adhidaiva-nimitteṣu
he mahat-mantrin śvaḥ dyūta-krīḍā-viśeṣān mahyam anu-kṣaṇaṃ vinivedayantu
kintu bhavataḥ eṣā vastra-kṣālana-vṛttiḥ mahyam na rocate
iti śrīmad-bhagavadgītāsu upaniṣatsu brahma-vidyāyām yoga-śāstre śrīkṛṣṇa-arjuna-saṃvāde arjuna-viṣāda-yogaḥ nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ
tvat-prayāṇa-samaye asmābhiḥ tubhyaṃ ye varāḥ anugṛhītāḥ te varāḥ agre te atīva upayuktāḥ bhaviṣyanti
yat balam kāma-rāga-vivarjitam aiśvaram rūpam jagat-vidhāraṇāya pṛthivyām āviṣṭam yena pṛthivī gurvī na adhaḥ patati na vidīryate ca
tayā ca tasya uparitana-bhavana-śāyitvam avagatya vīramati-samadhiṣṭhitasya bhavanasya dvāre gatvā tat-udghāṭanāya śabdam akarot
kasmāt kāryate pravartyate hi yasmāt na-vaśaḥ eva na-svatantraḥ eva karma sarvaḥ prāṇī prakṛti-jaiḥ prakṛtitaḥ jātaiḥ sattva-rajas-tamobhiḥ guṇaiḥ
pada-artha-upasthitau śakti-jñāna-lakṣaṇā-jñānayoḥ api pratyekam kāraṇatva-kalpanayā ca gauravam
ayaṃ śuka-mahat-ṛṣiḥ janmanā eva vairāgyaṃ prāptavān
rājā yaśodhare kim tvayā mātaṅgī-jana-praveśaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ
klaibyaṃ śukra-a-visargaḥ ca kṣīṇa-śukrasya lakṣaṇam
tatra ekaṃ viśālaṃ virūpa-akṣa-mandiram
pāpa-vṛtta-vacaḥ-sattvāḥ sūcakāḥ kalaha-priyāḥ
sura-indra-nāthaḥ asura-vīrya-hantā
karman-phala-tyāgaḥ eva sāttvikatvena guṇena tāmasatva-ādi-apekṣayā saṃnyāsaḥ ucyate
purātana-tāḍa-patrāṇi sarvāṇi dṛṣṭāni
sīmā-anta-vāsinaḥ eva praṣṭavyāḥ
dvauetau prāṇa-deha-arthau proktau vaidya-guṇa-āśrayau
asmad-karma-kṛt asmad-paramaḥ asmad-bhaktaḥ saṅga-varjitaḥ
karman-akarma-vijñānāt api gauṇāt phalasya na-śravaṇāt
tarhi asmad-karma-paramaḥ bhava asmad-artham karma asmad-karma tad-paramaḥ asmad-karma-paramaḥ
viparīta-darśitvāt aneka-candra-darśivat ityarthaḥ
tṛṣṇā-saṅgayoḥ samudbhavam tṛṣṇā-āsaṅga-samudbhavam
evaṃ prakāreṇa duryodhanena punaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ dyūta-krīḍā-artham āhūya parābhūtāḥ
yata-indriya-manas-buddhiḥ muniḥ mokṣa-parāyaṇaḥ
vāta-pitta-viṣa-unmāda-śoṣa-alakṣmī-jvara-apaham
śrīvasiṣṭhasya nava-nirmāṇa-kṣamatāṃ caitanyasya sphuliṃgam ca dṛṣṭvā saḥ svam ācārya-padaṃ tasmai samarpitavān
tathā ca nirukta-kārya-tā-avacchedaka-koṭau lākṣaṇika-vyakti-viśeṣa-abheda-bodha-bhinna tvam deyamiti grantha-kṛtām tātparyāt
draupadī sairandhrī bhūtvā dāsī-kāryam akarot na-jñāta-vāsasya ante taiḥ sva-paricayaḥ virāṭ-mahat-rājāya dattaḥ
mūrdhā-añcita-eka-caraṇaḥ cala-bāhu-ketuḥ
ākulai-kṛtya ca haranti prasabham prasahya prakāśam eva paśyataḥ viveka-vijñāna-yuktam manaḥ
tam tathā kṛpayā āviṣṭam aśru-pūrṇa-ākula-īkṣaṇam
yat saḥ adyaprabhṛti asmākaṃ priya-na-tithim api sa-sammānaṃ paśyatu
nidāghasya pratapta-ātape rājadhānyāḥ pratapta-lauha-pātrāṇi iva mārgāḥ yadā su-taptāḥ bhavanti tadā teṣu gamana-āgamanasya kā vārtā tān prati cakṣuṣ-unmīlanam api asidhārā-vrataṃ bhavati
paśyāmi tvāṃ dīpta-hutāśa-vaktram
śabdātamumartham pratyemiiti pratīteḥ bādhaka-bhāvena śabda-janya-tva-na-avagāhi tayā vākya-artha-buddheḥ śabda-janya tāeva prāmāṇikī
sabhāyāṃ kara-tala-dhvanayaḥ ca śrūyate
tataḥ ca parijana-vargasya haṭha-prārthanā-paravaśena rāyamahodayena dvitīya udvāha āracita
tat-kathana-samakālam eva gadādharaḥ bhagavān yamaḥ prakaṭitaḥ abhavat
evañca prathamā-anta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-ka-bodhasya siddhatvāt sarvatraeva tasya mukhya-viśeṣya tayā bhānamucitamiti cet
rājan-sabhā-avasāne nṛ-paḥ tenālīrāmam uvāca asmin alpīyasi kāla-avadhau mantriṇā kīdṛśaṃ duṣkaraṃ karma sampāditam
śaiśava-avasthāyām śrutām siṃha-sūkara-yuddha-kathām asmarat ayam
ghaṭamānaya iti-ādau bālena prathamataḥ gṛhīta-ānayana-kārya-viśeṣa-anvite śakti-grahe api paścāt kārya-viśeṣe
tatra rāṣṭra-niṣṭha-janānāṃ saṅghaṭanam karaṇīyam
ākhyāta-dvi-vacanāt dvitvamapiiti ubhaya-vidha-anubhavaḥ api śābdaḥ eva natuanyatarasyaapi na-śābdatvam kalpanīyam
dambha-ahaṅkāra-saṃyuktāḥ kāma-rāga-bala-anvitāḥ
tattva-vit ātmanaḥ yāthātmyam tattvam vetti iti tattva-vit parama-artha-darśi ityarthaḥ
kim tat parama-artha-tattvam sthita-prajñasya viṣayaḥ
tad-anantaram na-jñāta-vāsaḥ āsīt
bahu-dina-ante samāyātaṃ su-puṣṭagātraṃ patiṃ nirīkṣya duṣṭā ramābāī muditā ajāyata
tailaṃ vāta-śleṣma-praśamanānāṃ
tad-tad-saṃsargaka-bodhe tādṛśa-tādṛśa-samabhivyāhāra-jñānasya hetutvam kalpanīyamiti anantāḥ kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvāḥ prasajyante eva śābda-bodhe sarvatra saṃbandhaḥ viśeṣa-rūpeṇa eva saṃsarga-maryādayā bhāsate
dvandvaiḥ vimuktāḥ sukha-duḥkha-sañjñaiḥ
yajña-dāna-tapa-karma na tyājyam iti ca na-pare
gṛha-kārya-ādīnām karaṇe yadi api kaṣṭam bhavati sma
yathā ghaṭa-ādi-upādhi-paricchinnaḥ ghaṭa-ādi-ākāśaḥ ākāśa-aṃśaḥ san ghaṭa-ādi-nimitta-apāye ākāśam prāpya na nivartate
vāta-śleṣma-vibandheṣu rasaḥtasyaupadiśyate
tatra ca ekasmāt sajjanāt lekhanīṃ gṛhītvā caikapatraṃ loka-sevā-maṇḍala-nāmnā deyaṃ likhitavān
yat gṛhe gītā-rāmāyaṇa-ādayaḥ na milanti saḥ kiṃ na bhavati
tadā vṛttim vināapi ākāṃkṣā-balena tātparya-jñāna-anvaya-bodha-nirvāhāt naanvaye vṛttiḥ kalpyate
vatsāyā na-parimita-guṇa-ākṛṣṭa-hṛdayaḥ tathā mita-upakāra-bhārāt nata vismayasya parām koṭim ārūḍhaḥ tām ālokayan sāmiparimlānasmṛtiparamparayā bhṛśam ākulaḥ abhūt
tasyāḥca śakya-saṃbandha-grahāt eva jātatvena
janānāṃ śirasi saḥ viśāla-kāya-parvataḥ chatram iva abhavat
tatyathā sraṃsa-bhraṃśa-vyāsa-saṅga-bheda-sāda-harṣa-tarṣa-kampa-varta-cāla-toda-vyathā-ceṣṭā ādīni
viṣṇuḥ vā vikasita-puṇḍarīka-netraḥ
vamī-atīsāra-hṛdroga-visūcī-alasaka-jvarāḥ
yadi tathā bhavati tarhi kimanena svāmin-ceṣṭā-nirūpaṇena asmākam
tatākhyātamiti nirukta-arthaḥ iti naetasya dhātu-artha-viśeṣya tve pramāṇatāiti vācyam
etena preritā anye sam-upasthi-janā api yat kiñcit samarpayiṣyanti
etāvatā gadādhara-bhaṭṭācāryāṇām śābda-nirūpaṇa-paddhatiḥ kiñcitiva cintitā
ammo iyam sa-ati-snigdhayā dṛṣṭyā kena api manuṣyeṇa pibanti iva saha mantrayamāṇā tiṣṭhati
kim kuryāt tapasvinī kutra milet rambhāyā gṛham api na-tithi-saṃkulam
kārya-ālaya-karmaṇā ekaḥ prativeśī kebhyaścit dinebhyaḥ ekākī eva sva-adhikāriṇā saha nagara-antaraṃ gataḥ āsīt
saḥ mukuṭa-dhārī uttara-mādhyamika-vidyālaye saṃskṛta-pravaktā āsīt
prajā-hita-dakṣaḥ tathā ādarśabhūtaḥ rājā āsīt
tat niśamya nara-patiḥ āha priye yadi kaścit kṣudraḥ api janaḥ kasmaicit kiñcit dadāti tarhi saḥ api sva-hasta-dattam vastu pratyādātum lajjate
bhoḥ sukhaṃ khalu niḥ-kalatrāṇāṃ kāntāra-pra-veśaḥ
tatra dhana-dhānya-samṛddheḥ tāṇḍavaṃ pratyakṣam āsīt
vilokya uditaḥ bhagavān sarva-jana-sāmānya-pradīpaḥ candraḥ
tadā tvacā jñātam iti-ādi-nirūḍha-lakṣaṇā-sthale api tvac-śabda-śakya-carmaṇā atyanta-na-bheda-na-pratīteḥ prayojanasya saṃbhavāt tatra prayojana-abhāva-kathanam asaṃgatamiti cet
para-hita-ghāte kuśalāḥ duṣṭāḥ kimapi kimapi kurvanti
ariṣṭarṣabhaḥ tena hi gṛhyatām sva-jāti-sadṛśam praharaṇam
ahamapi tāvat damayantī-svayaṃvara-arthaṃ eva gacchāmi khalu
na-phala-ākāṅkṣibhiḥ na-phala-arthibhiḥ yajñaḥ vidhi-dṛṣṭaḥ śāstra-codanā-dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ yajñaḥ ijyate nirvartyate
kacchapaḥ sva-hasta-pādān prasārya vyomni tartum aceṣṭata
yadi khalu tava darpaḥ mātṛ-pakṣaḥ-ugra-rūpaḥ
saṃsāra-pravṛtti-kāraṇatvāt iti
evam tām bhaktimatīm āgraha-ārūḍhām ca avalokya śvaśura-śyāla-prabhṛtīn sarvān janān āpṛcchaya
punaḥ anveṣṭuṃ parāvṛttaḥ saḥ śyāmaṃ vṛkṣe nilīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa-maunaṃ tataḥ nirgatya sarvān api daśa-dvādaśa-sva-parivāra-sadasyān siṃhān tatra ānītavān
varcaḥ-bhedīni alābūni rūkṣa-śīta-gurūṇi ca
na ca vidyamāna-sarva-viṣayaiṇyām ekasyām īśvara-icchāyām paṭaḥapi viśeṣyaḥ tathā ca
tataḥ kutaścit-deśāt-āgatya dīrghasya-mukhaḥ nāma bakaḥ praṇamya-upaviṣṭaḥ
sva-rakṣaṇa-artham ca parama-ātmani dhanyavāda-purasaram kṛtajñatām muhuḥ muhuḥ hṛd-antare samudairayat
bāṇa-viddha-bhīṣaṇa-kesariṇyā garjanam iva asmat-mukhāta
yukta-svapna-avabodhasya yogaḥ bhavati duḥkha-hā
mahat-bhāṣya-virodhena astreṇa sarvān pakṣān nirākurvanti
yadi buddhi-sattā-viśiṣṭa-ghaṭaḥ vācyaḥ
dadhīci-mahat-ṛrṣiḥ indraṃ madhuraiḥ śabdaiḥ pṛṣṭavān bhoḥ devendra
samasta-bhūmaṇḍala-ādhipatyena api na ahaṃ suprabhāṃ vismarāmi
tayoḥtu pratyayaḥ prādhānyena iti etad-viruddha-artha-kalpanāyāḥ na-yukta tvāt
yava-karaṇaka-tva-abhāva-viśiṣṭe yāge vrīhi-karaṇa tvasya caanvayamupagamya
niṣedha-vācaka-śabdaḥ tu tatratye kośa eva na likhita
balaṃ balavatāṃ ca ahaṃ kāma-rāga-vivarjitam
maharṣi-ramaṇaṃ girijā-gṛha-svāminaḥ kiṃ kathitavantaḥ
asau vijayanagarasya rājan-jyoti-rvidā sākaṃ gupta-patra-vyavahāram akārṣīt
tasmāt śābda-hetu-padārtha-upasthāpaka-pada-tad-artha-saṃbandha-rūpā vṛttiḥ mukhya-jaghanya-bhedena dvi-vidhā evaiti
paredyavi yadā te sammilitāḥ tadā benjhiyonasya mukha-udghāṭanāt-pūrvameva anyaḥ bālaḥ uktavān mitra bhavān jānāti kiṃ yat beran rothscailḍvaryaḥ jerūsaleṃ-nagaram āgamiṣyati iti
yuṣmat-anu-smṛtiḥ eva dhārayati me jīvanam
pratyuta bhinna-bhinna-kāraṇāni eva tasya mṛtyau niradiśat
pradhānaī-bhūta-pratyaya-artha-bodhaka tvasyaabhāvāt
saptakaḥayaṃ sadaurbalyaḥ śopha-upadrava-saṃgrahaḥ
sarve bhrātaraḥ ca sva-sva-kārye tādṛg vyāpṛtā abhūvan
yasmiṃn caṇḍa-gada-abhighāta-janitaḥ śabdaḥ samuttiṣṭhati
kṣara-ākhyasya puruṣasya utpatti-bījam aneka-saṃsārin-jantu-kāma-karma-ādi-saṃskāra-āśrayaḥ
saṃketa-graha-sa-apekṣāyāḥ evaabhidhāyāḥ upayogāt vyaṅgye saṃketa-graha-abhāvena sutarām abhidhayā nirvāha-asaṃbhavāt
idampadam etad-artha-bodhakam bhavatu iti saṃkete bodhakatvam viṣayaḥ
na sat-asat viruddhayoḥ sattva-na-sattvayoḥ ekatraayogāt itiāśaṅkya
mahat-arha-vastrasya yā vyavasthā mahat-rājena kṛtā āsīt tat-sambandhe yuva-rāja pradhāna-amātyasya karṇe ca akathayat bhavān anubhavī amātyaḥ vartate
yaḥ bhuṅkte sva-deha-indriyāṇi eva tarpayati stenaḥ eva taskaraḥ eva saḥ deva-ādi-sva-apahārī
tadā śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ avadat he rājan etādṛśe andhakāre bhavatā kim sādhanīyam iti kaṭhora-dīkṣā svīkṛtā iti aṃśaḥ mayā tu na jñāyate
tad-vidyajña-saṃbhāṣā buddhi-vardhanānām
purātanāni chinnāni ca pañcan-ṣāṇi vastrāṇi ekasya upari ekam iti krameṇa dhṛtvā tad-parivāra-janāḥ kathamapi śaityaṃ soḍhavantaḥ
pracchanna-veṣaḥ-dharaḥ vyāghraḥ api meṣaiḥ saha vraje nirudhdaḥ abhavat
hetu-arthasya ca na-vikriyatvasya tulyatvāt viduṣaḥ sarva-karma-pratiṣedhaḥ eva prakaraṇa-arthaḥ abhipretaḥ bhagavatā
tataḥasau sva-karma-vaśāt nir-āśaḥ kaṭakam praviṣṭaḥ
cakra-vyūhe sthitaḥ abhimanyuḥ ekākī eva śatru-pakṣe vidyamānānāṃ sarva-śreṣṭha-mahat-rathināṃ garva-bhaṅgaṃ kṛtavān
kiṃrūpametatvada bhadra tasya guṇa-aguṇa-jñaḥ sadṛśaṃ prapatsye
sarasvatyāḥ vara-da-putra
vibandha-gaurava-udgāra-hṛllāsa-arocaka ādayaḥ
parantu saḥ smṛtavān yat adya tu tātaḥ patrikā-mudraṇa-viṣaye vyastaḥ mudraṇa-ālaye tiṣṭhati iti
śatrughna-lakṣmaṇa-gṛhīta-ghaṭe abhiṣeke chatre svayaṃ nṛpatinā rudatā gṛhite
kārā-gṛha-adhipatinā bandhanād vimocya saḥ ajñāpta mā bhaviṣyati evam kārṣī
smarāmi tām rātrim yadā svakīya-adhyayana-kakṣe adhīyānasya mama pārśve samāgatya revatī sahasā provāca samīra
ete śruta-vayo-vṛddhāḥ jita-ātmānaḥ mahā-ṛṣayaḥ
idam tu jñeyam ati-indriyatvena śabda-eka-pramāṇa-gamyatvāt na ghaṭa-ādi vat ubhaya-buddhi-anugata-pratyaya-viṣayam ityataḥ na sat tat na asat iti ucyate
ādhunika-saṃketa-sthale bodhakatva-jñāna-abhāve api saṃketa-jñānāt eva śābda-bodha-utpattyā vyabhicāreṇa bodhakatva-jñānasya kāraṇatva-na-sambhavāt na bodhakatvam śaktiḥ
saḥ yogī sama-loṣṭa-aśman-kāñcanaḥ loṣṭa-aśman-kāñcanāni samāni yasya saḥ sama-loṣṭa-aśman-kāñcanaḥ
kriyā-atiyogaḥ śokaḥca vega-nidrā-vinigrahaḥ
he śrīhare iti vadanam anyataḥ parivṛtya etena na-nicchā-kṛta-pāpena mama rājan-makuṭaṃ kalā-vihīnaṃ jātaṃ iti manye
bhaveasmin pavano-ddhānta-vīci-vibhramabhaṅgure
na prathamā-anta-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kaḥ
dina-dvaya-pūrvasya eva vārtā pratīyate
tābhyām jñāna-vijñānābhyām tṛptaḥ saṃjāta-alam-pratyayaḥ ātmā antaḥkaraṇam yasya saḥ jñāna-vijñāna-tṛpta-ātmā
iti bhāgari-smṛti-abhiprāyakaḥ
anantaram ca pratyāsanne abhinandana-dine svayam eva nimantraṇa-patrāṇi mudrāpya samagreṣu bhārateṣu vidvas-samāje patra-ālaya-dvāreṇa rāmadayāluḥ tāni vitaritavān
āskara-puraskāra-samiteḥ sadasyāḥ bhāratam āgatya rugṇa-ālaye eva tasmai puraskāraṃ dattavantaḥ
calita-kakuda-vālaḥ prasphurat-pāda-karṇaḥ
mūrkha-rājan-pada-vi-bhūṣitaḥ
vayam iva bhava harṣa-bāṣpa-netraḥ
tasya abheda-sambandhena ghaṭa-pada-arthe anvayaḥ
mārge svāmī mām avadat yadi tvam idaṃ hīraka-lābha-vṛttaṃ kasyacit na prakāśayeḥ
tadānīm bāhyāyāḥ bhuvaḥabhāvena bauddha-pṛthivyām eva śakti-graha-pūrvakam hiraṇyagarbhasya bauddha-pṛthivī-bodhaḥ iti
śābda-bodha-samāna-ākāra-jñāna vataḥ veda-kartuḥ bhramavattvam naāpādayitum śakyate
sukha-prāptya-arthaṃ kiṃ karaṇīyam
sāmpratam vitta-vimūḍhā grāmyā api na smaranti guru-laghu-bhāvam
yoga-ādhikyena tu phenila-rakta-candrikā-upagamanam iti atiyoga-lakṣaṇāni bhavanti
na ca pratyakṣa-ādau viṣayatā-bhāna-niyama-nirvāhāya pada-bhānam āvaśyakamiti vācyam
nir-prayojana-artha-bodhaka tve na-jñāta-prayojana-vat-artha-bodhaka-tva-lakṣaṇa-prāmāṇya-anupapattyā prāśastye lakṣaṇāaṅgīkriyate
sa-lajja-nayanā aham tat-samīpam na-gamanam
na caetat saṃbhavati anvita-abhidhāna-anurodhinām akhyāti-vādinām
mahat-ātmanaḥ anena upadeśena śānta-manāḥ puruṣaḥ sa-aṣṭan-aṅgaṃ taṃ praṇamya tūṣṇīṃ gṛhaṃ prati prasthitaḥ
śva chātrāvāsa-bhojana-ālaye māsika-śulkam deyam syāt
dīpa-āloka-sūcita-rūpaḥ saḥ eva idānīm eṣaḥ
patrikā-sampādana-kāryaṃ tu tasyāḥ āsīt eva
viśvāsa-ghāta-kartā yaḥ narakaṃ saḥ adhigacchati
na ca lakṣyasyaapi śakyatā-avacchedaka-rūpeṇa eva bodha-svīkāre śakyātanyena rūpeṇa jñāte bhavati lakṣaṇā
saḥ tyāgaḥ nityakarmasu saṅga-phala-parityāgaḥ sāttvikaḥ sattva-nirvṛttaḥ mataḥ abhipretaḥ
ākāṃkṣā-ādi-mat-pada-jñāne eva saṃsarga-dhīḥ tad-abhāve tad-abhāvaḥ iti svatantra-anvaya-vyatirekayoḥ sattvāt
bhū-svāmī sva-prāsāda-pārśvam āgataḥ
tad darśana-utpanna-harṣa-prakarṣaḥ kiyantam cida-adhvānam atītya tasya vaṭa-vṛkṣasya sudūra-prasṛtāsu śākhāsu baddhān turaṅgamān adrākṣīt
pada-vṛtti-nirūpaṇāya śakti-vādaḥ nirmitaḥ svātantryeṇa
na ca tathā na-aṅgīkāre dampatyoḥ vyāsajya-vṛtti-kartṛtvam na syāt
tad-mate vedasya na-pauruṣeya tvena īśvara-kartṛka-tva-abhāvāt
yoga-vibhraṣṭa-vacanāt ca gṛhasthasya cet karmiṇaḥ yogaḥ vihitaḥ ṣaṣṭhe adhyāye
na caanaikāntikānām candana-cyavana-ādīnām katham vyañjakatvamiti vācyam
te dvandva-moha-nirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍha-vratāḥ
evañca dhātu-artha-niṣṭha-prakāratā-nirūpita-bhāvanā-niṣṭha-viśeṣyatā-śālin-bodha-janakam ākhyātamiti phalitam
kim anyat jagataḥ kāraṇam na kiñcit adṛṣṭam dharma-adharma-ādi kāraṇa-antaram vidyate jagataḥ kāmaḥ eva prāṇinām kāraṇam iti lokāyatika-dṛṣṭiḥ iyam
tatra anvita-pada-arthaḥ-vyutpatteḥ
vartamāna-kālaḥ dhātu-artha-vyāpāre
sarve nara-indrāḥ hi nara-indra-kanyām
tataḥ ardha-rātre etasya nāpitasya vadhūḥdūtī punaḥtām gopīmupetyaavadat tava viraha-anala-dagdhaḥ asau smara-śara-jarjaritaḥ mumūrṣuḥiva vartate mahat-anubhāvaḥ
pracuraṃ dhana-dhānyaṃ gṛhītvā dala-bala-sahitaḥ rājā tat-paṇḍita-āvāsaṃ prāptaḥ
anvaye vṛtti-svīkāre vṛtti-jñāna-janyāt upasthiteḥ kāraṇasyaabhāvāt tasya śābda-anubhava-viṣaya tā na saṃbhavati
madhu śleṣma-pitta-praśamanānāṃ
vālī bhrātṛ-dārā-abhimarśanena tulya-doṣayoḥ aham eva daṇḍitaḥ na sugrīvaḥ
gṛhaṃ gṛhasya sarvaṃ vastu-jātaṃ ca vikrīya yātrāyai dhanaṃ saṃcitya putra-dāra-mātṛ-sahitaḥ prasthānam akārṣīt
yaḥ sarvatra na-abhisnehaḥ tat tat prāpya śubha-na-śubham
ekena vṛddha-mantriṇā divya-parīkṣā-karaṇāya rājñe sva-sammati pradattā
ākṛṣṭe ca kīlake cūrṇita-aṇḍa-dvayaḥ pañcatvam gataḥ
tat-na-yogya tve naṣṭaḥ eva puruṣaḥ bhavati
su-dīrgha-vapuḥ ahaṃ siṃhaṃ hantuṃ śaknomi
evam eva ātman-na-ātma-viveka-jñānena buddhi-vṛttyā vidyayā na-satya-rūpayā eva parama-arthataḥ na-vikriyaḥ eva ātmā vidvān ucyate
abhidhāyāḥ jñātāyāḥ eva artha-pratipatti-anukūla tvāt vyaṅgyatva-abhimata-niṣṭha tvena pūrvam tad-jñāna-abhāvena tayā tathā bodha-saṃbhavāt
vikramasya tṛtīya-śataka-ante hūṇānām bhayaṅkaram itihāsa-prasiddham ākramaṇam samabhūt
pada-upasthāpitānām na-ekadhā eka-śābda-bodha īya-sāṃsargika-viṣayatāyām vidveṣiṇaḥ
vṛddhasya vacana-virāmasam anantaram eva sarve yuvāna paścāttāpa-vigalita-antakaraṇāḥ tasya caraṇayoḥ nipetu
te eva janāḥ go-svāminām na-iṣṭaṃ kartum asamarthāḥ santaḥ etāḥ viṣa-pra-dānena hatavantaḥ
tat-artha-āviṣkaraṇāya anekaiḥ vivṛta-pada-pada-artha-vākya-artha-nyāyam api atyanta-viruddha-aneka-artha tvena laukikaiḥ gṛhyamāṇam upalabhya aham vivekataḥ artha-nirdhāraṇa-artham saṃkṣepataḥ vivaraṇam kariṣyāmi
vidurasya na-upasthitau duryodhanaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrāt pāṇḍavān dyūta-krīḍa-artham āhvātum ājñāṃ prāptavān
tatra kaścit eva sahasreṣu deva-pūjā-ādi-paraḥ sattva-niṣṭhaḥ bhavati
yoga-phalam upasaṃhṛtya punaḥ anvārambheṇa yogasya kartavyatā ucyate niścaya-anirvedayoḥ yoga-sādhanatva-vidhāna-artham
caitraḥ taṇḍulam pacati ityatra taṇḍula-prātipadika-arthaḥ dvitīyā-arthe karmatve
idānīm avasaraṃ prāpya mantriṇā tasmai kūpa-khanana-kāryaṃ rājan-koṣāt pra-bhūtaṃ dhanaṃ ca dāpitam
etau ācārya-pitāmahau tām dṛṣṭvā lajjāyamānau paṭa-anta-antarhita-mukhau sthitau
na ca tasya prātipadikenaeva lābhāt prathamāyāḥ tad-arthe sādhutva-artham tad-artha-anuvādaka tāiti yuktam
tena ca daśamīm yāvatprapūjayet iti-ādau yāvat-śabda-yoge dvitīyā sidhyati
eka-chatra-chāyām pṛthivīm samājñāpayati dur-ātmā kaṃsaḥ
tasya bhaktyā prītā bhagavatī kālī dhṛta-sahasra-vikarāla-vadanā tatpurataḥ prakaṭitā abhavat
viśvajiti yajñe vitīrṇa-sarvasvaḥ akiñcanī-bhūtaḥ api raghuḥ taṃ yajña-śālāyām uṣitvā dvi-tri-dināni pratīkṣituṃ prārthayata
iti cintayata śrīkaṇṭhasya api hṛdayam atīva anu-tāpa-taptam abhūt
vastutaḥtu rūpiṇam vinā rūpasya dharmasya pratipattiḥnaastiitieva na hemanta-kāle tvac-indriyeṇa śaitya-āśraya-himam na-viṣaya-nī-kṛtya api śaitya-pratyakṣa-udayāt
puraskāra-prāpti-artham eva na
tasyāḥ tat phena-dhavalaṃ rūpaṃ jala-tuṣāra-sekaṃ dṛṣṭvā agastyaḥ prathamaṃ hata-buddhaḥ anantaraṃ śoka-ākulaḥ abhavat
bhāvanāyāḥ kṛteḥ caitra-niṣṭhāyāḥ maitra-niṣṭhāyāḥ ca bhinnatayā caitra-niṣṭhāyām pāka-anukūla-kṛtau caitra-anya-na-vṛtti tvasya na-bādhita tvāt
tasmāt raghu-mahat-rājana saha kuberaḥ api yuddhaṃ kartuṃ na iṣṭavān
anvaya-avabodha-janakasya pada-arthasya pada-artha-antara-apekṣaṇāt anvayasya pratiyogi-sa-apekṣa-tvāt
dvi-tra-varṣīyaḥ āsīt
ataḥ teṣu a-laukika-bālakeṣu sarve snihyanti sma
ekadā maharṣi-ramaṇaṃ parīkṣitum eva kecana girijā-gṛha-svāminaḥ pṛṣṭavantaḥ śrutam asti
jihma-vyāyāma-śayanāt ati-bhāra-adhva-maithunāt
tatra viṣṇuḥ gāḍha-nīla-varṇa-sahitaḥ san kṛṣṇaḥ iti nāmnā vilasati
hiṃsa-ātmakaḥ para-pīḍā-kara-svabhāvaḥ
nāgī iva yāsi pataga-indra-bhaya-abhibhūtā
na tu dhātu-artha-ghaṭita-paramparā-saṃbandhena bhāvanāyām
vastu-sthiti-abhi-jñaḥ rājā putreṇa saha saha-parivāra sādhu-darśanāya prasthita
mama sva-artha sya ahaṅkārasya ca kāraṇataḥ etat-sarvam pravṛttam iti sva-gatam vadan paścāttāpam anubhūtavān saḥ
vṛddhaḥ dvijaḥ niśi-cara-anu-caraḥ saḥ eṣaḥ
kārya-anvita-śakti-vādinaḥ mīmāṃsakāḥ kāryatā-smāraka-śakti-mat-liṅ-ādi-samabhivyāhāra-bhāve anvaya-bodham apalapanti
ayam kaḥ iti na jānāmi iti-ādau iti-śabdaḥ samabhivyāhṛta-vākya-pratipādya-jijñāsā-viṣaya-dharma-viśeṣa-viṣayaka-na-bhinna-jñāna-abhāva-vāhanam iti bodhaḥ bhavatiiti vastu-sthitiḥ
etam prastāvam śrutvā nitarām kruddhaḥ mahat-rājaḥ avadat yuvan-rājan-madhūlikayoḥ vivāhaḥ kadācid api bhavitum na arhati
rāmanāthasya putrān dṛṣṭvā sundarāḥ bālāḥ ete iti praśaṃsitavān saḥ kṣaṇa-kāla-anantaram sarvathā dus-ceṣṭā-parāḥ bālāḥ ete iti ninditavān
kutaḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt yadā punaḥ kārya-karaṇa-sukha-duḥkha-rūpeṇa hetu-phala-ātmanā pariṇatayā prakṛtyā bhogyayā puruṣasya tad-viparītasya bhoktṛtve na avidyā-rūpaḥ saṃyogaḥ syāt
devatā-taddhita-sthale āgneyam iti-ādau prakṛti-pratyaya-arthayoḥ abheda-anvayasya sarva-siddha tvāt
te sarve paraṃ muditāḥ abhavan avadan ca mitra-vara yadi nṛ-paḥ tava kṛpayā nityam evaṃ śani-kopa-dṛṣṭyā vīkṣitaḥ syāt
tadā rājā pṛṣṭavān kim abhavat sā avadat eṣā aparājitā nāma auṣadhiḥ asya jāta-karma-samaye bhagavatā mārīcena dattā
ghaṭa-pada-artha-eka-deśa-ghaṭatve nityatva-anvaya-tātparyeṇa nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti prayoga-vāraṇāya avaśyam svīkaraṇīyāyāḥ padārthaḥ pada-arthena anveti na tad-ekadeśena iti vyuptatteḥvirodhāteva siddham
taiḥ saha isrel-deśasya hībrū-bhāṣāyāḥ ca nava-utthāna-viṣaye svīyānāṃ svapnānāṃ vinimaye ca adhikaṃ kālam anayat
evam kriyā-pada-rahita-sthale niyamena asti-pada-adhyāhāra-vādibhiḥ api
na tu tat śraddhāvattva-ādau iti ekāntataḥ jñāna-labdhi-upāyaḥ
kārya-ālayāt āgataḥ āsīt śekharaḥ tasya haste cāya-caṣakaṃ dadatī apṛcchat śekhara yadi bhārata-darśana-aṭana-sthāne kañcit grāmaṃ gaccheva
ataeva śakti-grāhaka-kośeṣu apabhraṃśāḥ
tasmin brahma-agnau apare anye brahma-vidaḥ yajñam yajña-śabda-vācyaḥ ātmā
kārya-na-vyavahita-pūrva-vṛtti-sva-vyāpāra-anyatara-ka tvasya eva kāraṇatā-rūpa tvāt
ityādauiva nānā-artha-sthale api prakṛta-na-prakṛtayoḥ arthayoḥ śaktyāeva bodhe bādhaka-abhāvāt
nidāna-ākṛti-saṃsargāt śvayathuḥ syāt dvi-doṣa-jaḥ
tathā śyāma-aruṇa-varṇaḥ prakṛti-varṇaḥ vā
gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ ityatra gaṅgā-pada-śakya-arthasya pravāhasya vākya-artha-anvayaḥ naupapadyate
viṣam bhuṅkṣvaityatraapi eka-padasya dviṣat-anna-bhojane
yathā gahana-vana-madhye vicarataḥ kasyacit na-śaraṇasya andhasya karāt kopi yaṣṭikām āharet tathaiva jīvana-ādhāra-bhūtasya tasya putrasya viśleṣaḥ tām akhedayat
asti-bhavantī-paraḥ prathama-puruṣaḥ na-prayujyamānaḥ apiasti iti kātyāyana-smaraṇasya eva prathamā-anta-padasya kriyā-pada-sa-ākāṃkṣa tve pramāṇatvāt
mātrā-kāla-kriyā-bhūmi-deha-doṣa-guṇā-antaram
evam yoga-abhyāsa-balāt ekāgrībhūtam nivāta-pradīpa-kalpam sat
devadattasya gṛha-abhāva-jñānāt bahis-sattva-jñānam iva arthāpatti-pramāṇa-janyā śvetaḥaśvaḥ dhāvatiiti pratipattiḥ
darśana-sama-kālam eva bauddha-bhikṣuḥ provāca yadi rājñaḥ mastake nārebu-hīrakam sthāpyeta tarhi rājā nir-rogaḥ bhaviṣyati
go-dugdha-pānena sarveṣāṃ biḍālyaḥ sthūlāḥ puṣṭāṅgāḥ ca āsan kintu tenālīrāmasya biḍālī kṛśa-kāyāḥ durbalā ca āsīt
a-yathā-balam ārambhaḥ niṣadha-rājan-kumāraḥ yāvatnamāṃ pariṇayati tāvatahaṃ tametat citra-paṭa-stham eva sevamānā kālamativāhayāmi
tadā tatra sthale aśva-atirikta-dravyasya bhāva-niścaye
vyutpatti-vāde api yasya ca bhāvena bhāva-lakṣaṇam iti sūtra-artha-vicāre
tat-sandeśa-anuguṇaṃ samādhānaṃ yaḥ dadyāt saḥ eva nalaḥ iti jñātuṃ śakyate
svasya vyavahāra-jñāna-viṣaye viveka-viṣaye ca pūrṇaḥ viśvāsaḥ āsīt rājñaḥ
iti-ādinā kartṛ-ādi-vācaka-tā-bodhaka tvamiti samāna-ākāra-sūtrāṇām vibhanna-arthaka-tva-svīkāra-āpattiḥ
ete ca anumāna-dīdhiti-vyākhyāne api prasaṅgāt śābda-bodha-aupayikān vyutpatti-viśeṣān anvaya-bodhān ca sa-udāharaṇam varṇayanti
bauddha-artha-siddhau eva jñāna-sāmānye viṣayasya kāraṇatva-sambhavāt tad-sādhana-avasare siddhavat tādṛśa-kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-upanyāsasya asaṃgatatvāt
ṛju trikoṣāphalitaṃ kola-asthi-agra-pramāṇitam
nārī nava-amala-jala-udbhava-lagna-hastā
yaḥ tu parama-artha-darśī saḥ
hanta te kathayiṣyāmi divyā hi ātma-vi-bhūtayaḥ
gajapati-vaṃśa-rājāḥ ca sarvathā pratīkṣante sma
viśeṣyatā-saṃbandhena tad-pada-janya-bodha-viṣaya-tva-prakāraka-īśvara-icchā vattvam tad-pada-vācya tvam
niyatam saṃbandhamavalambyaeva śabdaḥ artha-viśeṣa-vyañjakaḥ iti vyakti-vādinā api vaktavyam
tenālīrāmaḥ nija-caula-koṣāt daśa-svarṇa-mudrāḥ niṣkāsya tam avadat yadi rājan-guroḥ gṛhe gupta-mantraṇāyāḥ tathyāni tvaṃ prakaṭayeḥ
carati pulineṣu haṃsī kāśā-aṃśuka-vāsinī susaṃhṛṣṭā
īśvara-prāpti-arthaṃ tapaḥ kurvantaḥ ṛṣayaḥ tatra nivasanti sma
yogya-satkāreṇa mṛdu-pravartana-ādibhiḥ tava bandhu-hṛdayāni toṣaya
sāttvikī sattva-nirvṛttā deva-pūjā-ādi-viṣayā
parantu ku-yuktyā yat kriyate tat vīrasya śobhā-karam na iti krodha-miśrita-svareṇa uccaiḥ vadan vṛkṣataḥ avataran adhaḥ patitavān
śaṅkarasya vara-prabhāveṇa jayadrathaḥ cakra-vyūha-praveśa-dvāre eva pāṇḍavān avaruṇaddhi sma
tatyathā paktim a-paktiṃ darśanam a-darśanaṃ mātra-amātra tvamūṣmaṇaḥ prakṛti-vikṛti-varṇau śauryaṃ bhayaṃ krodhaṃ harṣaṃ mohaṃ prasādamitievamādīni caaparāṇi dvandvāniiti
benyahūdasya kaṭhora-anuśāsana-kāraṇataḥ saḥ mātā-pitarau vihāya anyeṣāṃ darśanam api viralatayā eva prāpnoti sma
bahu-kāla-paryantaṃ cintanaṃ kṛtvā saḥ uktavān bhavatu ahaṃ bhavate bhojanarūpeṇa anyat kimapi dāsyāmi
kocīnasthitam bhāratīya-vāyusenā-pra-śikṣaṇa-kendram api garuḍa nāmnā alaṃkṛtam
tri-caraṇa-atikrānta-tri-lokaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ khalu atrabhavān
loka-vyavahāra-sāmānya-darśanena tu laukikaiḥ āropita-kartṛtve bhikṣā-aṭana-ādau karmaṇi kartā bhavati
bhārata-darśana-aṭana-sthāne kañcit grāmaṃ gatvā tatra sevā-karaṇaṃ samīcīnam amanyata
ataḥ vārtikam dṛṣṭvā iti-ādi-vacanasya naavasaraḥ
atha dūrāteva sādaram rājñā praveśitaḥ sa-aṣṭan-aṅga-pātam praṇipatyaupaviṣṭaḥ
āyātākārā vanya-pradeśā sarvataḥ adhikam ca grīṣme api sama-śīta-uṣṇatvam
evañca caitra-niṣṭha-kṛti-janya-vyāpāra-janya-rūpa-parāvṛtti-āśrayaḥ taṇḍulaḥ iti tad-vākya-artha-bodhaḥ
arjunasya praśna-na-upapatteḥ ca
tataḥ tādṛśa-bhojanasya na-kartavya tvam balavat-na-iṣṭa-anubandhin-tva-rūpam anuminoti iti anumāna-paramparayā śatru-gṛha-bhojana-nivṛtti-tātparyaka tvam
aṅga-aṅgi-bhāvam na-jñātvā katham sāmarthya-nirṇayaḥ
nārada-hṛdaye vivāha-icchāyāḥ abhāvāt hima-ālayaṃ gatvā niṣṭhayā aṣṭa-akṣarī-mantraṃ japati sma
tasyā aśru-bindavaḥ bhūmau patitvā muktā-phala-rūpe pariṇatā
śīla-saujanyābhyām ca asau grāma-dvija-striya sarvathā atikramate sma
sīmni praviṣṭamātra eva sa sarvam avagatavān yat mantrin-senā-pati-prabhṛtayaḥ rājan-koṣāt dhanam āhṛtya āhṛtya nijaṃ dhana-koṣaṃ samedhayanti
udghāṭya peṭikām niṣkāsitāni jana-dur-labhāni bahūni mauktika-ādīni
akarmaṇi ca kārya-karaṇa-vyāpāra-uparame karmavat ātmani adhyāropite
taru-tala-nivāsinī śṛgālī pratyahaṃ vṛkṣa-mūlaṃ khanati
tasmāt karmaṇi adhikṛtān prati eva eṣaḥ saṃnyāsa-tyāga-vikalpaḥ
nalagiriḥ-mantra-auṣadhi-niyama-saṃ-bhṛtaḥ
deha-ātmanoḥ tu jñeya-jñātroḥ eva itara-itara-adhyāsaḥ
tulasī-sasya-rūpeṇa bhū-lokam avatīrṇā
na teṣāṃ saṃpūrṇa-bheṣaja-upapādanāya samutthānaviśeṣaḥ naasti
sādhāraṇaḥ janaḥ sva-janma-dine sampanna-janāya kim adadāt
taila-dhārāvat saṃtataḥ na-vicchinna-pratyayaḥ dhyānam
na-saktam phala-āsaṅga-rahitam
namaḥ bhagavate trai-lokya-kāraṇāya nārāyaṇāya
deva-dūtaḥ āśīrvāda-karaṇa-cchalena śiśoḥ samīpaṃ prāpya anya-darśanaṃ vinā tasya kaṇṭhaṃ niṣpīḍya śvāsaṃ nirudhya śiśuṃ māritavān
yataḥ na tena ātmani sa-hṛdayatva-abhāva kadāpi anubhūta
amba paredyuḥ sāyaṃkāle asmākaṃ varga-śikṣikāyāḥ janma-dina-āghoṣaḥ asti
sambhrāntāḥ galita-uttarīya-vasanāḥ trāsa-ākula-vyāhṛtāḥ
sambhrāntaḥ manmathaḥ ca na-anya-gatikatayā tataḥ dhāvitavantau
caitreṇa svāpaḥ kriyate ityatra tu kṛñ-artha-nirūpitam eva kartṛtvam āśrayatva-rūpam tṛtīyayā bodhyate
yoga-saṃnyasta-karmāṇam parama-artha-darśana-lakṣaṇena yogena saṃnyastāni karmāṇi yena parama-artha-darśinā dharma-adharma-ākhyāni tam yoga-saṃnyasta-karmāṇam
bhūtānām prakṛtiḥ avidyā-lakṣaṇā na-vyakta-ākhyā
ata khalu sva-artha-mūlam sukham jīvet iti hi asmākam siddhānta
tataḥ vāda-niyama-anusāreṇa kahoḍaḥ bandipaṇḍitāya samarpitaḥ
tatvat saṃpūrṇa-bheṣaja-upalambhāt āturāḥ
ataḥ rukmiṇyā samarpita-tulasī-dalena śrīkṛṣṇaḥ santuṣṭaḥ abhavat
pada-tad-arthayoḥ saṃbandhasya sāmānyataḥ dhātu-arthasya
yat sva-surakṣā-artham svayam eva prayatitavyam
tataḥ tu te tasya vadhena dāruṇāḥ manasvinaḥ nairṛta-rājan-bāndhavāḥ
śakyatā-avacchedaka-rūpeṇa lakṣya-artha-bhāne vṛkṣatvenaeva tad-pada-pratipādyasya bodhāt
śaśaghnī madhuhā bhāsaḥ gṛdhra-ulūka-kuliṅgakāḥ
tasya gṛhaṃ svarṇa-rajata-ratnaiḥ dhana-dhānyaiḥ ca paripūrṇaṃ bhaviṣyati
sarve sva-anubhava-anusāram samādhānam pradattavanta
katipaya-varṣa-anantaram kāṣṭha-vikretā dhanika sañjāta
mantri-saha-caraiḥ tvaritam ekā yojanā niramīyata
evam ekā danta-kathā asti yat śrīkṛṣṇaḥ garbhavatī subhadrāṃ dvārakā-ānayana-samaye cakra-vyūhasya praveśaḥ kathaṃ karaṇīyaḥ iti avadat
vātāma-abhiṣuka-akṣoṭa-mukūlaka-nikocakāḥ
ataḥca tad-vāci-nañaḥ śakya-koṭau api pratiyogi-sambandhaḥ praviśatievaiti vācyam
anya-labhya tvāt asti-pada-prayoga-ānarthakyam itiucyate
arjunaḥ tu saṃnyāsa-tyāga-śabda-arthayoḥ eva viśeṣa-bubhutsuḥ uvāca
pitā ca mama varṣa-dvaya-anantaraṃ dvitīyaḥ vivāhaḥ kṛtaḥ
tat idāniṃ tapas-dvārā śrīharim eva prāsādayituṃ hima-giri-śikharaṃ vayaṃ prayāmaḥ
yadi śvaityam hreṣā-śabdaḥ khura-vikṣapa-śabdaḥ ca sparūpataḥ evaavasitāḥ
tataḥ praviśati gopa-jana-parivṛtaḥ dāmodaraḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ ca
cīra-ajina-jaṭā-dhārī rāmaḥ bhavatu tāpasaḥ
dvi-sahasra-varṣāṇām anantaraṃ nirmīyamāṇaṃ prathamaṃ hībrū-gṛhaṃ bhaviṣyati asmākam
snigdha-ślakṣṇa-tanu-tvak tāṃ ye ca kāṅkṣanti dehinaḥ
vayaṃ ca samantāt lokā-apavāda-pātraṃ bhavāmaḥ
katham ca tam saṃpātya sa svayam api saṃbhram na-vi-mūḍha samabhavat
imaṃ vṛttāntaṃ mahat-rāja-virāṭāya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ
na-prāpya māṃ nivartante mṛtyu-saṃsāra-vartmani
śīta-uṣṇa-varṣa-lakṣaṇāḥ punaḥ hemanta-grīṣma-varṣāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ
iti sandarbheṇa dhātu-artha-nirūpaṇasya prāthamye nimittam varṇayantaḥ vaiyākaraṇa-bhūṣaṇa-kārāḥ tiṅ-anta-śūnyam api vākakyamabhyupagacchanti
nañā lakṣaṇayā caitra-niṣṭha-abhāvaḥ bodhyate
pada-arthasya pada-artha-eka-deśena pada-janya-upasthiti-prakāreṇa anvayasya na-vyutpanna tvāt
grāmasya bālakā parasparam baddha-hastā mūkasya vivāha-upa-lakṣye nṛtya-ratāḥ vartante
sva-artha-parāyaṇā jagati kim kim na kurvanti
śrīkaṇṭha bhāmatyā praṇaya-vedanā-prahāreṇa vi-khaṇḍita-garvitaḥ lajjā-vilambita-ānana iva maunam tasthau
udara-pūraṃ ca bhojanaṃ kārayitvā sāmānya-śuṣka-roṭikāyāḥ api mahattvam abodhayat iti
uḍḍayana-abhyāsa-artham alpaḥ kāla-avadhiḥ apekṣyate
nirukta-vyavahāre karmatva-padam karman-saṃjñā-param iti prācīnāḥ vadanti
prathamā-ādi-sup-vibhaktīnām artha-vicāreṇa bhāṭṭarahasya-granthaḥ samāptim nītaḥ
tatra ca kāryatā-avacchedaka-koṭau viṣaya-viṣayaka tvam na niveśanīyam
varṇa-sphoṭa-ādīn aṣṭa-vidhān sphoṭān viśadīkṛtyaante na-khaṇḍa-vākya-jāti-sphoṭam brahma-rūpa iṇamuktvā
chātrā paṭhana-patha-cyutā vipatham urīcakru
sarva-śāstra-artha-vettā vāda-marma-jñaḥ ca bhūtvā taṃ bandi-paṇḍitaṃ vāde jeṣyāmi
teṣām ca madhye kaścana yuvā suṣamayā vijita-śambara-ari
atra vākya-artha-padam tad-avagama-param tad-hetu-tva-padam ca pada-artha-hetuka-tva-param bodhyam
tena tava ātma-rūpa-prāptiḥ bhavati
kiñcit kālaṃ yāvat vane itaḥ tataḥ aṭan rākṣasa-āvāsa-sthānaṃ prāptavān
adhika-adhikam dhanam adhigantum ucita-na-ucitāni sādhanāni āśrayate
śara-vara-parivītam śānta-vegam śarīram
āśrayaḥca sva-vṛtti-āśrayatva-nirūpaka-tva-saṃbandhena viklṛpti-rūpa-phale
gṛha-prāpti-paryantaṃ sakṛt api parivṛtya na dṛṣṭaṃ tena
śrī śrī janaka-mahat-rāja parāk iti ghoṣaṇā śrutā
tad-pāda-viyuktaṃ pāda-trāṇam eva vilokayan pramattaḥ iva rājan-putraḥ sarva-kālam abhiramate
nalaḥ ātmagatam etat antaḥpura-udyānam sakhīnāṃ sa-rasa-sambhāṣaṇaiḥ sa-rasa-sambhāṣaṇaiḥ iva bhāti
tasya nir-dhana tvam sva-artha-anvayi-arthaka-vibhakti-na-prakṛti tvam
alakṣayat cate prāṇa-apāna-gatī ete ruddhvā nirudhya prāṇāyāma-parāyaṇāḥ prāṇāyāma-tatparāḥ
gupta-cara-vibhāgena yat prati-vedanaṃ prastutaṃ tat udvega-janakam āsīt
na-dambhitvam sva-dharma-prakaṭīkaraṇam dambhitvam
prativeśi-vasati-vāsinaḥ etādṛśeṣu avasareṣu mārga-avarodhaṃ kṛtvā svakīyaṃ roṣaṃ prakaṭayanti sma
katipaya-dina-anantaram yuvakaḥ ayam tasmin eva nagare gataḥ śramikaḥ bhūtvā catvare samupaviṣṭaḥ
tathāpi yatra bodhya-pramā-pūrvam bodhya-upasthitiḥ apekṣyate tatraeva bodhya-bodhaka-saṃbandha-jñānam kāraṇam
rājā prasannena cetasā provāca tat-kṛte ṣaṣṭi-grāma-dāna-patram likhāmi
na kāya-kleśa-nimittam duḥkham sāṃkhyāḥ ātmani paśyanti
māna-apamānayoḥ tulyaḥ tulyaḥ mitra-ari-pakṣayoḥ
api ca akṣairmā dīvyaḥ ityādikam akṣa-krīḍāṃ tad-na-iṣṭa-phalaṃ ca dṛṣṭvaiva proktam
tatkathaṃ guru-dakṣiṇā-samānaṃ bhavitum arhati iti
vayam tu kevalam priyadarśanā lalanā grahīṣyāma pāka-sainya-adhikārī sa-aṭṭahāsam udaghoṣayat
jharajhara-nipatat-jala-dhārā
adhyātman-jñāna-nityatvam ātman-ādi-viṣayam jñānam adhyātman-jñānam
śṛṅga-agra-koṭi-kiraṇaiḥ kham iva ālikhan ca
tat śāstram yathā-darśita-artham buddhvā buddhimān syāt bhavet na anyathā kṛta-kṛtyaḥ ca bhārata kṛtam kṛtyam kartavyam yena saḥ kṛta-kṛtyaḥ
yathā saṅkalpitam ratha-aśva-gajam ratna-ādikam vā rājñā
sarva-saṅkalpa-saṃnyāsī sarvān saṃkalpān iha amutra-artha-kāma-hetūn saṃnyasitum śīlam asya iti sarva-saṅkalpa-saṃnyāsī
saṃpratipattiḥ kāla-jñāna-prayojanānām
taruṇa-jana-sahāyaḥ cintyatām veśa-vāsaḥ
abhyāsa-yoga-yuktena mayi citta-samarpaṇa-viṣaya-bhūte kasmin tulya-pratyayā-vṛtti-lakṣaṇaḥ vilakṣaṇa-pratyaya-na-antaritaḥ abhyāsaḥ saḥ ca abhyāsaḥ yogaḥ tena yuktam tatra eva vyāpṛtam yoginaḥ cetaḥ tena
devā api asya rūpasya nityaṃ-darśana-ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ
śubhā-śubha-parijñāne
om-tat-śabdayoḥ viniyogaḥ uktaḥ atha idānīm sat-śabdasya viniyogaḥ kathyate
niśita-vimala-khaḍgāḥ krodha-visphārita-akṣāḥ
durdina-vinaṣṭa-jyotsnā rātriḥ vartate nimīlitā-ākārā
tasya sa-guṇa-kārasya parama-īśvarasya kula-guruḥ ahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi iti bhāgyam
prāṅgaṇa-praveśa-samanantaraṃ jhaṭiti unnataṃ prākāra-dvāraṃ pidhāya argalaṃ yojitavān benyahūdaḥ
para-samaveta-kriyā-janya-phala-śālin-tva-sama-niyatam na-khaṇḍam karmatvam manyante
śyāmasya viṣaye tasya mātā-pitarau cikitsā-ālaya-karma-cārī kiṃ kathitavān
athavā kumāra-rakṣaṇa-artham na-ṛtam api satyam paśyāmi
diti-suta-nāśa-kare rathe vibhāti
āhārya-parokṣa-na-prasiddheḥ iti vācyam
pūrvaṃ mūla-phala-jñāna-hetoḥ uktaṃ yatauṣadham
tatra ca na kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-kalpanā-gauravam
kāvya-hetu-vākya-artha-jñānam kaveḥ padāni janayantiiti na yujyate
sthālī-pulāka-nyāyena pāṇinīya-itara-anuśāsana-uddhāraḥ pradarśyate
tad-apekṣayā sthūla-bahu-viṣayam pratyakṣam
jala-da-samaya-ghoṣaṇā-āḍambara-na-eka-rūpa-kriyā-jṛmbhakāḥ vajrabhṛt-gṛṣṭayaḥ
sat sat eva asat asat eva iti niścaya-na-upapatteḥ
anantara-varṣe viśva-mahat-yuddhaṃ samāptiṃ gatam
mūtrāṇāṃ triphalāyāḥca sneha-vyāpatti-bheṣajam
gaṇapati-pūjana-ādi mārkaṇḍeya-pūjanam yāvat sampādita sarvaḥ api śāstra-vidhi
na ca evam pada-viśeṣasya eva anvaya-buddhi-hetu tve
taṃ vidyāt duḥkha-saṃyoga-viyogaṃ yoga-sañjñitam
yataḥ na lakṣaṇā-nāstitvaḍh-vādinaḥ śakya-saṃbandham eva niṣedhanti
yuddhe vaiśravaṇa-ālaye acala-śilā-vega-pratisphālinā
strī-madya-nityāḥ grīṣme ca bṛṃhaṇīyāḥ narāḥ smṛtāḥ
grāmaḥ na-pradhāna-karman
itaḥ tri-yojana-parimite dūre ati-prācīnaḥ kaścana śiva-ālayaḥ asti
tebhyaḥ daśavārṣikaḥ kārā-vāsa-daṇḍaḥ ādiṣṭaḥ bhū-patinā
na kevalam sva-dharma-kīrti-parityāgaḥ
ayaṃ tuatra viśeṣaḥ śīta-rūkṣa-laghu-viśada-śrama-upavāsa-atikarśana-kṣapaṇa ādibhiḥvāyuḥ prakupitaḥ tvak-māṃsa-śoṇita ādīniabhibhūya śophaṃ janayati
dīna-ārta-vacasā kopi bhagavantaṃ stavīta cet
saṃhitā-brāhmaṇa-āraṇyakeṣu dvayoḥ api viśālaṃ jñānaṃ praśnātītam iti rājā sabhā-sadaḥ ca samyag jñātavantaḥ
catvāraḥ divasāḥ vyatiyānti ṣaṭ-divasa-artham masūrī-nagaram asmābhiḥ gantavyam asti
bhavādṛśai sat-śiṣyaiḥ mama abhinandana-grantha-nirmāṇāya tat-mudraṇāya tat-prakāśanāya ca ya saṅkalpa dhāritaḥ tena na ayam mama abhinandanam api tu sura-sarasvatyā iti vicārya momudyate me mana
katipaya-māsa-anantaram cikitsā-ālaye deveśa svāsthya-lābham avāpya kārāgāre svakīyam hṛdaya-a-bhinnam mitram śerasiṃham sākṣātkartum na-sakṛt agamat
yat eṣaḥ vyādhiḥ khādyeṣu apamiśraṇa-sama-udbhavaḥ pratīyate
samam paśyan upalabhamānaḥ hi yasmāt sarvatra sarva-bhūteṣu samavasthitam tulyatayā avasthitam īśvaram atīta-anantara-śloka-ukta-lakṣaṇam ityarthaḥ
prasannena mahat-rājena tenālīrāmāya svarṇa-mudrā-pūritaṃ sthālakaṃ pradattam rājyasya vidūṣaka-pade ca tasya niyuktiḥ vihitā
śītam pravṛddham āvām ca sva-pānthin-āvāsād gavyūti-paryantam krośa-dvayam samāgatau
kartṛtva-antara-viśeṣaṇa-tā-āpannāyām ca kriyāyām kartṛtva-saṃbandhena anvayaḥ nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ bhavati
nanu gaṅgā-pade tīra-bodhaka-tva-sattvāt tīra-vācaka-tva-āpattyā gaṅgā-padasya tīre lakṣaṇāyāḥ uccheda-prasaṅgaḥ cet na
viddha-kṣarat-kṣata-ja-rañjita-sarva-gātram
rājan-mātā he damayanti asmin divase puṇyāhavācana-samaye veda-vit-samāje kaḥapi sudevaḥ nāma brāhmaṇaḥ tvāṃ draṣṭum icchati dūrataḥ dṛṣṭvā saḥ eṣaḥ bhūsuraḥ itaḥ eva āgacchati
na vā tat-sambhāvanā-avasaraḥ ca
śuṣka-sphig-udara-grīvaḥ dhamanī-jāla-santataḥ
kasmiṃścit yāyage dvija-kule vinaya-pratirūpasya nitānta-udāra-caritrasya sarvadeva-abhidhasya kanyātvena labdha-janiḥ vibhāvinī mahatā saṃrambheṇa su-pālitā sam-upalālitā ca nikhilaiḥ kula-janai
kiñca anyat na-vihitam na-pratiṣiddham ca karma tad-kāla-phalam
cintādīnāḥ śoka-saṃdagdha-dehāḥ vikrośantaṃ pārthivaṃ garhayanti
ekadā nibhṛtam śṛgālaḥ brūtesakhe asmin vana-eka-deśe sasya-pūrṇa-kṣetram asti
param tava manaḥ tu nir-vyāja-sahānubhūtinā ā-pūritam āsīt
vastutaḥ lakṣaṇāyāḥ aṅgīkāreapi na kārya-kāraṇa-bhāva-antara-kalpanā-gauravam
pākaḥca ākhyāta-artha-kṛti-anvayī
ataḥ eva avagata-nirukta-vākya-arthaḥ puruṣaḥ
taṃ dhāvantaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve brāhmaṇāḥ rājan-guruḥ ca kara-dhṛta-su-tapta-śaṃkha-lauha-cakrāḥ tam anvadhāvan
iti śaṅkā-nirāsāya lakṣaṇā-nirūpaka-grantha-avatāraḥ caetamarthamupodbalayati
kim punaḥ atra mīmāṃsā-phalam nanu etat eva eṣām anyatamasya parama-niḥśreyasa-sādhanatva-avadhāraṇam
abheda-anvaya-bodhe samāna-vibhaktika tvasya tantratvāt
api tu tad-prakāraka-anyadīya-jñāna-viṣaya-tva-avagāhī iti na na-upapadyamāna-tva-jñānena pratibadhyate
kiṃtu deva yadiapi mahāmantriṇā gṛdhreṇa saṃdhānamupanyastam tathāapi tena rājñā saṃprati bhūta-jaya-darpāt na mantavyam
tadīyam vaibhavam dāsa-vargam ca vilokya brahmacāriṇā nirmala-ānandena tat-sukha-tulanayā sva-sukha-naiyūnyam iva pratītam hanūmat-mandira-bhaktāḥ tat-ājñām tathā na paripālayanti yathā mahat-dhanikasya asya sevakā
śrāntatām vismṛtya kauśikī-nadyāḥ-tīre kathām śrṛṇotu iti
kevalaṃ mama-bhartā-anveṣaṇe lagnaiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥeva sambhāṣe
nānā-nadī-nada-gatena tava prasādāt
rātrim api yuga-sahasra-antām ahan-parimāṇām eva
tadā lakṣā-dhika-rasikaiḥ sa-aśru-nayanaiḥ tasmai śraddhā-añjaliḥ arpitaḥ
kintu jagat-kartā na-parimita-śaktimān
sarveṣāmeva bhāvānāṃ bhāva-abhāvau naantareṇa yoga-ayoga-atiyoga-mithyāyogān samupalabhyete
yaḥ śābda-bodha-vicāra-virahitaḥ
mahat-vākya-artha-bodhaḥ viśiṣṭa-vaiśiṣṭya-avagāhi iva jāyate
somaḥca a-vyāhata-balaḥ śiśirābhiḥ bhābhiḥāpūrayaṃ jagat āpyāyayati śaśvat
vadhvā upari ca varadṛṣṭi vaidika-saṃskāra-anumatā patati
sa tu śānta-mukha-mudra āgatya ṛṣe vāma-bhāge upaviṣṭa ṛṣiḥ ca sva-hastam tat-śirasi nidhāya sva-prema prākaṭayat
he raṃga kalāśālāyām vidyā-vyāsaṃge vatsara-traya-ātma kaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇa-kālaḥ iva atītaḥ
kṣaṇa-kālam vicintya saḥ sabhāsadaḥ paśyan dṛḍha-svareṇa avadat etam aham bhraṣṭa-ācāra-nir-mūlana-vibhāgasya mukhyam kṛtavān asmi iti
ahaṃ cintayāmi yat adya asmākaṃ mahatī āvaśyakatā asti ādhunikasya hībrū-śabda-koṣasya
damayantī svamin aham adhunā eva tvāṃ dik-pālaka-sākṣitvena pariṇayāmi iti mama abhilāṣaḥ
mayā sarvatra rājakīya-śikṣā-vibhāgeṣu lokasevā-āyogasya vijñaptīnām uttare
hṛt-kaṇṭha-indriya-saṃśuddhiḥ laghutvaṃ śirasaḥ śamaḥ
kaveḥ kāvya-karaṇa-prayojakam saṃsarga-jñānam katham bhavetśabdasyaabhāvāt
tena hi ucyatām ikṣvāku-kula-nyaṅgabhūtaḥ bharataḥ darśanamabhilaṣatiiti
na ca pratyayānām prakṛti-artha-upasthāpita-artha-anvita-sva-artha-vyutpattiḥ api svīkriyate iti
tasyāḥ na-upama-saundaryeṇa saḥ ākṛṣṭaḥ
hanu-manyā-grāhaḥ kaṇḍūḥ krimayaḥ pāṇḍutā mukhe
tasyāḥ aśrūṇi vastra-vayana-yantre nyapatan
prakāratā-sambandhena nañ-artha-viśeṣyaka-śābda-bodham prati dhātu-janya-bhāvanā-upasthiteḥ viśeṣyatā-saṃbandhena hetutvāt
katipaya-māsa-anantaraṃ saḥ eva mahat-ātmanaḥ rājñā punarapi bhagavat-carcāyai āhūtaḥ
yayā ca īśvara-śaktyā bhakta-anugraha-ādi-prayojanāya brahma pratiṣṭhate pravartate
sva-icchayā udaka-ādi-āhāraḥ anubhūyatām
tulyatayā eka-pada-upasthāpya-anvayi tāyāḥ eva dvandva-sādhutā-prayojaka-tva-upagamāt
sṛṣṭeḥ mahimānaṃ dṛṣṭvā vismaya-ānanda-bharitaḥ aṣṭāvakraḥ indra-ādīn devān dhyāyan prayāti sma
yat aham parājitaḥ bhaviṣyāmi tarhi bhavān mat-gṛha-stham śreṣṭham vastu netum śaknoti
atha idānīm parābhaviṣyataḥ sarva-na-artha-mūlam idam ucyate
caturthe dine bhū-svāmī nidrā-abhibhūtaḥ san pra-gāḍha-nidrāyām ni-magnaḥ
parantu ghaṭatva-niṣṭha-turīya-viṣayatā-śālin-śābdam prati ghaṭa-padasya kāraṇatva-aṅgīkāre
tatra buddhimatā mānasa-vyādhi-parītena api satā buddhyā hita-a-hitam avekṣyaavekṣya dharma-artha-kāmānām a-hitānām an-upasevane hitānāṃ caupasevane prayatitavyaṃ
na ca prayojyatvam janyatva-rūpam janya-janya-tva-rūpam vā na saṃbhavatiitiuktamiti vācyam
kaḥ punaḥ ayam kṣetra-kṣetrajñayoḥ saṃyogaḥ abhipretaḥ na tāvat rajjvā iva ghaṭasya avayava-saṃśleṣa-dvārakaḥ saṃbandha-viśeṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ kṣetreṇa kṣetrajñasya saṃbhavati
ananta-samāsa-padānām na-prāmāṇika-ananta-śakti-kalpane gauravāt
yena buddhi-yogena samyak-darśana-lakṣaṇena mām parameśvaram ātman-bhūtam ātmatvena upayānti pratipadyante
sacivaḥ vā yasya sattā-ātaṃka-krāntaḥ kaścana yuvā mām udboḍhum ākṛṣṭa syāt
tava prācīna-yahūdya-sāmrājyasya sīmānaḥ iti eṣaḥ lekhaḥ nitarāṃ vivādāspadaṃ bhavati
vaiyākaraṇaiḥ ākhyata-artha-ekatva-anvitasya tad-arthasya kartuḥ dhātu-arthe viśeṣaṇatayā anvayāt eka-kartṛkaḥ pākaḥ iti bodhaḥ iṣyate
na hi vaiśeṣikaiḥ kulāla-daṇḍa-cakra-ādi-vyāpārāt prāk ghaṭa-ādīnām astitvam iṣyate
kim tarhi avikriyasya eva dvitīyā-tṛtīyā-avasthā-prāptiḥ ātmanaḥ dṛṣṭā
vāyoḥ na-uṣṇa-na-śīta-sparśatām pratipādayataḥ tārkikān parihasan iva jvalat aṅgāra-saṅkāśa-tāpa uṣṇa vāyuḥ vātum ārebhe
māsa-dvaya-anantaram deveśa vibhāvinī-pariṇayam api cakāra
kṣetrajña-īśvara-ekatva-viṣayam jñānam mokṣa-sādhanam yat jñātvā amṛtam aśnute iti uktam
kathaya janaka-mahat-rājam
śrīpālaḥ mandirasya purataḥ eva sthitvā prārthanām kṛtavān he rāma śrūyate yat pitṛ-vākya-pari-pālanāya bhavatā rājyam tyaktvā araṇyam prati gatam iti
hanta tarhi ātmani kriyā-kāraka-phala-ātmantāyāḥ svataḥ abhāve
paryavasyat-śābda-bodha-avidūra-prāk-kṣaṇa-sthite
pṛcchāmi tvām dharma-sammūḍha-cetāḥ
ekasmin divase akasmāt harijanānām kūpe prastara-patana-prārabdham abhūt
te tam grāma-adhipam gālikā-pradāna-purassaram nyabadhnan proktavantaḥ ca vayam tvām kājī-nyāyālayam nītvā daṇḍam dāpayiṣyāmaḥ
nibiḍa-gulma-āvṛtām mām draṣṭum na prabhavet uṣa iti pratītā vartmana madhye tam upaviśantam dadarśa viśrabdham ca sthitavatī sā
tathā śabdaḥapi tad-tad-pratiyogi-bodhana-kārya-bhede hetuḥ
sva-rājya-sthāpanasya pratijñā
yā abhīṣṭa-phala-dāyinī
nidhyāyantīṣu senāsu sam-utpanna-śaṅghā-piṇḍite tasmin yūthe asya an-arthasya utpādakaḥ kaścit padātiḥ bhartāramevaupasthitaḥ
devānām rudra-āditya-ādīnām vāsavaḥ indraḥ asmi
api punaḥ api na-hṛta-patnī kasya me viphalam jīvanam saphalam syāt iti evam ādīn nānā-vidhān vikalpān vikalpayan sa drutataram tatra śoṇita-sikta-bhū-tale sthale yayau
vaiśvānaraḥ san prāṇinām prāṇavatām deham āśritaḥ praviṣṭaḥ prāṇa-apāna-samāyuktaḥ prāṇa-apānābhyām samāyuktaḥ saṃyuktaḥ pacāmi paktim karomi annam aśanam catur-vidham catur-prakāram bhojyam bhakṣyam coṣyam lehyam ca
sva-abhyupagama-virodhaḥ ca nityam niṣphalam karma iti abhyupagamya mokṣa-phalāya iti bruvataḥ
yadyapi gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti-ādau tīre gaṅgā-pada-śakya-saṃbandha-jñānam apekṣyate
gacchatā kālena ayameva śikṣaṇa-vidhiḥ bhāṣā-śikṣaṇa-vidhiṣu atyantaṃ śīghra-phala-dāyaka-vidhitvena samagre api jagati aṅgīkṛtaḥ abhavat
mṛgaiḥtulyāḥ vyāghrāḥ vadha-nibhṛta-siṃhāḥ ca girayaḥ
chātrāvāsasya pramukha-praveśa-dvāri dṛṣṭaḥ tena
padānām artha-antara-anvita-sva-arthe śaktiḥ
nalaḥ rājan-antaḥpura-vāsinau āvāṃ na prakṛti-mādhuryaṃ jānīvaḥ
evaṃ rasa-malau sva-pramāṇa-avasthitau āśrayasya sama-dhātoḥ dhātu-sāmyam anuvartayataḥ
atra ca ātman-īśvara-bhedam āśritya viśvarūpe īśvare cetas-samādhāna-lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ uktaḥ
sopi durdaiva-nihata-buddhi-vaibhavaḥ mārīcaṃ sahāyakaṃ vidhāya sītāṃ harttuṃ manaḥ cakre
dṛṣṭā ca kāmya-agnihotra-ādau kāma-upamardena kāmya-agnihotra-ādi-hāniḥ
ubhe api mātu nir-dhana tayā kanyā-vinimaya-kalpe na-yogya-pāṇi-patite na-kāle eva divam gate
bhīmasya kopa-śikhinā yudhi pārtha-pattri-caṇḍa-anilaiḥ ca kuru-vaṃśa-vanam vi-naṣṭam
tasmāt pūrvaṃ uttānapādasya eva icchā-anusāreṇa himasumāra-mahat-rājasya kanyā brāhmī iti api ca vāyukanyā ilā iti dve dhruvaḥ vṛṇītavān āsīt
pada-janya-pada-artha-jñāna-kāle hi smarāmiitievaanuvyavasāyaḥ jāyate na tu śābdayāmiiti
tadā tasya purataḥ nir-kapaṭā dhī-vara-kanyā āgatya sthitā
saḥ tān bhartsayan iva jagāda svayam na-nyāya-karaṇe yadi rājñām api pravṛttiḥ tadā prajānām tu kathā eva kā bhavanta tasyā saundaryeṇa mugdhā kāma-śara-pīḍitā kartavya-na-kartavyadhi-jñāna-śūnyā saṃjātā iti pratīyate
na teṣu bhogeṣu ramate budhaḥ vivekī avagata-paramārtha-tattvaḥ
nanu ca karman-yogaḥ api ātman-svarūpa-nirūpaṇa-pradeśeṣu tatra tatra pratipādyate eva
pañca gulmāḥ iti vāta-pitta-kapha-sannipāta-śoṇita-jāḥ
pada-artha-upasthiteḥ ca vividha-ānupūrvī-sādhāraṇa-śabda-janya-pada-artha-upasthiti tvenaekāeva kāraṇatāiti lāghavam
jaghanyaguṇa-vṛttiḥ-sthā adhaḥ gacchanti tāmasāḥ
tasya rāga-ālāpana-samaye devaśarmā tanmayaḥ āsīt
tādṛśa-bodha-nirvāhāya tatra prathamā-anta-padam adhyāhriyate iti vācyam
arthasya ca śābda-bodha-viṣaya tvamastievaiti kva tādātmya-ādhyāsaḥ
vāta-uddhūta-uttarīyaḥ mukuṭa-maṇi-gaṇaiḥ tārakāḥ sampramṛdnan
dahati tvacamutthāne tṛṣṇā-moha-jvara-pradā
tathā ca pade sva-artha-abhidhāna-śaktiḥ
asmat-aṃśa-sambhūtasya sudāmnaḥ aṃśena yuktaḥ eva saḥ
sapta visarpāḥ iti vāta-pitta-kapha-agni-kardamaka-granthi-sannipāta-ākhyāḥ
na na-kṛtena iha loke kaścana kaścit api pratyavāya-prāpti-rūpaḥ ātman-hāni-lakṣaṇaḥ vā na eva asti
sa-vega-dhāvanāt tasya vadanaṃ vivṛtam āsīt pramāṇa-adhika-śvāsa-grahaṇāt saḥ kiñcit vaktum api na apārayat
kintu aham atra tvat-āgamanāt pūrvam nāṅgaka-phala-bhakṣaṇam ārabdhavān eva abhūvam
na viparīta-ādi-grahaṇam tat nimittam vā taimirikatva-ādi-doṣaḥ grahītuḥ
mantra-āyurveda-prāmāṇya tvāt āpta-prāmāṇya tvāt vedasya prāmāṇyam iti-ādikam upadideśa
tasya niṣkriya-ātman-darśana-saṃpannatvāt
veda-vedāṅga-tattva-jñaḥ
citra-go-svāmī ca go-padasya arthaḥ na vṛttyā prakṛti-arthaḥ iti tena dvitīyā-artha-anvaya-na-upapattiḥ
sarva-karma-phala-tyāgam sarveṣām karmaṇām phala-saṃnyāsam sarva-karma-phala-tyāgam tataḥ na-antaram kuru yata-ātmavān saṃyata-cittaḥ san ityarthaḥ
yābhyām prakṛtibhyām īśvaraḥ jagat-utpatti-sthiti-pralaya-hetuḥ
karkaśa-jaṭila-antakaraṇā
sarvatas-pāṇi-pādam tat jñeyam
jñātvā śāstra-vidhāna-uktam karma kartum iha arhasi
āhārā rājasasya iṣṭā duḥkha-śoka-āmaya-pradāḥ
tasya caabhedena śyāma-pada-artha-eka-deśa-śyāma-rūpe anvayaḥ ghana-śabdasya lakṣakatve tasya upamāna-bodhaka-tva-abhāvena upamānāni sāmānya-vacanaiḥ pā
tataḥ prati-āgata-prāṇam idānīṃ bhartāraṃ prekṣyaanena mama bhrātā hataḥanena mama pitā anena mama sutaḥ anena mama vayasyaḥ iti anyathā bhartuḥ parākramaṃ varṇayantaḥ sarvataḥabhidrutāḥte pāpāḥ
ataḥ eva dhātu-artha-mukhya-viśeṣya-kaḥ bodhaḥ jāyate
tad-anubhāvaka tve smaraṇa-janaka-tva-kalpanā-vaiyarthyāt
prasīdantu bali-śambara-mahat-kālāḥ
āsīt sa prati-śodha-vahni
na tathā pada-vākya-grantheṣu upalabhyate
vipra-visarjana-anantaram eva gṛha-sadasyaiḥ bhoktavyam
tatra gatvā sakala-vṛttāntaḥ ṭiṭṭibhena bhagavataḥ garuḍasya purataḥ niveditaḥ deva samudreṇaaham sva-gṛha-avasthitaḥ vināaparādhenaeva nigṛhītaḥ
sa-amarṣa-kṛṣṇa-dhṛta-raśmi-guṇa-pratodaḥ
rākeśena tasmin samaye sva-jīvana-vṛttānta-kathane yaḥ rasaḥ nikṣipta mama ca antare tam imam śrāvam śrāvam yādṛśī tanmayatā uditā sarvam idam anubhava-sākṣi kam eva
brahma ca tat agniḥ ca saḥ homa-adhikaraṇatva-vivakṣayā brahma-agniḥ
avakāśasya samaya gārgī-bhāratī-vijjikā-sadṛśyaḥ śubha-karmaṇi eva niyukta syāt iti uddeśyam ādāya tayā ema
parantu sarvathā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ antimaḥ vyāsa-mahat-ṛṣiḥ
ataḥ tad-dharma-prakāreṇa tad-viṣayaka-śābda-bodhe vṛtti-jñāna-janya-tad-dharma-avacchinna-tad-viṣayaka-upasthitiḥ hetuḥiti svīkaraṇīyam
na duḥkha-śīla-ācāra-upacāraḥ
sva-dharma-ākhyeṣu karmasu vartamānasya yā siddhi-na-siddhyoḥ samatva-buddhiḥ īśvara-arpita-cetaḥ tayā tat kauśalam kuśala-bhāvaḥ
na prathamā-anta-arthasya iti cet
grāmya-ānūpa-audaka-piśitāni ca madhu-tila-guḍa-payaḥ-māṣa-mūlaka-bisaiḥ virūḍha-dhānyaiḥ vā naekadhyamadyāt
su-dur-darśam suṣṭhu duḥkhena darśanam asya iti su-dur-darśam
koṣa-nirmāṇa-kāryam eva karotu
ādau kāraka-vibhakti-artha-nirṇayaḥ tataḥ kāraka-itara-vibhakti-artha-nirṇayaḥ iti kramaḥ samavalambitaḥ
miṣṭa-anna-sahitena bhojanena drākṣā-rasa-pānena ca pariṇaya-bhoja-utsavaḥ api samāptiṃ gataḥ
pārthaḥ kariṣyati tat ugra-dhanuḥ-sahāyaḥ
api tu pratyakṣamapi śabda-viṣayakam iti śabda-rahita-vikalpakam naastiityatra
śīta-uṣṇa-sukha-duḥkheṣu samaḥ
pāṇi-kara-hasta-śabdāḥ trayaḥ api eka-artha-bodhakāḥ
vandhyā-putra-ādīnām na-darśanāt
yama-niyama-ādi-sahitatvena ca dur-anuṣṭheyāt
tatra vanāni phala-puṣpa-bharitāni dṛṣṭāni
deva-devarṣi-siddha-vimala-cāritrāṃ tatrabhavatīṃ sītāmādāya ṛkṣa-rākṣasa-vānara-mukhyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ saṃprāptaḥtatrabhavān śarad-vimala-gagana-candra-abhirāmaḥ rāmaḥ
dīpa-nirvāṇa-gandham ca suhad-vākyam arundhatīm
bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān aham upādhi-kṛta-vistara-bhedaḥ
ayam tu asmad-karma-kṛt mām eva paramām gatim pratipadyate iti asmad-paramaḥ
tad-anantaram ca śiṣṭa-ācāra-anusāram
iti vividha-vicāraṇa-vyagra-mānasa śrīkaṇṭhaḥ eka-pade eva samāgacchantam kṛṣaka-samudāyam vīkṣya tata utthāya gṛham prati prasthita
krūratama śerasiṃha parama-ugra-vāda mitrasya sam-akṣam śiśu-sadṛśam rudan ārakṣibhiḥ nigṛhīta
ataḥ śava-anta-gataḥ vetālaḥ tataḥ na-dṛśyaḥ bhūtvā punaḥ vṛkṣasya śākhām avalambitavān
lākṣaṇika-kamala-padena api kamalatvenaeva vyakti-viśeṣa-bodha-upagame uddeśyatā-avacchedaka-vidheyatā-avacchedakayoḥ bheda-abhāvāt
tām-ākhyātukāma satvaram-āgataḥ-aham
evaṃ pratīyate yat tvāṃ prati īrṣya-anala-dagdhaḥ asau sat-mārgāt calitaḥ jātaḥ
nirukta-jñāna-ghaṭitā ca nirukta-pratyakṣa-sāmagrī
samprati na āsīt tasyā na-marṣa-leśaḥ api budhanīm prati
nānā-śastra-praharaṇāḥ sarve yuddha-viśāradāḥ
kintu puruṣāṇām kṛtyam kaiḥ vacobhiḥ vācyam bhavet rūpa-lubdhāḥ te bahiḥ āḍambara-anurāgiṇa kṣaṇa-bhaṅgura-cākacikyasya abhilāṣiṇa bhūttvā yoṣita su-komalam api hṛdayam tiraskurvanti
karañjabīja-eḍagajaṃ sa-kuṣṭhaṃ go-mūtra-piṣṭaṃ ca paraḥ pradehaḥ
dharma-na-viruddhaḥ bhūteṣu kāmaḥ asmi bharata-ṛṣabha
māhendra-salila-praśānta-santāpe jagati
pañca-dina-anantaram rājā bhramitum udyānam prati gatavān
tvarita-taraṃ vā yāsyasi sa-vi-śramaḥ vā
rājā phalasya na-āsvādita-pūrvaṃ mādhuryaṃ yadā bhūri prāśaṃsat
tenālīrāmaḥ mūrkha-rāja-padavīṃ jagrāha puro-hitena kṛṣṇadevena ca pūrvameva asau murkha-rāja-upādhinā vi-bhūṣitaḥ āsīt
ataḥ kartuḥ abhāvāt śāstra-na-ārthakyam iti cet
tataḥ praviśati dhanu-bāṇa-pāṇiḥ lakṣmaṇaḥ
jvalanam iha āśu vimukta-jīvita-āśā
mahārāṇāpratāpaḥ tasya aśvaṃ cetakam āruhya turuka-senā-adhipateḥ mānasiṃhasya purataḥ sthitaḥ
tadāapi gauḥānīyatāmiti vākye go-pada-arthasya go-padāt svarūpataḥ upasthitasya gotvasya viśeṣyatayā bhāna-na-upapattiḥ
hā vatsa abhimanyo īdṛśe api nāma puruṣa-kṣaya-kārake kula-vigrahe vartamāne bāla-bhāva-nimajjanam asmākam bhāgya-krameṇa kurvan kutra idānīm pautraka gataḥ asi
idam tu sarva-karma-saṃnyāsa-viṣayam prastutam
yathā vahni-niṣṭhāyāḥ dāha-janana-sāmarthya-ātmanka-śakteḥ dāha-janane svarūpataḥ upayogeapi pada-gatā bodha-janana-sāmarthya-ātmanikā śaktiḥ jñātāevaupayujyate
dhannā ca ahan-niśam svāmina prāṇa-rakṣā-artham prayatate sma
rajata-śilā-paṭṭikā-nirmitā kakṣa-bhittaya kutra vyalīyanta iti na jñātam kenapi patra-rupyaka noṭa iti bhāṣāyāmsaṃgrāhikābhi peṭikābhiḥ api riktatā-hetunā vijṛmbhaṇam iva ābhyasyate sma
te daśaratham dhanuṣ-bhaṅga-vārtām nivedya prārthitavantaḥ yat na-cirāt eva bhavatā vivāha-nimittam prasthānam karaṇīyam iti
gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti-ādau gaṅgā-śabda-artha-pravāha-dhī-bodhya-tīra-niṣṭhaḥ pravāha-pratiyogikaḥ saṃyoga-ādiḥ saṃbandhaḥ lakṣaṇā
guru-kula taḥ sva-rājyam prati āgamana-samaye yathā bhadravarmā na jānīyāt tathā guru-kulasya pradhāna-ācāryaḥ himakaram viśiṣṭām para-kāya-praveśa-vidyām bodhitavān
samāgatāni patrāṇi patra-vāhaka-hastāt ācchidya teṣu sūrpa-tuṣa-nyāyena nir-artha kāni patrāṇi apākṛtya keśavaprasādasya patram asau gaveṣayāmāsa
sā udatarat sanyāsi-mahat-rāja atra me pati-devaḥ ciraṃ nidrāti
sa-māṣa-vidalā vṛṣyā ghṛta-kṣīra-upasādhitā
tatratya-vicāra-paddhati-paryālocanāyām
tad-anantaraṃ rathasya dvārakā-praveśa-kāraṇena cakra-vyūhāt bahiḥ katham āgantavyam iti viṣayaḥ avaśiṣṭaḥ āsīt
bala-vīrya-rūpa-prajñā-medhā-dhana-utsāha-hāni-hetutvāt adharma-tat-janita-naraka-ādi-hetutvāt ca pariṇāme tad-upabhoga-pariṇāma-ante viṣam iva
sa-adhibhūta-adhidaivam mām sa-adhiyajñam ca ye viduḥ
svayam karnalaḥ tat-patnī ca sāyam sva-bhavana-śādbalasya lana paricaryām
tataḥ bhīmaḥ svasya mātuḥ sva-bhāva-ādi kam nivedya apṛcchat kim bhavatī sva-cāturyeṇa mama mātuḥ svabhāve parivartanam ānetum śaknuyāt iti
asmāt citra-paṭāt anantaraṃ tasya yaśas-mārgaḥ dine dine vistṛtaḥ eva jātaḥ pāthera pāṃcalī citra-paṭāya dvādaśa āntārāṣṭriyāṇi pāritoṣikāni tathā rāṣṭra-pati-suvarṇapadakam api prāptāni
brahma-buddhi-upamṛditatvāt
sthira-matiḥ sthirā parama-artha-viṣayā yasya matiḥ saḥ sthira-matiḥ
svāmini āgate sati maruvaṇāyamāne tat-jīvane sañjāyate akasmāt eva kācit na-kāla-jala-da-varṣā
tasmāt sa-khaṇḍam eva kriyā-janya-phala-śālin tvam karmatvam
buddhiḥ ātman-svarūpa-viṣayā na-yuktasya na-samāhita-antaḥkaraṇasya
tathā hi phala-parīkṣāyām agni-hotra-ādeḥ kāla-antara-bhāvi-svarga-phalaka tvam vyutpādya
tataḥ tatra na-upapatti-pratisandhānam
tasya satyatāyāḥ parīkṣāṃ vinā daṇḍa-pra-dānam na-ucitam
na-vaśa-indriya-cittānām hastin-snānam iva kriyā
asmat-cittā asmat-gata-prāṇā bodhayantaḥ parasparam
nirmalānanda brahmacārī parama-sukha-samṛddham samṛddham vilokitukāma grāmaṭikām prasthita maṭhikā-ākhyām
dhanus-śālā-rakṣakeṇa siṃhabalena vāryamāṇaḥ tam karṇa-mūle prahṛtya hatvā dhanuḥ samādāya dvi-khaṇḍam kṛtvā sāmpratam upasthāna-abhi-mukhaḥ gataḥ
māṃsa-jānāṃ tu saṃśuddhiḥ śastra-kṣāra-agni-karma ca
jala-bindu-prokṣaṇena prabodhayantī uvāca katham śrīkaṇṭha śrīkaṇṭhaḥ api mārga-ullaṃghana-śrama-upalabdhām nidrām pariharan
ata eva ahaṃ goā-pradeśasya purtagālīya-vyāpāriṇaḥ makhamala-pāda-trāṇe ānītavān asmi
tad-sevayā santuṣṭaḥ saḥ sva-jaṭā-rakṣitaṃ sparśa-maṇiṃ niḥsārya sad-gṛha-sthaṃ kathitavān asya sparśena lohaḥ suvarṇe parivartitaḥ bhavati
prakṛta-yāga-kriyā-viṣaya-kṛti-ādhāra tātvena anugata-rūpeṇa kṛtimattā-rūpa-kartṛtvasya vyāsajya-vṛtti-sambhavāt
tuṣāra-pūrṇa-utpala-patra-netrā harṣa-asram-āsāram ivautsṛjantī
evam vācakānām ghaṭa-ādi-śabdānām api pāribhāṣikatva-āpattiḥ
īśvara-saṃketasya śaktitva-mate gaṅgā-padasya tīre śaktiḥ siddhāeva gaṅgā-padāt tīra-bodha-udayena satmātra-viṣayaka-īśvara-icchāyāḥ tīre gaṅgā-pada-boddhavya-tva-avagāhi tvātiti vācyam
śvaḥ aham tvām tadbālāsamparkāpavitrībhūtam sa-prāyaścitta-vidhānam pavitrīkariṣyāmi
kālaḥ asmi loka-kṣaya-kṛt pravṛddhaḥ lokān samāhartum iha pravṛttaḥ
tat-artham api ca katham prabandha karttavya kevalam āya-vyaya-lekhanam antarā na kasmin api viṣaye yogyatā mama kārya-karaṇe
naapi pratyaya-pada-vācya tvam tat tatra īśvara-saṃkete māna-abhāvāt
tena krodha-āviṣṭaḥ yavana-rājasya sva-mātulaṃ śāyistekhānaṃ pañca-saptāti-lakṣa-sainyena saha
tasyāḥ prathamaḥ samayaḥ āsīt yat akṣara-saṃyojana-kāryam anyatra eva kārayitvā dātavyam iti
uktam ca vāram vāram yat etat sthālī-pātra-ādi kam madīyam eva vastu stenā ime apaharanti param phalam asya viparītam āsīt
tadā śvaśuraḥ bhāraviṃ sva-kāryaṃ sa-avadhāna-tā-pūrvakaṃ sampādayituṃ paruṣa-vācā kathitavān api
evam samasyā parihṛtā iti ataḥ rājā nitarām santuṣṭaḥ punaḥ kadācit bhū-svāmi-veṣeṇa gatvā vaṇijā dinapālena militvā saḥ avadat bhavataḥ upāyasya anusaraṇāt uttamam eva phalam prāptam
teṣāṃ abhiprāyaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti vicāreṇa dādāsāheba prati citra-paṭa-gṛhaṃ gatvā tatra āgatānāṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ nirīkṣaṇaṃ kṛtavān
saṃprāptāḥ kṣiti-patayaḥ sa-jīva-śeṣāḥ
mātṛ-pitṛ-sevām sodarī-hasta-bhojanam kṛtvā nagaram prati gatvā pattane tāni vastūni krītvā sāyaṃtane tat gṛhe gṛhiṇyai dāsyāmi
na sandhyāsu abhyavahāra-adhyayana-strī-svapna-sevī syāt
kṣamā-dayā-iti-ādīn śabdān aham na jānāmi
sā sundarī tatsadṛśam eva dvitīya-pāda-trāṇaṃ niḥsārya pradarśatavatī
aye kiṃ nu khalu mayi vi-jñāpana-vyagre śabdaḥ iva śrūyate
anubhava-janana-sāmarthyam eva śaktiḥ
saḥ pitaram avadat yat eṣaḥ vyavahāraḥ na-nyāyyaḥ pakṣa-pāta-upetaḥ ca iti
kāliyaḥbhagavan asmad-viṣa-dūṣitam idam jalam
gṛhīta-grāhin tvena smaraṇa-na-viśiṣṭa tvāt
rāmarudra-bhaṭṭācāryāḥ ca śābda-bodha-anuvyavasāyam śrṛṇomi itiabhilapanti
tat dṛṣṭvā tu hiraṇyakaśipuḥ mahat-rājaḥ atīva kopa-āviṣṭaḥ tadā tena punaḥ gaja-pāda-prahāraiḥ prahlādasya vadhaḥ ājñāpitaḥ
tataḥ te krameṇa vana-devatām upagamya sva-sva-putrāṇāṃ vaṃśa-rūpa-guṇa-ākṛtīnāṃ kathane pravṛttāḥ babhūvuḥ
sva-anu-rūpaṃ dhaninam udyama-patiṃ vā patiṃ prāptuṃ yogyā api sā ḍeborā svasmāt varṣebhyaḥ nyūna-vayaskaṃ kṣaya-roga-pīḍitaṃ durāgrahavantam api benyahūdaṃ svecchayā pariṇīya
atha vā pratyayānām saṃnihita-pada-artha-anvita-sva-artha-bodhaka-tva-vyutpattiḥ svīkriyate
eka-eka-pada-śravaṇa-anantaram-ananvita-tad-tad-artha-upasthitau satyām eka-smṛti-ārūḍhebhyaḥ padebhyaḥ ākāṃkṣita-yogya-sannihita-artha-antara-anvita-pratītiḥ jāyate iti na anyonya-āśrayaḥ
na ca ghaṭamānayaityatra vākya-bheda-āpattiḥ ghaṭa-padena na-anvita-ghaṭasya ānaya-padena ghaṭa-anvita-ānayanasya ca viśeṣya-viśeṣaṇa-bhāva-bheda-bhinnasya bodhātiti vācyam
pratyāvartane vilambam na-sahamānaḥ ṛṣiḥ svayameva samupasthitaḥ nir-jhariṇī-kūle
asmad-tattva-vedana-abhāvāt eva na mām bhajate
tat-kṛpayā eva sukharāmaḥ api prārambhika-pāṭha-śālāyām praviṣṭaḥ san pañcamīm kakṣām samuttīrṇa
bodhakatve na-ādi tvamca sva-prayojya-śābda-bodha-samāna-ākāra-pūrva-pūrva-bodha-dhvaṃsa-kāla īnatvam
iti vimṛśya na-pramattā tam uddeśam nibhṛtam prati-āgamana-udyatā sa-niśvāsa-nirodha kam rutam aśrauṣīt
kālidāsīyāyām kavitāyām mārgācalavyatikarākulitā eva sindhu śaila-adhirāja-tanayā na yayau na tasthau iti daśā smṛti-patham āruḍhā
kopa-jihmā-ānanaḥ saḥ saha-pāṭhī sva-bhāṣayā tam abhartsayat
snātasya yasya sam-upa-sthita-daivatasya puṇya-aha-ghoṣa-virame paṭahāḥ nadanti
sandhyā-anurañjita-vapuḥ pratibhāti sūryaḥ
pāñcāla-upadraveṇa śikṣaṇa-saṃsthānām avarodhād viśvavidyālaya grīṣmana-avakāśāt anantaram api na-niścita-kālam yāvat na-udghāṭita eva avartata
kiyat kāla-anantaram pāṭaliputrasya senā-aṅgaṇam vijaya-yātrā-ghoṣeṇa samāpūritam
śaradṛṣeḥ kathana-anusāram āvām atra āgatavantau svaḥ iti bhavatī vaikuṇṭha-īśvara-maharṣim vadatu
bhavataḥ nikaṭa-sthaḥ kaścit śani-doṣa-pīḍitaḥ vartate
parantu ghaṭa-ādi-viṣaya tāyāḥ eva
balidāne chinna-aṅga-vyakteḥ niṣedhatvāt te rājānaṃ muktavantaḥ
na ca śaitya-pāvanatva-ādau lakṣaṇāyām tad-nimittam asti
rātrau pralamba-taru-paṃkti-gāmina sarve api dūra-sthāḥ rājan-mārgā śūnyāḥ adṛśyanta
sup-artha-nirṇaya-avasāne
tathā ca naiyāyikaiḥ śābde pada-bhāna-aṅgīkārāt anyatra pratyakṣa-ādau taiṣām tad-na-bhāna-āgrahaḥ mudhāeva
sa-vyabhicāra-prakaraṇe
etādṛśa-pratibandhakatā-jñānasya anupayuktatvāt
yathā yathā paścima-kṣitija-upari prasṛtā kamalinī-nāyakasya anuraktā raśmaya gaganam paryatyajan tathā tathā kalā-paripūrṇasya kalā-nāthasya śītalā śubhrāḥ ca kāntimanta kiraṇā samaste api vihāyasi yathā iccham prāsaran
tathā bhavān saṃsāre sthitaḥ api karma-bandha-muktaḥ mādṛśāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ mānavāḥ kiṃ tathā bhavitum arhanti
vidyā-dāna-kāraṇāt bahūni phalāni api tasmin santi
sarva-indriya-guṇa-ābhāsam sarvāṇi ca tāni indriyāṇi śrotṛ-ādīni buddhi-indriya-karman-indriya-ākhyāni
madhya-ahna-paryantam mṛgayām kṛtvā nitarām śrāntaḥ saḥ sarovara-tīre sarvaiḥ saha upaviśya bhojanam akarot
naśa-dhātoḥ na-darśana-anukūla-vyāpāraḥ
parama-dukha-sammiśre asmin samaye narendra sa-vāṣpa svagatam avādīthanta mayā vicāritam āsīt
varṇayanti ca bhagavat-pādāḥ nirukta-śruteḥ tad-tad-vācaka-śabda-anusandhāna-pūrvaka-tad-tad-sṛṣṭi-para tvam devatā-adhikaraṇe
sutā pitaram provācapitā tasyāḥ āgraham nibhālya sutayā saha kūṣmāṇḍa-latā-samīpam prāpa kartanikayā tat phalam viccheda
viśvanātha-ārya-varyebhyaḥ ca hārdān na-ekān dhanya-vādān samarpayāmi
saṃskāra-samudāya-atiriktā vāsanā-āśraya-bhūtā daṇḍāyamānā avidyā naasti itievam
kvacit ākhyāta-artha-viśeṣyakaḥ ca śābda-bodhaḥ jāyate
saḥ tasya śṛṅgaṃ sa-nagaṃ sa-nāgaṃ sa-kāñcanaṃ dhātu-sahasra-juṣṭam
na aham prakāśaḥ sarvasya yoga-māyā-samāvṛtaḥ
punar-śabdaḥ pāda-pūraṇa-arthaḥ
bālām bhaya-ākula-vilola-viṣāda-netrām
kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāyāṇāṃ vipākaḥ prāyaśaḥ kaṭuḥ
yadi api ete na paśyanti lobha-upahata-cetasaḥ
bhūtika tvam api udyānam gaccha kuraṅgī-rakṣaṇa-artham
rājñā tasyai sva-hṛdaya-śukti-mauktika-mālā arpitā na idam sādhāraṇam kiñcit
darbhaṅgā-nṛpa-mānya-śrī-veṅkaṭrāma-tanū-bhavaḥ
vihāram samāpya prati-āgamana-samaye ubhau api sva-pituḥ nirṇayam śrāvitavān himakaraḥ
yadāpi sva-pārśva-upaviṣṭām tvām avalokayam
tyāga-saṃnyāsa-śabda-vācyaḥ hi yaḥ arthaḥ saḥ ekaḥ eva iti abhipretya āha tyāgaḥ hi iti
giraṃ manojñāṃ madhurā-artha-ramyāṃ
tādṛśa-śakti-nirūpikā ghaṭatva-karmatā-ādi-viṣayaka-śābda-dhīḥ
yat praśasyataram etayoḥ karman-anuṣṭhāna-karman-saṃnyāsayoḥ tat kartavyam
tasya nirṇayaḥ sva-artha-preritaḥ sarvathā na
tataḥasauāgatya maṇḍūka-nātha-sya sarpasya pṛṣṭamārūḍhavān
tatra tatra tri-loka-dhṛt
sarvān tathā bhūta-viśeṣa-saṅghān
anena moha-nāśa-praśna-prati-vacanena sarva-śāstra-artha-jñāna-phalam tāvat eva iti niścitam darśitam bhavati
sarvam śrutvā sannyāsī manda-hāsa-pūrvakam uktavān vatsa eka ekena eka ekam kartavyam nirvoḍhavyam bhavati loke
maraṇa-sīmā-karaṇam jīvataḥ avaśyaṃbhāvi hi kāma-krodha-udbhavaḥ vegaḥ
dāsyāmi saṃyuga-hatān sa-rathā-aśva-nāgān
sasya-pari-pūrite asmin udyāne puṣpāṇi vikasitāni āsan
ākāṃkṣā-sannidhi-prāpta-yogya-artha-antara-saṃgatān
snāna-ādi samāpya tīram āgataḥ keśavaḥ sarvatra śiva-liṅga-śataṃ pūjitaṃ dadarśa
imām nadīm grāha-bhuja-ga-saṅkulām
sajjalakaḥ atha kena idānīm sandhi-cheda-mārgaḥ sūcayitavyaḥ syāt
sādhyānāṃ trividhaḥca alpa-madhyama-utkṛṣṭatāṃ prati
mṛga-kartṛka-utkaṭa-dhāvane vā lakṣaṇā
kāla-upanāmaka-harirāma-mahodayāḥ sup-artha-nirṇaya-avasāne mūla-anuktāni vākyāniuddhṛtya
etat nirūpyam kim anena ātman-vit-kartṛkayoḥ saṃnyāsa-karman-yogayoḥ niḥśreyasakaratvam prayojanam uktvā
na-sat-mārgam āśrayāmi cet kaḥ māṃ loke bahumaṃsyati ityapi saḥ uktavān
tadā sā tān sva-gṛha-abhyanta
amarīkā-deśa-udbhavā cīna-deśe su-ciram uvāsa
asmad-kārmuka-udara-viniḥsṛta-bāṇa-jālaiḥ
dāsī-dāsa-ādayaḥ ca yāni khalu dhanika-gṛha-sthasya āvaśyakāni vastūni
chatrasālasya kūṭa-nītiṃ jñātvā idānīm avaraṅgajebena bahalolakhānaḥ nāma yuddha-nīti-kuśalaḥ niyuktaḥ
